::centre
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa
::

# Khuddakanikāye

## Jātakapāḷi

#### (Dutiyo bhāgo)

### 17. Cattālīsanipāto

#### 521. Tesakuṇajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vessantaraṃ {pb:T:1.0530}{pb:V:2.0001}{pb:M:2.0001} taṃ pucchāmi, sakuṇa bhaddamatthu te;
::

::gathalast
Rajjaṃ kāretukāmena, kiṃ su kiccaṃ kataṃ varaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cirassaṃ vata maṃ tāto, kaṃso bārāṇasiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Pamatto appamattaṃ maṃ, pitā puttaṃ acodayi.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭhameneva vitathaṃ, kodhaṃ hāsaṃ nivāraye;
::

::gathalast
Tato kiccāni kāreyya, taṃ vataṃ āhu khattiya.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:V:2.0002} tvaṃ tāta tapokammaṃ {note:tape kammaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, pubbe katamasaṃsayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ratto duṭṭho ca yaṃ kayirā, na taṃ kayirā tato puna {note:punaṃ (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khattiyassa pamattassa, raṭṭhasmiṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhana;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe bhogā vinassanti, rañño taṃ vuccate aghaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sirī tāta alakkhī ca {note:sirī ca tāta lakkhī ca (syā. pī.)}, pucchitā etadabravuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uṭṭhāna {note:uṭṭhāne (syā.)} vīriye pose, ramāhaṃ anusūyake.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Usūyake {pb:M:2.0002} duhadaye, purise kammadussake;
::

::gathalast
Kālakaṇṇī mahārāja, ramati {note:ramāti (ka.)} cakkabhañjanī.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So tvaṃ sabbesu suhadayo {note:so tvaṃ sabbesaṃ suhadayo (syā. pī.), so tvaṃ sabbe suhadayo (ka.)}, sabbesaṃ rakkhito bhava;
::

::gathalast
Alakkhiṃ nuda mahārāja, lakkhyā bhava nivesanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa {pb:T:1.0531} lakkhīdhitisampanno, puriso hi mahaggato;
::

::gathalast
Amittānaṃ kāsipati, mūlaṃ aggañca chindati.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakkopi hi bhūtapati, uṭṭhāne nappamajjati;
::

::gathalast
Sa kalyāṇe dhitiṃ katvā, uṭṭhāne kurute mano.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gandhabbā pitaro devā, sājīvā {note:sañjīvā (pī.)} honti tādino;
::

::gathalast
Uṭṭhāhato {note:uṭṭhahato (syā. pī.)} appamajjato {note:mappamajjato (ka.)}, anutiṭṭhanti devatā.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So appamatto akkuddho {note:akkuṭṭho (pī.)}, tāta kiccāni kāraya;
::

::gathalast
Vāyamassu ca kiccesu, nālaso vindate sukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattheva te vattapadā, esāva {note:esā ca (pī.)} anusāsanī;
::

::gathalast
Alaṃ mitte sukhāpetuṃ, amittānaṃ dukhāya {note:dukkhāya (pī.)} ca’’.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakkhisi tvaṃ {note:sakkhī tuvaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} kuṇḍalini, maññasi khattabandhuni {note:khattiyabandhunī (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Rajjaṃ kāretukāmena, kiṃ su kiccaṃ kataṃ varaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dveva tāta padakāni, yattha {note:yesu (pī.)} sabbaṃ patiṭṭhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aladdhassa ca yo lābho, laddhassa cānurakkhaṇā.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amacce tāta jānāhi, dhīre atthassa kovide;
::

::gathalast
Anakkhā kitave tāta, asoṇḍe avināsake.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo ca taṃ tāta rakkheyya, dhanaṃ yañceva te siyā;
::

::gathalast
Sūtova rathaṃ saṅgaṇhe, so te kiccāni kāraye.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Susaṅgahitantajano, sayaṃ vittaṃ avekkhiya;
::

::gathalast
Nidhiñca iṇadānañca, na kare parapattiyā.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sayaṃ {pb:V:2.0003}{pb:M:2.0003} āyaṃ {pb:T:1.0532} vayaṃ {note:āyavayaṃ (pī.)} jaññā, sayaṃ jaññā katākataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Niggaṇhe niggahārahaṃ, paggaṇhe paggahārahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sayaṃ jānapadaṃ atthaṃ, anusāsa rathesabha;
::

::gathalast
Mā te adhammikā yuttā, dhanaṃ raṭṭhañca nāsayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā ca vegena kiccāni, karosi {note:kāresi (sī. syā. pī.)} kārayesi vā;
::

::gathalast
Vegasā hi kataṃ kammaṃ, mando pacchānutappati.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā te adhisare muñca, subāḷhamadhikodhitaṃ {note:kopitaṃ (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Kodhasā hi bahū phītā, kulā akulataṃ gatā.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā tāta issaromhīti, anatthāya patārayi;
::

::gathalast
Itthīnaṃ purisānañca, mā te āsi dukhudrayo.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Apetalomahaṃsassa, rañño kāmānusārino;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe bhogā vinassanti, rañño taṃ vuccate aghaṃ.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattheva te vattapadā, esāva anusāsanī;
::

::gatha2
Dakkhassudāni puññakaro, asoṇḍo avināsako;
::

::gathalast
Sīlavāssu {note:sīlavāssa (ṭīkā)} mahārāja, dussīlo vinipātiko’’ {note:vinipātako (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Apucchimha kosiyagottaṃ {note:apucchimhā kosiyagottaṃ (syā.), apucchamhāpi kosikaṃ (pī.)}, kuṇḍaliniṃ tatheva ca;
::

::gathalast
Tvaṃ dāni vadehi jambuka {note:jambuka tvaṃ dāni vadehi (syā. pī.)}, balānaṃ balamuttamaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Balaṃ pañcavidhaṃ loke, purisasmiṃ mahaggate;
::

::gathalast
Tattha bāhubalaṃ nāma, carimaṃ vuccate balaṃ.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhogabalañca dīghāvu, dutiyaṃ vuccate balaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Amaccabalañca {pb:T:1.0533} dīghāvu, tatiyaṃ vuccate balaṃ.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhijaccabalaṃ ceva, taṃ catutthaṃ asaṃsayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yāni cetāni sabbāni, adhigaṇhāti paṇḍito.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ balānaṃ balaṃ seṭṭhaṃ, aggaṃ paññābaṃ balaṃ {note:varaṃ (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Paññābalenupatthaddho, atthaṃ vindati paṇḍito.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Api {pb:M:2.0004} ce labhati mando, phītaṃ dharaṇimuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Akāmassa pasayhaṃ vā, añño taṃ paṭipajjati.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhijātopi ce hoti, rajjaṃ laddhāna khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Duppañño hi kāsipati, sabbenapi na jīvati.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paññāva {pb:V:2.0004} sutaṃ vinicchinī {note:paññā sutavinicchinī (syā. pī.)}, paññā kitti silokavaḍḍhanī {note:vaddhanī (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Paññāsahito naro idha, api dukkhe sukhāni vindati.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paññañca kho asussūsaṃ, na koci adhigacchati;
::

::gathalast
Bahussutaṃ anāgamma, dhammaṭṭhaṃ avinibbhujaṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo ca dhammavibhaṅgaññū {note:yo dhammañca vibhāgaññū (pī.)}, kāluṭṭhāyī matandito;
::

::gathalast
Anuṭṭhahati kālena, kammaphalaṃ tassa ijjhati {note:kammaphalaṃ tassijjhati, phalaṃ tassa samijjhati (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anāyatana {note:nā’nāyatana (pī.)} sīlassa, anāyatana {note:nā’nāyatana (pī.)} sevino;
::

::gathalast
Na nibbindiyakārissa, sammadattho vipaccati.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhattañca payuttassa, tathāyatanasevino;
::

::gathalast
Anibbindiyakārissa, sammadattho vipaccati.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yogappayogasaṅkhātaṃ, sambhatassānurakkhaṇaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Tāni {pb:T:1.0534} tvaṃ tāta sevassu, mā akammāya randhayi;
::

::gathalast
Akammunā hi dummedho, naḷāgāraṃva sīdati’’.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja, mātāpitūsu khattiya;
::

::gathalast
Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna, rāja saggaṃ gamissasi.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja, puttadāresu khattiya;
::

::gathalast
Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna, rāja saggaṃ gamissasi.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja, mittāmaccesu khattiya;
::

::gathalast
Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna, rāja saggaṃ gamissasi.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja, vāhanesu balesu ca;
::

::gathalast
Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna, rāja saggaṃ gamissasi.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammaṃ {pb:M:2.0005} cara mahārāja, gāmesu nigamesu ca…pe….
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja, raṭṭhesu {note:raṭṭhe (pī.)} janapadesu ca…pe….
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja, samaṇa {note:samaṇe (syā. ka.)} brāhmaṇesu ca…pe….
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja, migapakkhīsu khattiya;
::

::gathalast
Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna, rāja saggaṃ gamissasi.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammaṃ {pb:T:1.0535} cara mahārāja, dhammo ciṇṇo sukhāvaho {note:dhammo suciṇṇo sukhamāvahati (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna, rāja saggaṃ gamissasi.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja, saindā {note:indo (pī.), sindā (ka.)} devā sabrahmakā;
::

::gathalast
Suciṇṇena divaṃ pattā, mā dhammaṃ rāja pāmado {note:pamādo (pī. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattheva {pb:V:2.0005} te {note:vete (pī.)} vattapadā, esāva {note:esā ca (pī.)} anusāsanī;
::

::gathalast
Sappaññasevī kalyāṇī, samattaṃ sāma {note:sāmaṃ (ka.)} taṃ vidū’’ti.
::

::centre
Tesakuṇajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 522. Sarabhaṅgajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Alaṅkatā kuṇḍalino suvatthā, veḷuriyamuttātharukhaggabandhā {note:baddhā (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Rathesabhā tiṭṭhatha ke nu tumhe, kathaṃ vo jānanti manussaloke’’.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahamaṭṭhako bhīmaratho panāyaṃ, kāliṅgarājā pana uggatoyaṃ {note:uggato ayaṃ (pī.), uggatāyaṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Susaññatānaṃ isīnaṃ {note:susaññatānisinaṃ (pī.)} dassanāya, idhāgatā pucchitāyemha pañhe’’.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vehāyasaṃ {pb:M:2.0006} tiṭṭhasi {note:tiṭṭhati (pī.)} antalikkhe, pathaddhuno pannaraseva cando;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ yakkha mahānubhāva, kathaṃ taṃ jānanti manussaloke’’.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yamāhu devesu sujampatīti, maghavāti {pb:T:1.0536} taṃ āhu manussaloke;
::

::gathalast
Sa devarājā idamajja patto, susaññatānaṃ isīnaṃ dassanāya’’.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dūre sutā no isayo samāgatā, mahiddhikā iddhiguṇūpapannā;
::

::gathalast
Vandāmi te ayire pasannacitto, ye jīvalokettha manussaseṭṭhā’’.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Gandho isīnaṃ ciradikkhitānaṃ {note:dakkhitānaṃ (syā. pī.)}, kāyā cuto gacchati mālutena;
::

::gathalast
Ito paṭikkamma sahassanetta, gandho isīnaṃ asuci devarāja’’.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gandho isīnaṃ ciradikkhitānaṃ, kāyā cuto gacchatu mālutena;
::

::gatha2
Vicitrapupphaṃ surabhiṃva mālaṃ, gandhañca etaṃ pāṭikaṅkhāma bhante;
::

::gathalast
Na hettha devā paṭikkūlasaññino’’.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Purindado bhūtapatī yasassī, devānamindo sakko {note:idaṃ padaṃ natthi (sī. syā. pī. potthakesu)} maghavā sujampati;
::

::gathalast
Sa devarājā asuragaṇappamaddano, okāsamākaṅkhati pañha pucchituṃ.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko {pb:T:1.0537} nevimesaṃ idha paṇḍitānaṃ, pañhe puṭṭho nipuṇe byākarissati;
::

::gathalast
Tiṇṇañca raññaṃ manujādhipānaṃ, devānamindassa ca vāsavassa’’.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayaṃ {pb:M:2.0007} isi {note:isī (sī. pī.)} sarabhaṅgo tapassī {note:yasassī (sī.)}, yato jāto virato methunasmā;
::

::gathalast
Āceraputto {note:ācariyaputto (pī. ka.)} suvinītarūpo, so nesaṃ pañhāni viyākarissati’’.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Koṇḍañña pañhāni viyākarohi, yācanti taṃ isayo sādhurūpā;
::

::gathalast
Koṇḍañña eso manujesu dhammo, yaṃ vuddha {note:vaddha (pī.), buddha (ka.)} māgacchati esa bhāro’’.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Katāvakāsā {pb:V:2.0006} pucchantu bhonto, yaṃ kiñci pañhaṃ manasābhipatthitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahañhi taṃ taṃ vo viyākarissaṃ, ñatvā sayaṃ lokamimaṃ parañca’’.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato ca maghavā sakko, atthadassī purindado;
::

::gathalast
Apucchi paṭhamaṃ pañhaṃ, yañcāsi abhipatthitaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ sū vadhitvā na kadāci socati, kissappahānaṃ isayo vaṇṇayanti;
::

::gathalast
Kassīdha {pb:T:1.0538} vuttaṃ pharusaṃ khametha, akkhāhi me koṇḍañña etamatthaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kodhaṃ vadhitvā na kadāci socati, makkhappahānaṃ isayo vaṇṇayanti;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesaṃ vuttaṃ pharusaṃ khametha, etaṃ khantiṃ uttamamāhu santo’’.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakkā ubhinnaṃ {note:hi dvinnaṃ (pī.)} vacanaṃ titikkhituṃ, sadisassa vā seṭṭhatarassa {note:seṭṭhanarassa (pī.)} vāpi;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ nu hīnassa vaco khametha, akkhāhi me koṇḍañña etamatthaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhayā {pb:M:2.0008} hi seṭṭhassa vaco khametha, sārambhahetū pana sādisassa;
::

::gathalast
Yo cīdha hīnassa vaco khametha, etaṃ khantiṃ uttamamāhu santo’’.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ vijaññā catupattharūpaṃ {note:catumaṭṭharūpaṃ (syā. pī.)}, seṭṭhaṃ sarikkhaṃ athavāpi hīnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Virūparūpena caranti santo, tasmā hi sabbesaṃ vaco khametha’’.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hetamatthaṃ mahatīpi senā, sarājikā yujjhamānā labhetha;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ {pb:T:1.0539} khantimā sappuriso labhetha, khantī balassūpasamanti verā’’.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Subhāsitaṃ te anumodiyāna, aññaṃ taṃ pucchāmi tadiṅgha brūhi;
::

::gatha2
Yathā ahuṃ {note:ahū (sī. syā. pī.)} daṇḍakī nāḷikero {note:nāḷikīro (sī. syā. pī.)}, athajjuno kalābu cāpi rājā;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ gatiṃ brūhi supāpakamminaṃ, katthūpapannā isinaṃ viheṭhakā’’.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kisañhi {note:kisaṃpi (pī.)} vacchaṃ avakiriya daṇḍakī, ucchinnamūlo sajano saraṭṭho;
::

::gathalast
Kukkuḷanāme nirayamhi paccati, tassa phuliṅgāni patanti kāye.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo saññate pabbajite aheṭhayi {note:avañcasi (pī.)}, dhammaṃ bhaṇante samaṇe adūsake;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ nāḷikeraṃ sunakhā parattha, saṅgamma khādanti viphandamānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athajjuno {pb:M:2.0009} niraye sattisūle, avaṃsiro patito uddhaṃpādo {note:uddhapādo (syā.), addhapādo (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Aṅgīrasaṃ gotamaṃ heṭhayitvā, khantiṃ tapassiṃ cirabrahmacāriṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:T:1.0540} khaṇḍaso pabbajitaṃ achedayi, khantiṃ vadantaṃ samaṇaṃ adūsakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kalābuvīciṃ upapajja paccati, mahāpatāpaṃ {note:mahābhitāpaṃ (pī.)} kaṭukaṃ bhayānakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etāni sutvā nirayāni paṇḍito, aññāni pāpiṭṭhatarāni cettha;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ care samaṇabrāhmaṇesu, evaṅkaro saggamupeti ṭhānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Subhāsitaṃ {pb:V:2.0007} te anumodiyāna, aññaṃ taṃ pucchāmi tadiṅgha brūhi;
::

::gatha2
Kathaṃvidhaṃ sīlavantaṃ vadanti, kathaṃvidhaṃ paññavantaṃ vadanti;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃvidhaṃ sappurisaṃ vadanti, kathaṃvidhaṃ no siri no jahāti’’.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāyena vācāya ca yo’dha {note:yo ca (pī.)} saññato, manasā ca kiñci na karoti pāpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na attahetū alikaṃ bhaṇeti {note:bhaṇāti (sī. syā. pī.)}, tathāvidhaṃ sīlavantaṃ vadanti.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gambhīrapañhaṃ manasābhicintayaṃ {note:manasā vicintayaṃ (sī.)}, nāccāhitaṃ kamma karoti luddaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kālāgataṃ {pb:T:1.0541} {note:kālābhataṃ (pī.)} atthapadaṃ na riñcati, tathāvidhaṃ paññavantaṃ vadanti.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:M:2.0010} ve kataññū katavedi dhīro, kalyāṇamitto daḷhabhatti ca hoti;
::

::gathalast
Dukhitassa sakkacca karoti kiccaṃ, tathāvidhaṃ sappurisaṃ vadanti.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etehi sabbehi guṇehupeto, saddho mudū saṃvibhāgī vadaññū;
::

::gathalast
Saṅgāhakaṃ sakhilaṃ saṇhavācaṃ, tathāvidhaṃ no siri no jahāti’’.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Subhāsitaṃ te anumodiyāna, aññaṃ taṃ pucchāmi tadiṅgha brūhi;
::

::gathalast
Sīlaṃ siriñcāpi satañca dhammaṃ, paññañca kaṃ seṭṭhataraṃ vadanti’’.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paññā hi seṭṭhā kusalā vadanti, nakkhattarājāriva tārakānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sīlaṃ sīrī cāpi satañca dhammo {note:dhammā (pī.)}, anvāyikā paññavato bhavanti’’.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Subhāsitaṃ te anumodiyāna, aññaṃ taṃ pucchāmi tadiṅgha brūhi;
::

::gatha2
Kathaṃkaro {pb:T:1.0542} kintikaro kimācaraṃ, kiṃ sevamāno labhatīdha paññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paññāya dānippaṭipaṃ {note:dāni paṭipadaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} vadehi, kathaṃkaro paññavā hoti macco’’.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sevetha vuddhe nipuṇe bahussute, uggāhako ca paripucchako siyā;
::

::gathalast
Suṇeyya sakkacca subhāsitāni, evaṃkaro paññavā hoti macco.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘{pb:M:2.0011} Paññavā kāmaguṇe avekkhati, aniccato dukkhato rogato ca;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ vipassī pajahāti chandaṃ, dukkhesu kāmesu mahabbhayesu.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa vītarāgo pavineyya dosaṃ, mettaṃ {note:metta (syā. ka.)} cittaṃ bhāvaye {note:bhāveyya (sī. syā. ka.)} appamāṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ, anindito brahmamupeti ṭhānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahatthiyaṃ {note:mahiddhiyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} āgamanaṃ ahosi, tavamaṭṭhakā {note:maṭṭhaka (sī. syā. ka.)} bhīmarathassa cāpi;
::

::gathalast
Kāliṅgarājassa ca uggatassa, sabbesa {pb:T:1.0543} vo kāmarāgo pahīno’’.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evametaṃ paracittavedi, sabbesa no kāmarāgo pahīno;
::

::gathalast
Karohi okāsamanuggahāya, yathā gatiṃ te abhisambhavema’’.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Karomi okāsamanuggahāya, tathā hi vo kāmarāgo pahīno;
::

::gathalast
Pharātha kāyaṃ vipulāya pītiyā, yathā gatiṃ me abhisambhavetha’’.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbaṃ {pb:V:2.0008} karissāma tavānusāsaniṃ, yaṃ yaṃ tuvaṃ vakkhasi bhūripañña;
::

::gathalast
Pharāma kāyaṃ vipulāya pītiyā, yathā gatiṃ te abhisambhavema’’.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Katāya {note:katāyaṃ (sī. pī.)} vacchassa kisassa pūjā, gacchantu bhonto isayo sādhurūpā;
::

::gathalast
Jhāne ratā hotha sadā samāhitā, esā ratī pabbajitassa seṭṭhā’’.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sutvāna {pb:M:2.0012} gāthā paramatthasaṃhitā, subhāsitā isinā paṇḍitena;
::

::gathalast
Te vedajātā anumodamānā, pakkāmu {pb:T:1.0544} {note:pakkamu (ka.)} devā devapuraṃ yasassino.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gāthā imā atthavatī subyañjanā, subhāsitā isinā paṇḍitena;
::

::gatha2
Yo kocimā aṭṭhikatvā {note:aṭṭhiṃ katvā (ka.)} suṇeyya, labhetha pubbāpariyaṃ visesaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Laddhāna pubbāpariyaṃ visesaṃ, adassanaṃ maccurājassa gacche’’.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sālissaro sāriputto, meṇḍissaro ca kassapo;
::

::gathalast
Pabbato anuruddho ca, kaccāyano ca devalo {note:devilo (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anusisso ca ānando, kisavaccho ca kolito;
::

::gatha2
Nārado udāyī thero {note:nārado puṇṇo mantānīputto (sī.)}, parisā buddhaparisā;
::

::gathalast
Sarabhaṅgo lokanātho, evaṃ dhāretha jātaka’’nti.
::

::centre
Sarabhaṅgajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 523. Alambusājātakaṃ (3)

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha bravi brahā indo, vatrabhū jayataṃ pitā;
::

::gathalast
Devakaññaṃ parābhetvā, sudhammāyaṃ alambusaṃ.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Misse devā taṃ yācanti, tāvatiṃsā saindakā;
::

::gathalast
Isippalobhane {pb:T:1.0545} {note:isipalobhike (sī. syā.), isiṃ palobhike (pī.)} gaccha, isisiṅgaṃ alambuse.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Purāyaṃ amhe acceti {note:nācceti (syā. ka.)}, vattavā {note:vatavā (sī. syā. pī.)} brahmacariyavā;
::

::gathalast
Nibbānābhirato vuddho {note:vaddho (pī.), buddho (syā. ka.)}, tassa maggāni āvara’’.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devarāja kimeva tvaṃ, mameva tuvaṃ sikkhasi;
::

::gathalast
Isippalobhane {note:isipalobhike (sī. syā.), isiṃ palobhike (pī.)} gaccha, santi aññāpi accharā.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mādisiyo {pb:M:2.0013} pavarā ceva, asoke nandane vane;
::

::gathalast
Tāsampi hotu pariyāyo, tāpi yantu palobhanā’’ {note:palobhikā (syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā {pb:V:2.0009} hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, santi aññāpi accharā;
::

::gathalast
Tādisiyo pavarā ceva, asoke nandane vane.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na tā evaṃ pajānanti, pāricariyaṃ pumaṃ gatā;
::

::gathalast
Yādisaṃ tvaṃ pajānāsi, nāri sabbaṅgasobhane.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tvameva gaccha kalyāṇi, itthīnaṃ pavarā casi;
::

::gathalast
Taveva vaṇṇarūpena, savasamānayissasi’’ {note:vasamānāpayissasi (syā.), vasamānāmayissasi (pī.), taṃ vasamānayissasi (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na vāhaṃ na gamissāmi, devarājena pesitā;
::

::gathalast
Vibhemi cetaṃ āsāduṃ, uggatejo hi brāhmaṇo.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aneke nirayaṃ pattā, isimāsādiyā janā;
::

::gathalast
Āpannā mohasaṃsāraṃ, tasmā lomāni haṃsaye’’.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna pakkāmi, accharā kāmavaṇṇinī;
::

::gathalast
Missā missitu {note:missetu (sī. syā. pī.)} micchantī, isisiṅgaṃ alambusā.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sā ca taṃ vanamogayha, isisiṅgena rakkhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bimbajālakasañchannaṃ{pb:T:1.0546}, samantā aḍḍhayojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pātova pātarāsamhi, udaṇhasamayaṃ {note:udayasamayaṃ (syā.), udantasamayaṃ (ka.)} pati;
::

::gathalast
Aggiṭṭhaṃ parimajjantaṃ, isisiṅgaṃ upāgami’’.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kā nu vijjurivābhāsi, osadhī viya tārakā;
::

::gathalast
Vicittahatthābharaṇā {note:vicittavatthābharaṇā (sī.)}, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā {note:āmukkamaṇikuṇḍalā (?)}.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ādiccavaṇṇasaṅkāsā, hemacandanagandhinī;
::

::gathalast
Saññatūrū mahāmāyā, kumārī cārudassanā.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vilaggā {note:vilākā (sī. syā. pī.)} mudukā suddhā, pādā te suppatiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Gamanā kāmanīyā {note:kamanā kamanīyā (sī. pī.)} te, harantiyeva me mano.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anupubbāva {pb:M:2.0014} te ūrū, nāganāsasamūpamā;
::

::gathalast
Vimaṭṭhā tuyhaṃ sussoṇī, akkhassa phalakaṃ yathā.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uppalasseva kiñjakkhā, nābhi te sādhu saṇṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Pūrā kaṇhañjanasseva, dūrato paṭidissati.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duvidhā jātā urajā, avaṇṭā sādhu paccudā;
::

::gathalast
Payodharā apatitā {note:appatītā (sī. syā. pī.)}, aḍḍhalābusamā thanā.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dīghā kambutalābhāsā, gīvā eṇeyyakā yathā;
::

::gathalast
Paṇḍarāvaraṇā vaggu, catutthamanasannibhā.
::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uddhaggā {pb:V:2.0010} ca adhaggā ca, dumaggaparimajjitā;
::

::gathalast
Duvijā nelasambhūtā, dantā tava sudassanā.
::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Apaṇḍarā lohitantā, jiñjūka {note:jiñjuka (sī. syā. pī.)} phalasannibhā;
::

::gathalast
Āyatā {pb:T:1.0547} ca visālā ca, nettā tava sudassanā.
::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nātidīghā susammaṭṭhā, kanakabyā {note:kanakaggā (pī.)} samocitā;
::

::gathalast
Uttamaṅgaruhā tuyhaṃ, kesā candanagandhikā.
::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāvatā kasigorakkhā, vāṇijānaṃ {note:vaṇijānaṃ (pī.)} ca yā gati;
::

::gathalast
Isīnañca parakkantaṃ, saññatānaṃ tapassinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na te samasamaṃ passe, asmiṃ pathavi {note:puthuvi (pī.)} maṇḍale;
::

::gathalast
Ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na pañhakālo bhaddante, kassapevaṃ gate sati;
::

::gatha2
Ehi samma ramissāma, ubho asmākamassame;
::

::gathalast
Ehi taṃ upagūhissaṃ {note:upaguyhissaṃ (syā.)}, ratīnaṃ kusalo bhava’’.
::

::hangnum
121\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna pakkāmi, accharā kāmavaṇṇinī;
::

::gathalast
Missā missitumicchantī, isisiṅgaṃ alambusā’’.
::

::hangnum
122\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So ca vegena nikkhamma, chetvā dandhaparakkamaṃ {note:dandhapadakkamaṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Tamuttamāsu veṇīsu, ajjhappatto {note:ajjhāpatto (pī.)} parāmasi;
::

::hangnum
123\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamudāvatta {pb:M:2.0015} kalyāṇī, palissaji susobhanā {note:susobhaṇī (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Cavitamhi {note:cavi tamhā (syā. ka.)} brahmacariyā, yathā taṃ atha tositā.
::

::hangnum
124\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Manasā agamā indaṃ, vasantaṃ nandane vane;
::

::gathalast
Tassā saṅkappamaññāya, maghavā devakuñjaro.
::

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pallaṅkaṃ pahiṇī khippaṃ, sovaṇṇaṃ sopavāhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sauttaracchadapaññāsaṃ, sahassapaṭiyatthataṃ {note:paṭikatthataṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
126\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamenaṃ {pb:T:1.0548} tattha dhāresi, ure katvāna sobhanā;
::

::gathalast
Yathā ekamuhuttaṃva, tīṇi vassāni dhārayi.
::

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vimado tīhi vassehi, pabujjhitvāna brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Addasāsi harita {note:harī (pī.)} rukkhe, samantā aggiyāyanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Navapattavanaṃ phullaṃ, kokilaggaṇaghositaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samantā paviloketvā, rudaṃ assūni vattayi.
::

::hangnum
129\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:2.0011} juhe na jape {note:jappe (ka.)} mante, aggihuttaṃ pahāpitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ko nu me pāricariyāya, pubbe cittaṃ palobhayi.
::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Araññe me viharato, yo me tejā ha sambhutaṃ {note:sambhataṃ (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Nānāratnaparipūraṃ, nāvaṃva gaṇhi aṇṇave’’.
::

::hangnum
131\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ te pāricariyāya, devarājena pesitā;
::

::gathalast
Avadhiṃ {note:avadhī (syā. pī. ka.)} cittaṃ cittena, pamādo {note:pamādā (syā. pī.)} tvaṃ na bujjhasi’’.
::

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imāni kira maṃ tāto, kassapo anusāsati;
::

::gathalast
Kamalāsadisitthiyo {note:sarisitthiyo (syā. pī.)}, tāyo bujjhesi māṇava.
::

::hangnum
133\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ure gaṇḍāyo bujjhesi, tāyo bujjhesi māṇava;
::

::gathalast
Iccānusāsi maṃ tāto, yathā maṃ anukampako.
::

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassāhaṃ vacanaṃ nākaṃ, pitu vuddhassa sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Araññe nimmanussamhi, svajja jhāyāmi {note:svājjajjhāyāmi (sī. pī.)} ekako.
::

::hangnum
135\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sohaṃ {pb:M:2.0016} tathā karissāmi, dhiratthu jīvitena me;
::

::gathalast
Puna vā tādiso hessaṃ, maraṇaṃ me bhavissati’’.
::

::hangnum
136\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa {pb:T:1.0549} tejaṃ {note:tejañca (sī. pī.)} vīriyañca, dhitiṃ {note:dhitiñca (pī.)} ñatvā avaṭṭhitaṃ {note:suvaḍḍhitaṃ (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sirasā aggahī pāde, isisiṅgaṃ alambusā.
::

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā me kujjha {note:kujjhi (pī.)} mahāvīra, mā me kujjha {note:kujjhi (pī.)} mahāise;
::

::gatha2
Mahā attho mayā ciṇṇo, tidasānaṃ yasassinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tayā saṃkampitaṃ āsi, sabbaṃ devapuraṃ tadā’’.
::

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāvatiṃsā ca ye devā, tidasānañca vāsavo;
::

::gathalast
Tvañca bhadde sukhī hohi, gaccha kaññe yathāsukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa pāde gahetvāna, katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, tamhā ṭhānā apakkami.
::

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo ca tassāsi pallaṅko, sovaṇṇo sopavāhano;
::

::gatha2
Sauttaracchadapaññāso, sahassapaṭiyatthato;
::

::gathalast
Tameva pallaṅkamāruyha, agā devāna santike.
::

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamokkamiva āyantiṃ, jalantiṃ vijjutaṃ yathā;
::

::gathalast
Patīto sumano vitto, devindo adadā varaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
142\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Varañce {pb:V:2.0012} me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gathalast
Nisippalobhikā {note:na isipalobhikā (syā.), na isipalobhiyaṃ (pī.)} gacche, etaṃ sakka varaṃ vare’’ti.
::

::centre
Alambusājātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 524. Saṅkhapālajātakaṃ (4)

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ariyāvakāsosi pasannanetto, maññe {pb:T:1.0550} bhavaṃ pabbajito kulamhā;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ nu vittāni pahāya bhoge, pabbaji nikkhamma gharā sapañña’’ {note:sapañño (syā.), sapaññā (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
144\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sayaṃ {pb:M:2.0017} vimānaṃ naradeva disvā, mahānubhāvassa mahoragassa;
::

::gathalast
Disvāna puññāna mahāvipākaṃ, saddhāyahaṃ pabbajitomhi rāja’’.
::

::hangnum
145\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na kāmakāmā na bhayā na dosā, vācaṃ musā pabbajitā bhaṇanti;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ, sutvāna me jāyihitippasādo’’.
::

::hangnum
146\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vāṇijja {note:vaṇijja (pī.)} raṭṭhādhipa gacchamāno, pathe addasāsimhi bhojaputte {note:milācaputte (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Pavaddhakāyaṃ uragaṃ mahantaṃ, ādāya gacchante pamodamāne’’.
::

::hangnum
147\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sohaṃ samāgamma janinda tehi, pahaṭṭhalomo avacamhi bhīto;
::

::gathalast
Kuhiṃ ayaṃ nīyati {note:niyyati (ka.)} bhīmakāyo, nāgena kiṃ kāhatha bhojaputtā.
::

::hangnum
148\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāgo ayaṃ nīyati bhojanatthā {note:bhojanatthaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, pavaddhakāyo {pb:T:1.0551} urago mahanto;
::

::gathalast
Sāduñca thūlañca muduñca maṃsaṃ, na tvaṃ rasaññāsi videhaputta.
::

::hangnum
149\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito mayaṃ gantvā sakaṃ niketaṃ {note:niketanaṃ (pī.)}, ādāya satthāni vikopayitvā;
::

::gathalast
Maṃsāni bhokkhāma {note:bhakkhāma (syā.)} pamodamānā, mayañhi ve sattavo pannagānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
150\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace ayaṃ nīyati bhojanatthā, pavaddhakāyo urago mahanto;
::

::gathalast
Dadāmi vo balibaddāni {note:balivaddāni (pī.)} soḷasa, nāgaṃ imaṃ muñcatha bandhanasmā.
::

::hangnum
151\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā {pb:M:2.0018} hi no bhakkho ayaṃ manāpo, bahū ca no uragā bhuttapubbā {note:bahuṃ ca no urago bhuttapubbo (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Karoma te taṃ vacanaṃ aḷāra {note:āḷāra (ka.) evamuparipi}, mittañca no hohi videhaputta.
::

::hangnum
152\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadassu te bandhanā mocayiṃsu, yaṃ natthuto paṭimokkassa pāse;
::

::gathalast
Mutto ca so bandhanā nāgarājā, pakkāmi pācīnamukho muhuttaṃ.
::

::hangnum
153\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gantvāna pācīnamukho muhuttaṃ, puṇṇehi {pb:T:1.0552} nettehi palokayī maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tadāssahaṃ piṭṭhito anvagacchiṃ, dasaṅguliṃ añjaliṃ paggahetvā.
::

::hangnum
154\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gaccheva {pb:V:2.0013} kho tvaṃ taramānarūpo, mā taṃ amittā punaraggahesuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dukkho hi luddehi punā samāgamo, adassanaṃ bhojaputtāna gaccha.
::

::hangnum
155\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Agamāsi so rahadaṃ vippasannaṃ, nīlobhāsaṃ ramaṇīyaṃ sutitthaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samotataṃ {note:samonataṃ (syā. ka.)} jambuhi vetasāhi, pāvekkhi nittiṇṇabhayo patīto.
::

::hangnum
156\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So taṃ pavissa na cirassa nāgo, dibbena me pāturahuṃ janinda;
::

::gathalast
Upaṭṭhahī maṃ pitaraṃva putto, hadayaṅgamaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ bhaṇanto.
::

::hangnum
157\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tvaṃ {pb:M:2.0019} mesi mātā ca pitā {note:pitā ca (pī.)} aḷāra, abbhantaro pāṇadado sahāyo;
::

::gatha2
Sakañca iddhiṃ paṭilābhakosmi {note:paṭilābhitosmi (pī.)}, aḷāra passa me nivesanāni;
::

::gathalast
Pahūtabhakkhaṃ bahuannapānaṃ, masakkasāraṃ {pb:T:1.0553} viya vāsavassa’’.
::

::hangnum
158\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ bhūmibhāgehi upetarūpaṃ, asakkharā ceva mudū subhā ca;
::

::gathalast
Nīcattiṇā {note:nīcā tiṇā (syā. pī.)} apparajā ca bhūmi, pāsādikā yattha jahanti sokaṃ.
::

::hangnum
159\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anāvakulā veḷuriyūpanīlā, catuddisaṃ ambavanaṃ surammaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pakkā ca pesī ca phalā suphullā, niccotukā dhārayantī phalāni.
::

::hangnum
160\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesaṃ vanānaṃ naradeva majjhe, nivesanaṃ bhassarasannikāsaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rajataggaḷaṃ sovaṇṇamayaṃ uḷāraṃ, obhāsatī vijjurivantalikkhe.
::

::hangnum
161\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maṇīmayā soṇṇamayā {note:sovaṇṇamayā (sī. syā. pī.)} uḷārā, anekacittā satataṃ sunimmitā;
::

::gathalast
Paripūrā kaññāhi alaṅkatābhi, suvaṇṇakāyūradharāhi rāja.
::

::hangnum
162\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So saṅkhapālo taramānarūpo, pāsādamāruyha anomavaṇṇo;
::

::gathalast
Sahassathambhaṃ atulānubhāvaṃ, yatthassa {pb:T:1.0554} bhariyā mahesī ahosi.
::

::hangnum
163\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekā {pb:M:2.0020} ca nārī taramānarūpā, ādāya veḷuriyamayaṃ mahagghaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Subhaṃ maṇiṃ jātimantūpapannaṃ, acoditā āsanamabbhihāsi.
::

::hangnum
164\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato maṃ urago hatthe gahetvā, nisīdayī pāmukhaāsanasmiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idamāsanaṃ atra bhavaṃ nisīdatu, bhavañhi me aññataro garūnaṃ.
::

::hangnum
165\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññā ca nārī taramānarūpā, ādāya vāriṃ upasaṅkamitvā;
::

::gathalast
Pādāni pakkhālayī me janinda, bhariyāva {note:bhariyā ca (pī.)} bhattū patino piyassa.
::

::hangnum
166\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aparā ca nārī taramānarūpā, paggayha sovaṇṇamayāya {note:sovaṇṇamayā (pī.)} pātiyā;
::

::gathalast
Anekasūpaṃ vividhaṃ viyañjanaṃ, upanāmayī bhatta manuññarūpaṃ.
::

::hangnum
167\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Turiyehi {note:tūriyehi (ka.)} maṃ bhārata bhuttavantaṃ, upaṭṭhahuṃ bhattu mano viditvā;
::

::gathalast
Tatuttariṃ {note:taduttariṃ (ka.)} maṃ nipatī mahantaṃ, dibbehi {pb:T:1.0555} kāmehi anappakehi.
::

::hangnum
168\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhariyā {pb:V:2.0014} mametā tisatā aḷāra, sabbattamajjhā padumuttarābhā;
::

::gathalast
Aḷāra etāssu te kāmakārā, dadāmi te tā paricārayassu.
::

::hangnum
169\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṃvaccharaṃ dibbarasānubhutvā, tadāssuhaṃ {note:tadassahaṃ (pī.)} uttarimajjhabhāsiṃ {note:uttari paccabhāsiṃ (sī. syā.), uttariṃ paccabhāsiṃ (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Nāgassidaṃ kinti kathañca laddhaṃ, kathajjhagamāsi vimānaseṭṭhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
170\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhicca {pb:M:2.0021} laddhaṃ pariṇāmajaṃ te, sayaṃkataṃ udāhu devehi dinnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ {note:te (pī.)} nāgarājetamatthaṃ, kathajjhagamāsi vimānaseṭṭhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
171\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nādhicca laddhaṃ na pariṇāmajaṃ me, na sayaṃkataṃ nāpi devehi dinnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakehi kammehi apāpakehi, puññehi me laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
172\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ te vataṃ kiṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ, kissa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi me nāgarājetamatthaṃ, kathaṃ {pb:T:1.0556} nu te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
173\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājā ahosiṃ magadhānamissaro, duyyodhano nāma mahānubhāvo;
::

::gathalast
So ittaraṃ jīvitaṃ saṃviditvā, asassataṃ vipariṇāmadhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
174\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Annañca pānañca pasannacitto, sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adāsiṃ {note:adāsi (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Opānabhūtaṃ me gharaṃ tadāsi, santappitā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca.
::

::hangnum
175\.
::

::gatha1
{note:ayaṃ gāthā pī. potthake natthi} ‘‘Mālañca gandhañca vilepanañca, padīpiyaṃ {note:padīpayaṃ (syā. ka.)} yānamupassayañca;
::

::gathalast
Acchādanaṃ seyyamathannapānaṃ, sakkacca dānāni adamha tattha {note:ayaṃ gāthā pī. potthake natthi}.
::

::hangnum
176\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:M:2.0022} me vataṃ taṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ, tassa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko;
::

::gatha2
Teneva me laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ, pahūtabhakkhaṃ bahuannapānaṃ’’;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Naccehi gītehi cupetarūpaṃ, ciraṭṭhitikaṃ na ca sassatāyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
177\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appānubhāvā taṃ mahānubhāvaṃ, tejassinaṃ {pb:T:1.0557} hanti atejavanto;
::

::gathalast
Kimeva dāṭhāvudha kiṃ paṭicca, hatthatta {note:hatthattha (sī. syā. pī.)} māgacchi vanibbakānaṃ {note:vaṇibbakānaṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
178\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhayaṃ nu te anvagataṃ mahantaṃ, tejo nu te nānvagaṃ dantamūlaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kimeva dāṭhāvudha kiṃ paṭicca, kilesamāpajji vanibbakānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
179\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na me bhayaṃ anvagataṃ mahantaṃ, tejo na sakkā mama tehi hantuṃ {note:tebhihantuṃ (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Satañca dhammāni sukittitāni, samuddavelāva duraccayāni.
::

::hangnum
180\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ aḷāra, uposathaṃ niccamupāvasāmi;
::

::gathalast
Athāgamuṃ soḷasa bhojaputtā, rajjuṃ gahetvāna daḷhañca pāsaṃ.
::

::hangnum
181\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhetvāna nāsaṃ atikassa {note:antakassa (ka.)} rajjuṃ, nayiṃsu maṃ samparigayha luddā;
::

::gathalast
Etādisaṃ dukkhamahaṃ titikkhaṃ {note:titikkhiṃ (pī.)}, uposathaṃ appaṭikopayanto’’.
::

::hangnum
182\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekāyane {pb:V:2.0015}{pb:M:2.0023} taṃ pathe addasaṃsu, balena {pb:T:1.0558} vaṇṇena cupetarūpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Siriyā paññāya ca bhāvitosi, kiṃ patthayaṃ {note:kimatthiyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} nāga tapo karosi.
::

::hangnum
183\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na puttahetū na dhanassa hetu, na āyuno cāpi aḷāra hetu;
::

::gathalast
Manussayoniṃ abhipatthayāno, tasmā parakkamma tapo karomi’’.
::

::hangnum
184\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tvaṃ lohitakkho vihatantaraṃso, alaṅkato kappitakesamassu;
::

::gathalast
Surosito lohitacandanena, gandhabbarājāva disā pabhāsasi {note:pabhāsi (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
185\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, sabbehi kāmehi samaṅgibhūto;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ nāgarājetamatthaṃ, seyyo ito kena manussaloko’’.
::

::hangnum
186\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aḷāra nāññatra manussalokā, suddhī va saṃvijjati saṃyamo vā;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca laddhāna manussayoniṃ, kāhāmi jātimaraṇassa antaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
187\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṃvaccharo {pb:T:1.0559} me vasato {note:vusito (pī.)} tavantike, annena pānena upaṭṭhitosmi;
::

::gathalast
Āmantayitvāna palemi nāga, cirappavuṭṭhosmi {note:cirappavuttho asmi (pī.)} ahaṃ janinda’’.
::

::hangnum
188\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puttā ca dārā anujīvino ca {note:ca’nujīvino (syā. pī.)}, niccānusiṭṭhā upatiṭṭhate taṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kaccinnu taṃ nābhisapittha {note:nābhisaṃsittha (syā. pī.)} koci, piyañhi me dassanaṃ tuyhaṃ {note:tuyha (pī.)} aḷāra’’.
::

::hangnum
189\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāpi {pb:M:2.0024} mātū ca pitū agāre, putto piyo paṭivihito vaseyya {note:seyyo (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tatopi mayhaṃ idhameva seyyo, cittañhi te nāga mayī pasannaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
190\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maṇī mamaṃ vijjati lohitaṅko {note:lohitaṅgo (ka.)}, dhanāharo maṇiratanaṃ uḷāraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ādāya tvaṃ {note:taṃ (pī.)} gaccha sakaṃ niketaṃ, laddhā dhanaṃ taṃ maṇimossajassu’’.
::

::hangnum
191\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Diṭṭhā mayā mānusakāpi kāmā, asassatā vipariṇāmadhammā;
::

::gathalast
Ādīnavaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā, saddhāyahaṃ pabbajitomhi rāja.
::

::hangnum
192\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dumapphalānīva {pb:T:1.0560} patanti māṇavā, daharā ca vuddhā ca sarīrabhedā;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvā pabbajitomhi rāja, apaṇṇakaṃ sāmaññameva seyyo’’.
::

::hangnum
193\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā have sevitabbā sapaññā, bahussutā ye bahuṭhānacintino;
::

::gathalast
Nāgañca sutvāna tavañcaḷāra, kāhāmi puññāni anappakāni’’.
::

::hangnum
194\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā have sevitabbā sapaññā, bahussutā ye bahuṭhānacintino;
::

::gathalast
Nāgañca sutvāna mamañca rāja, karohi puññāni anappakānī’’ti.

::centre
Saṅkhapālajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 525. Cūḷasutasomajātakaṃ (5)

::hangnum
195\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āmantayāmi {pb:V:2.0016}{pb:M:2.0025} nigamaṃ, mittāmacce parissaje {note:pārisajje (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Sirasmiṃ palitaṃ jātaṃ, pabbajjaṃ dāni rocahaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
196\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhumme kathaṃ nu bhaṇasi, sallaṃ me deva urasi kappesi {note:kampesi (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sattasatā te bhariyā, kathaṃ {pb:T:1.0561} nu te tā bhavissanti’’.
::

::hangnum
197\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paññāyihinti etā, daharā aññampi tā gamissanti;
::

::gathalast
Saggañcassa patthayāno, tena ahaṃ pabbajissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
198\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dulladdhaṃ me āsi sutasoma, yassa te homahaṃ mātā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ me vilapantiyā, anapekkho pabbajasi deva.
::

::hangnum
199\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dulladdhaṃ me āsi sutasoma, yaṃ taṃ ahaṃ vijāyissaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ me vilapantiyā, anapekkho pabbajasi deva’’.
::

::hangnum
200\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko nāmeso dhammo, sutasoma kā ca nāma pabbajjā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ no amhe jiṇṇe, anapekkho pabbajasi deva.
::

::hangnum
201\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puttāpi tuyhaṃ bahavo, daharā appattayobbanā;
::

::gathalast
Mañjū tepi {note:te (sī. pī.)} taṃ apassantā, maññe {pb:T:1.0562} dukkhaṃ nigacchanti’’.
::

::hangnum
202\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puttehi ca me etehi, daharehi appattayobbanehi;
::

::gathalast
Mañjūhi sabbehipi tumhehi, cirampi ṭhatvā vināsabhāvo’’ {note:vinābhāvo (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
203\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chinnaṃ {pb:M:2.0026} nu tuyhaṃ hadayaṃ, adu te {note:ādu (sī. pī.), ādū (syā.)} karuṇā ca natthi amhesu;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ no vikandantiyo {note:vikkandantiyo (sī.)}, anapekkho pabbajasi deva’’.
::

::hangnum
204\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na ca mayhaṃ chinnaṃ hadayaṃ, atthi karuṇāpi mayhaṃ tumhesu;
::

::gathalast
Saggañca patthayāno, tena ahaṃ {note:tenāhaṃ (sī. syā.), tenamahaṃ (pī.)} pabbajissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
205\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dulladdhaṃ me āsi, sutasoma yassa te ahaṃ bhariyā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ me vilapantiyā, anapekkho pabbajasi deva.
::

::hangnum
206\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dulladdhaṃ me āsi, sutasoma yassa te ahaṃ bhariyā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ me kucchipaṭisandhiṃ {note:maṃ kucchimatiṃ santiṃ (pī.)}, anapekkho {pb:T:1.0563} pabbajasi deva.
::

::hangnum
207\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paripakko me gabbho, kucchigato yāva naṃ vijāyāmi;
::

::gathalast
Māhaṃ ekā vidhavā, pacchā dukkhāni addakkhiṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
208\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paripakko te gabbho, kucchigato iṅgha tvaṃ {note:tva (sī.), naṃ (pī.)} vijāyassu;
::

::gathalast
Puttaṃ anomavaṇṇaṃ, taṃ hitvā pabbajissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
209\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā {pb:V:2.0017} tvaṃ cande rudi, mā soci vanatimiramattakkhi;
::

::gathalast
Āroha varapāsādaṃ {note:ca pāsādaṃ (pī.)}, anapekkho ahaṃ gamissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
210\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko {pb:M:2.0027} taṃ amma kopesi, kiṃ rodasi pekkhasi ca maṃ bāḷhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kaṃ avajjhaṃ ghātemi {note:ghātemi kaṃ avajjhaṃ (pī.), taṃ avajjhaṃ ghātemi (ka.)}, ñātīnaṃ udikkhamānānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
211\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi so sakkā hantuṃ, vijitāvī {note:jīvitāvī (pī.)} yo maṃ tāta kopesi;
::

::gathalast
Pitā te maṃ tāta avaca, anapekkho {pb:T:1.0564} ahaṃ gamissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
212\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yohaṃ pubbe niyyāmi, uyyānaṃ mattakuñjare ca yodhemi;
::

::gathalast
Sutasome pabbajite, kathaṃ nu dāni karissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
213\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mātucca {note:mātu ca (sī. syā.)} me rudantyā {note:rudatyā (pī.)}, jeṭṭhassa ca bhātuno akāmassa;
::

::gathalast
Hatthepi te gahessaṃ, na hi gacchasi {note:gañchisi (pī.)} no akāmānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
214\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uṭṭhehi tvaṃ dhāti, imaṃ kumāraṃ ramehi aññattha;
::

::gathalast
Mā me paripanthamakāsi {note:makā (sī. pī.)}, saggaṃ mama patthayānassa’’.
::

::hangnum
215\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ nūnimaṃ dadeyyaṃ {note:jaheyyaṃ (pī.)} pabhaṅkaraṃ, ko nu me imināttho {note:ko nu me iminā attho (sī. syā.), ko nu me nattho (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sutasome pabbajite, kiṃ nu menaṃ karissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
216\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Koso {pb:M:2.0028} ca tuyhaṃ vipulo, koṭṭhāgārañca tuyhaṃ paripūraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pathavī ca tuyhaṃ vijitā, ramassu {pb:T:1.0565} mā pabbaji {note:pabbajassu (sī.), pabbaja (pī.)} deva’’.
::

::hangnum
217\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Koso ca mayhaṃ vipulo, koṭṭhāgārañca mayhaṃ paripūraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pathavī ca mayhaṃ vijitā, taṃ hitvā pabbajissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
218\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mayhampi dhanaṃ pahūtaṃ, saṅkhātuṃ {note:saṅkhyātuṃ (sī.)} nopi deva sakkomi;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ te dadāmi sabbampi {note:taṃ deva te dadāmi sabbampi (sī.), taṃ te dadāmi sabbaṃ (pī.)}, ramassu mā pabbaji deva’’.
::

::hangnum
219\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jānāmi {note:jānāmi te (sī. syā.)} dhanaṃ pahūtaṃ, kulavaddhana pūjito tayā casmi;
::

::gathalast
Saggañca patthayāno, tena ahaṃ pabbajissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
220\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ukkaṇṭhitosmi bāḷhaṃ, arati maṃ somadatta āvisati {note:āvīsati (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Bahukāpi {note:bahukā hi (sī. syā.)} me antarāyā, ajjevāhaṃ pabbajissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
221\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idañca tuyhaṃ rucitaṃ, sutasoma ajjeva dāni tvaṃ pabbaja;
::

::gathalast
Ahampi pabbajissāmi, na {pb:T:1.0566} ussahe tayā vinā ahaṃ ṭhātuṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
222\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi sakkā pabbajituṃ, nagare na hi paccati janapade ca’’;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Sutasome pabbajite, kathaṃ nu dāni karissāma’’.
::

::hangnum
223\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::gathalast

### 18. Paṇṇāsanipāto

#### 526. Niḷinikājātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uddayhate {pb:T:2.0001}{pb:V:2.0020}{pb:M:2.0031} {note:uḍḍayhate (sī. pī.)} janapado, raṭṭhañcāpi vinassati;
::

::gathalast
Ehi niḷinike {note:niḷike (sī. syā. pī.), evamuparipi} gaccha, taṃ me brāhmaṇamānaya’’.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ dukkhakkhamā rāja, nāhaṃ addhānakovidā;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ ahaṃ gamissāmi, vanaṃ kuñjarasevitaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phītaṃ janapadaṃ gantvā, hatthinā ca rathena ca;
::

::gathalast
Dārusaṅghāṭayānena, evaṃ gaccha niḷinike.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthiassarathe pattī, gacchevādāya khattiye;
::

::gathalast
Taveva vaṇṇarūpena, vasaṃ tamānayissasi’’.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kadalīdhajapaññāṇo, ābhujīparivārito;
::

::gathalast
Eso padissati rammo, isisiṅgassa assamo.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Eso aggissa saṅkhāto, eso dhūmo padissati;
::

::gathalast
Maññe no aggiṃ hāpeti, isisiṅgo mahiddhiko’’.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañca {pb:T:2.0002} disvāna āyantiṃ, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Isisiṅgo pāvisi bhīto, assamaṃ paṇṇachādanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assamassa ca sā dvāre, geṇḍukenassa {note:bheṇḍukenassa (sī. pī.)} kīḷati;
::

::gathalast
Vidaṃsayantī aṅgāni, guyhaṃ pakāsitāni ca.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañca disvāna kīḷantiṃ, paṇṇasālagato jaṭī;
::

::gathalast
Assamā nikkhamitvāna, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ambho ko nāma so rukkho, yassa tevaṃgataṃ phalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dūrepi khittaṃ pacceti, na taṃ ohāya gacchati’’.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assamassa {pb:M:2.0032} mama {note:maṃ (sī.)} brahme, samīpe gandhamādane;
::

::gatha2
Bahavo {note:pabbate (sī.)} tādisā rukkhā, yassa tevaṃgataṃ phalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dūrepi khittaṃ pacceti, na maṃ ohāya gacchati’’.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etū {pb:V:2.0021} {note:etu (sī. syā. ka.)} bhavaṃ assamimaṃ adetu, pajjañca bhakkhañca paṭiccha dammi;
::

::gathalast
Idamāsanaṃ atra bhavaṃ nisīdatu, ito bhavaṃ mūlaphalāni bhuñjatu’’ {note:khādatu (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ te idaṃ ūrūnamantarasmiṃ, supicchitaṃ kaṇharivappakāsati;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ, kose nu te uttamaṅgaṃ paviṭṭhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ vane mūlaphalesanaṃ caraṃ, āsādayiṃ {pb:T:2.0003} {note:assādayiṃ (ka.)} acchaṃ sughorarūpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So maṃ patitvā sahasājjhapatto, panujja maṃ abbahi {note:abbuhi (syā. ka.)} uttamaṅgaṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāyaṃ vaṇo khajjati kaṇḍuvāyati, sabbañca kālaṃ na labhāmi sātaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paho bhavaṃ kaṇḍumimaṃ vinetuṃ, kurutaṃ bhavaṃ yācito brāhmaṇatthaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gambhīrarūpo te vaṇo salohito, apūtiko vaṇagandho {note:pakkagandho (sī.), pannagandho (syā. pī.)} mahā ca;
::

::gathalast
Karomi te kiñci kasāyayogaṃ, yathā bhavaṃ paramasukhī bhaveyya’’.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:2.0033} mantayogā na kasāyayogā, na osadhā brahmacāri {note:brahmacārī (sī. syā. pī.)} kamanti;
::

::gathalast
Ghaṭṭe mudukena {note:yaṃ te mudu tena (sī.), yaṃ te mudū tena (pī.)} vinehi kaṇḍuṃ {note:kaṇḍukaṃ (pī.)}, yathā ahaṃ paramasukhī bhaveyyaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito nu bhoto katamena assamo, kacci bhavaṃ abhiramasi {note:abhiramasī (pī.)} araññe;
::

::gathalast
Kacci nu te {note:kacci te (pī.)} mūlaphalaṃ pahūtaṃ, kacci bhavantaṃ na vihiṃsanti vāḷā’’.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito {pb:T:2.0004} ujuṃ uttarāyaṃ disāyaṃ, khemānadī himavatā pabhāvī {note:pabhāti (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tassā tīre assamo mayha rammo, aho bhavaṃ assamaṃ mayhaṃ passe.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ambā ca sālā tilakā ca jambuyo, uddālakā pāṭaliyo ca phullā;
::

::gathalast
Samantato kimpurisābhigītaṃ, aho bhavaṃ assamaṃ mayhaṃ passe.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tālā ca mūlā ca phalā ca mettha, vaṇṇena gandhena upetarūpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ bhūmibhāgehi upetarūpaṃ, aho bhavaṃ assamaṃ mayhaṃ passe.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phalā ca mūlā ca pahūtamettha, vaṇṇena gandhena rasenupetā;
::

::gathalast
Āyanti ca luddakā taṃ padesaṃ, mā me tato mūlaphalaṃ ahāsuṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pitā mamaṃ mūlaphalesanaṃ gato, idāni āgacchati sāyakāle;
::

::gathalast
Ubhova gacchāmase assamaṃ taṃ, yāva {pb:T:2.0005} pitā mūlaphalato etu’’.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññe {pb:M:2.0034} bahū isayo sādhurūpā, rājīsayo anumagge vasanti;
::

::gathalast
Te yeva pucchesi mamassamaṃ taṃ, te taṃ nayissanti mamaṃ sakāse’’.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na te kaṭṭhāni bhinnāni, na te udakamābhataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aggīpi te na hāpito {note:hāsito (sī. syā.)}, kiṃ nu mandova jhāyasi.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhinnāni kaṭṭhāni huto ca aggi, tapanīpi te samitā brahmacārī {note:brahmacāri (?)};
::

::gathalast
Pīṭhañca mayhaṃ udakañca hoti, ramasi tuvaṃ {note:tvaṃ (sī.)} brahmabhūto puratthā.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhinnakaṭṭhosi {pb:V:2.0022} anābhatodako, ahāpitaggīsi {note:ahāpitaggīpi (ka.)} asiddhabhojano {note:asiṭṭhabhojano (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Na me tuvaṃ ālapasī mamajja, naṭṭhaṃ nu kiṃ cetasikañca dukkhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idhāgamā jaṭilo brahmacārī, sudassaneyyo sutanū vineti;
::

::gathalast
Nevātidīgho na panātirasso, sukaṇhakaṇhacchadanehi bhoto.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amassujāto {pb:T:2.0006} apurāṇavaṇṇī, ādhārarūpañca panassa kaṇṭhe;
::

::gathalast
Dve yamā {note:dve passa (sī.), dvāssa (pī.)} gaṇḍā uresu jātā, suvaṇṇatindukanibhā {note:suvaṇṇapindūpanibhā (sī.), suvaṇṇatiṇḍusannibhā (syā.), sovannapiṇḍūpanibhā (pī.)} pabhassarā.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mukhañca tassa bhusadassaneyyaṃ, kaṇṇesu lambanti ca kuñcitaggā;
::

::gathalast
Te jotare carato māṇavassa, suttañca yaṃ saṃyamanaṃ jaṭānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññā {pb:M:2.0035} ca tassa saṃyamāni {note:saṃyamanī (sī. pī.)} catasso, nīlā pītā {note:nīlāpi tā (pī.)} lohitikā {note:lohitakā (syā. pī. ka.)} ca setā;
::

::gathalast
Tā piṃsare {note:saṃsare (sī. syā.)} carato māṇavassa, tiriṭi {note:cirīṭi (sī. pī.)} saṅghāriva pāvusamhi.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na mikhalaṃ muñjamayaṃ dhāreti, na santhare {note:santace (sī.), santacaṃ (pī.), santare (ka.)} no pana pabbajassa;
::

::gathalast
Tā jotare jaghanantare {note:jaghanavare (sī. pī.)} vilaggā, sateratā vijjurivantalikkhe.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akhīlakāni ca avaṇṭakāni, heṭṭhā nabhyā kaṭisamohitāni;
::

::gathalast
Aghaṭṭitā niccakīḷaṃ karonti, haṃ tāta kiṃrukkhaphalāni tāni.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jaṭā {pb:T:2.0007} ca tassa bhusadassaneyyā, parosataṃ vellitaggā sugandhā;
::

::gathalast
Dvedhā siro sādhu vibhattarūpo, aho nu kho mayha tathā jaṭāssu.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā ca so pakirati tā jaṭāyo, vaṇṇena gandhena upetarūpā;
::

::gathalast
Nīluppalaṃ vātasameritaṃva, tatheva saṃvāti panassamo ayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṅko ca tassa bhusadassaneyyo, netādiso yādiso mayhaṃ kāye {note:kāyo (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
So vāyatī erito mālutena, vanaṃ yathā aggagimhe suphullaṃ.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nihanti {pb:M:2.0036} so rukkhaphalaṃ pathabyā, sucittarūpaṃ ruciraṃ dassaneyyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khittañca tassa punareti hatthaṃ, haṃ tāta kiṃrukkhaphalaṃ nu kho taṃ.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dantā ca tassa bhusadassaneyyā, suddhā samā saṅkhavarūpapannā;
::

::gathalast
Mano pasādenti vivariyamānā, na hi {note:na ha (sī. pī.)} nūna so sākamakhādi tehi.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akakkasaṃ {pb:T:2.0008} aggaḷitaṃ muhuṃ muduṃ, ujuṃ anuddhataṃ acapalamassa bhāsitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rudaṃ manuññaṃ karavīkasussaraṃ, hadayaṅgamaṃ rañjayateva me mano.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bindussaro nātivisaṭṭhavākyo {note:nātivissaṭṭhavākyo (sī. syā. pī.)}, na nūna sajjhāyamatippayutto;
::

::gathalast
Icchāmi bho {note:kho (sī. syā. pī.)} taṃ punadeva daṭṭhuṃ, mitto hi {note:mittaṃ hi (sī. syā. pī.)} me māṇavohu {note:māṇavāhu (sī. syā.), māṇavāhū (pī.)} puratthā.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Susandhi {pb:V:2.0023} sabbattha vimaṭṭhimaṃ vaṇaṃ, puthū {note:puthuṃ (pī.), puthu (ka.)} sujātaṃ kharapattasannibhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Teneva maṃ uttariyāna māṇavo, vivaritaṃ ūruṃ jaghanena pīḷayi.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tapanti ābhanti virocare ca, sateratā vijjurivantalikkhe;
::

::gathalast
Bāhā mudū añjanalomasādisā, vicitravaṭṭaṅgulikāssa sobhare.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akakkasaṅgo {pb:M:2.0037} na ca dīghalomo, nakhāssa dīghā api lohitaggā;
::

::gathalast
Mudūhi bāhāhi palissajanto, kalyāṇarūpo ramayaṃ {note:ramayhaṃ (ka.)} upaṭṭhahi.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dumassa {pb:T:2.0009} tūlūpanibhā pabhassarā, suvaṇṇakambutalavaṭṭasucchavī;
::

::gathalast
Hatthā mudū tehi maṃ saṃphusitvā, ito gato tena maṃ dahanti tāta.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na nūna {note:na ha nūna (sī. pī.)} so khārividhaṃ ahāsi, na nūna so kaṭṭhāni sayaṃ abhañji;
::

::gathalast
Na nūna so hanti dume kuṭhāriyā {note:kudhāriyā (ka.)}, na hissa {note:na pissa (sī. syā. pī.)} hatthesu khilāni atthi.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accho ca kho tassa vaṇaṃ akāsi, so maṃbravi sukhitaṃ maṃ karohi;
::

::gathalast
Tāhaṃ kariṃ tena mamāsi sokhyaṃ, so cabravi sukhitosmīti brahme.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayañca te māluvapaṇṇasanthatā, vikiṇṇarūpāva mayā ca tena ca;
::

::gathalast
Kilantarūpā udake ramitvā, punappunaṃ paṇṇakuṭiṃ vajāma.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na majja mantā paṭibhanti tāta, na aggihuttaṃ napi yaññatantaṃ {note:yaññatantraṃ (sī.), yaññaṃ tatra (pī. ka.), yaññatatra (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Na cāpi te mūlaphalāni bhuñje, yāva {pb:T:2.0010} na passāmi taṃ brahmacāriṃ.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā {pb:M:2.0038} pajānāsi tuvampi tāta, yassaṃ disaṃ {note:disāyaṃ (syā. pī. ka.)} vasate brahmacārī;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ maṃ disaṃ pāpaya tāta khippaṃ, mā te ahaṃ amarimassamamhi.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vicitraphullaṃ {note:vicitrapupphaṃ (sī. pī.)} hi vanaṃ sutaṃ mayā, dijābhighuṭṭhaṃ dijasaṅghasevitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ maṃ vanaṃ pāpaya tāta khippaṃ, purā te pāṇaṃ vijahāmi assame’’.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imasmāhaṃ jotirase vanamhi, gandhabbadevaccharasaṅghasevite;
::

::gathalast
Isīnamāvāse sanantanamhi, netādisaṃ aratiṃ pāpuṇetha.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavanti mittāni atho na honti, ñātīsu mittesu karonti pemaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ayañca jammo kissa vā niviṭṭho, yo neva jānāti kutomhi āgato.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṃvāsena hi mittāni, sandhiyanti {note:sandhīyanti (sī. pī.)} punappunaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sveva mitto {note:sā ca metti (pī.)} asaṃgantu, asaṃvāsena jīrati.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace {pb:T:2.0011} tuvaṃ dakkhasi brahmacāriṃ, sace tuvaṃ sallape {note:sallapi (sī.)} brahmacārinā;
::

::gathalast
Sampannasassaṃva mahodakena, tapoguṇaṃ khippamimaṃ pahissasi {note:pahassasi (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Punapi {pb:V:2.0024} {note:punappi (pī.)} ce dakkhasi brahmacāriṃ, punapi {note:punappi (pī.)} ce sallape brahmacārinā;
::

::gathalast
Sampannasassaṃva mahodakena, usmāgataṃ khippamimaṃ pahissasi.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhūtāni {pb:M:2.0039} hetāni {note:etāni (pī.)} caranti tāta, virūparūpena manussaloke;
::

::gathalast
Na tāni sevetha naro sapañño, āsajja naṃ nassati brahmacārī’’ti.
::

::centre
Niḷinikājātakaṃ {note:naḷinījātakaṃ (sī.), naḷinijātakaṃ (pī.)} paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 527. Ummādantījātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nivesanaṃ kassa nudaṃ sunanda, pākārena paṇḍumayena guttaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kā dissati aggisikhāva dūre, vehāyasaṃ {note:vehāsayaṃ (sī. pī.)} pabbataggeva acci.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhītā {pb:T:2.0012} nvayaṃ {note:nayaṃ (sī. pī.), nvāyaṃ (syā.)} kassa sunanda hoti, suṇisā nvayaṃ {note:nayaṃ (sī. pī.), nvāyaṃ (syā.)} kassa athopi bhariyā;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi me khippamidheva puṭṭho, avāvaṭā yadi vā atthi bhattā’’.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahañhi jānāmi janinda etaṃ, matyā ca petyā ca athopi assā;
::

::gathalast
Taveva so puriso bhūmipāla, rattindivaṃ appamatto tavatthe.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iddho ca phīto ca suvaḍḍhito {note:subāḷhiko (pī.)} ca, amacco ca te aññataro janinda;
::

::gathalast
Tassesā bhariyābhipārakassa {note:ahipārakassa (sī. pī.), abhipādakassa (ka.)}, ummādantī {note:ummādantīti (ka.)} nāmadheyyena rāja’’.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ambho {pb:M:2.0040} ambho nāmamidaṃ imissā, matyā ca petyā ca kataṃ susādhu;
::

::gathalast
Tadā {note:tathā (sī. syā. pī.)} hi mayhaṃ avalokayantī, ummattakaṃ ummadantī akāsi’’.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yā puṇṇamāse {note:puṇṇamāye (ka.)} migamandalocanā, upāvisi puṇḍarīkattacaṅgī;
::

::gathalast
Dve puṇṇamāyo tadahū amaññahaṃ, disvāna pārāvatarattavāsiniṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aḷārapamhehi {pb:T:2.0013} subhehi vaggubhi, palobhayantī maṃ yadā udikkhati;
::

::gathalast
Vijambhamānā harateva me mano, jātā vane kimpurisīva pabbate.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadā hi brahatī sāmā, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā;
::

::gathalast
Ekaccavasanā nārī, migī bhantāvudikkhati.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kadāssu maṃ tambanakhā sulomā, bāhāmudū candanasāralittā;
::

::gathalast
Vaṭṭaṅgulī sannatadhīrakuttiyā, nārī upaññissati sīsato subhā.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kadāssu maṃ kañcanajāluracchadā, dhītā tirīṭissa vilaggamajjhā;
::

::gathalast
Mudūhi bāhāhi palissajissati, brahāvane jātadumaṃva māluvā.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kadāssu {pb:V:2.0025} {note:kadāssu maṃ (syā. ka.)} lākhārasarattasucchavī, bindutthanī puṇḍarīkattacaṅgī;
::

::gathalast
Mukhaṃ mukhena upanāmayissati, soṇḍova soṇḍassa surāya thālaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadāddasaṃ {note:yathāddasaṃ (pī.)} taṃ tiṭṭhantiṃ, sabbabhaddaṃ {note:sabbagattaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} manoramaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato {pb:T:2.0014} sakassa cittassa, nāvabodhāmi kañcinaṃ {note:kiñcinaṃ (ka.), kiñcanaṃ (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ummādantimahaṃ {pb:M:2.0041} daṭṭhā {note:diṭṭhā (sī. syā. pī. ka.)}, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na supāmi divārattiṃ, sahassaṃva parājito.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakko ce {note:ca (sī. pī.)} me varaṃ dajjā, so ca labbhetha me varo;
::

::gatha2
Ekarattaṃ dvirattaṃ {note:dirattaṃ (pī.)} vā, bhaveyyaṃ abhipārako;
::

::gathalast
Ummādantyā ramitvāna, sivirājā tato siyaṃ’’ {note:siyā (syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhūtāni me bhūtapatī namassato, āgamma yakkho idametadabravi;
::

::gathalast
Rañño mano ummadantyā niviṭṭho, dadāmi te taṃ paricārayassu’’.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puññā vidhaṃse amaro na camhi, jano ca me pāpamidañca {note:pāpamidanti (sī. pī.)} jaññā;
::

::gathalast
Bhuso ca tyassa manaso vighāto, datvā piyaṃ ummadantiṃ adaṭṭhā’’.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Janinda nāññatra tayā mayā vā, sabbāpi kammassa katassa jaññā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ te mayā ummadantī padinnā, bhusehi rājā vanathaṃ sajāhi’’.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo pāpakaṃ kamma karaṃ manusso, so {pb:T:2.0015} maññati māyida {note:māyidha (ka.)} maññiṃsu aññe;
::

::gathalast
Passanti bhūtāni karontametaṃ, yuttā ca ye honti narā pathabyā.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Añño nu te koci {note:kodha (pī.)} naro pathabyā, saddheyya {note:saddaheyya (sī.)} lokasmi na me piyāti;
::

::gathalast
Bhuso ca tyassa manaso vighāto, datvā piyaṃ ummadantiṃ adaṭṭhā’’.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā {pb:M:2.0042} piyā mayha janinda esā, na sā mamaṃ appiyā bhūmipāla;
::

Gaccheva tvaṃ ummadantiṃ bhadante, sīhova selassa guhaṃ upeti’’.

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na pīḷitā attadukhena dhīrā, sukhapphalaṃ kamma pariccajanti;
::

::gathalast
Sammohitā vāpi sukhena mattā, na pāpakammañca {note:pāpakaṃ kamma (pī.)} samācaranti’’.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuvañhi mātā ca pitā ca mayhaṃ, bhattā patī posako devatā ca;
::

::gathalast
Dāso ahaṃ tuyha saputtadāro, yathāsukhaṃ sāmi {note:sibba (sī.), sīvi (syā.)} karohi kāmaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo issaromhīti karoti pāpaṃ, katvā {pb:T:2.0016} ca so nuttasate {note:nuttapate (pī.)} paresaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na tena so jīvati dīghamāyu {note:dīghamāyuṃ (sī. syā.)}, devāpi pāpena samekkhare naṃ.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññātakaṃ sāmikehī padinnaṃ, dhamme ṭhitā ye paṭicchanti dānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paṭicchakā dāyakā cāpi tattha, sukhapphalaññeva karonti kammaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Añño {pb:V:2.0026} nu te koci naro pathabyā, saddheyya lokasmi na me piyāti;
::

::gathalast
Bhuso ca tyassa manaso vighāto, datvā piyaṃ ummadantiṃ adaṭṭhā’’.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā piyā mayha janinda esā, na sā mamaṃ appiyā bhūmipāla;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ te mayā ummadantī padinnā, bhusehi rājā vanathaṃ sajāhi’’.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:M:2.0043} attadukkhena parassa dukkhaṃ, sukhena vā attasukhaṃ dahāti;
::

::gathalast
Yathevidaṃ mayha tathā paresaṃ, yo {note:so (pī.)} evaṃ jānāti {note:pajānāti (ka.)} sa vedi dhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Añño nu te koci naro pathabyā, saddheyya {pb:T:2.0017} lokasmi na me piyāti;
::

::gathalast
Bhuso ca tyassa manaso vighāto, datvā piyaṃ ummadantiṃ adaṭṭhā’’.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Janinda jānāsi piyā mamesā, na sā mamaṃ appiyā bhūmipāla;
::

::gathalast
Piyena te dammi piyaṃ janinda, piyadāyino deva piyaṃ labhanti’’.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So nūnāhaṃ vadhissāmi, attānaṃ kāmahetukaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na hi dhammaṃ adhammena, ahaṃ vadhitumussahe’’.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace tuvaṃ mayha satiṃ {note:santi (ka.)} janinda, na kāmayāsi naravīra seṭṭha;
::

::gathalast
Cajāmi naṃ sabbajanassa sibyā {note:sibba (sī. pī.), majjhe (syā.)}, mayā pamuttaṃ tato avhayesi {note:avhayāsi (ka.)} naṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adūsiyaṃ ce abhipāraka tvaṃ, cajāsi katte ahitāya tyassa;
::

::gathalast
Mahā ca te upavādopi assa, na cāpi tyassa nagaramhi pakkho’’.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ sahissaṃ upavādametaṃ, nindaṃ pasaṃsaṃ garahañca sabbaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mametamāgacchatu bhūmipāla, yathāsukhaṃ {pb:T:2.0018} sivi {note:sibba (sī. pī.)} karohi kāmaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:M:2.0044} neva nindaṃ na panappasaṃsaṃ, ādiyati garahaṃ nopi pūjaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sirī ca lakkhī ca apeti tamhā, āpo suvuṭṭhīva yathā thalamhā’’.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci dukkhañca sukhañca etto, dhammātisārañca manovighātaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Urasā ahaṃ paccuttarissāmi {note:paṭicchissāmi (sī. syā.), paccupadissāmi (pī.)} sabbaṃ, pathavī yathā thāvarānaṃ tasānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammātisārañca manovighātaṃ, dukkhañca nicchāmi ahaṃ paresaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekovimaṃ hārayissāmi bhāraṃ, dhamme ṭhito kiñci ahāpayanto’’.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saggūpagaṃ puññakammaṃ janinda, mā me tuvaṃ antarāyaṃ akāsi;
::

::gathalast
Dadāmi te ummadantiṃ pasanno, rājāva yaññe dhanaṃ brāhmaṇānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā tuvaṃ katte hitesi mayhaṃ, sakhā mamaṃ ummadantī tuvañca;
::

::gathalast
Nindeyyu devā pitaro ca sabbe, pāpañca {pb:T:2.0019} passaṃ abhisamparāyaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hetadhammaṃ sivirāja vajjuṃ, sanegamā jānapadā ca sabbe;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ te mayā ummadantī padinnā, bhusehi rājā vanathaṃ sajāhi’’.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā {pb:V:2.0027} tuvaṃ katte hitesi mayhaṃ, sakhā mamaṃ ummadantī tuvañca;
::

::gathalast
Satañca dhammāni sukittitāni, samuddavelāva duraccayāni’’.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āhuneyyo {pb:M:2.0045} mesi hitānukampī, dhātā vidhātā casi kāmapālo;
::

::gathalast
Tayī hutā rāja mahapphalā hi {note:mahapphalā hi me (pī.)}, kāmena me ummadantiṃ paṭiccha’’.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā hi sabbaṃ abhipāraka tvaṃ, dhammaṃ acārī mama kattuputta;
::

::gathalast
Añño nu te ko idha sotthikattā, dvipado naro aruṇe jīvaloke’’.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuvaṃ nu seṭṭho tvamanuttarosi, tvaṃ dhammagū {note:dhammagutto (sī.)} dhammavidū sumedho;
::

::gathalast
So dhammagutto cirameva jīva, dhammañca {pb:T:2.0020} me desaya dhammapāla’’.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadiṅgha abhipāraka, suṇohi vacanaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ te desayissāmi, sataṃ āsevitaṃ ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sādhu dhammaruci rājā, sādhu paññāṇavā naro;
::

::gathalast
Sādhu mittānamaddubbho, pāpassākaraṇaṃ sukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkodhanassa vijite, ṭhitadhammassa rājino;
::

::gathalast
Sukhaṃ manussā āsetha, sītacchāyāya saṅghare.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na cāhametaṃ abhirocayāmi, kammaṃ asamekkhakataṃ asādhu;
::

::gathalast
Ye vāpi ñatvāna sayaṃ karonti, upamā imā mayhaṃ tuvaṃ suṇohi.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gavaṃ ce taramānānaṃ, jimhaṃ gacchati puṅgavo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbā tā jimhaṃ gacchanti, nette jimhaṃ gate sati.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evameva {note:evamevaṃ (pī.)} manussesu, yo hoti seṭṭhasammato;
::

::gatha2
So ce adhammaṃ carati, pageva itarā pajā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ {pb:T:2.0021} raṭṭhaṃ dukhaṃ seti, rājā ce hoti adhammiko.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gavaṃ {pb:M:2.0046} ce taramānānaṃ, ujuṃ gacchati puṅgavo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbā gāvī ujuṃ yanti, nette ujuṃ gate sati.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evameva manussesu, yo hoti seṭṭhasammato;
::

::gatha2
So sace dhammaṃ carati, pageva itarā pajā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ raṭṭhaṃ sukhaṃ seti, rājā ce hoti dhammiko.
::

::hangnum

::gatha1

#### 528. Mahābodhijātakaṃ (3)

::gatha1

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Saniḷīnikamavhayano paṭhamo, dutiyo pana saummadantivaro;
::

::gathalast
Tatiyo pana bodhisirīvhayano, kathitā pana tīṇi jinena subhāti.

### 19. Saṭṭhinipāto

#### 529. Soṇakajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa {pb:T:2.0031}{pb:V:2.0034}{pb:M:2.0053} sutvā sataṃ dammi, sahassaṃ diṭṭha {note:daṭṭhu (sī. pī.)} soṇakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ko me soṇakamakkhāti, sahāyaṃ paṃsukīḷitaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athabravī māṇavako, daharo pañcacūḷako;
::

::gatha2
Mayhaṃ sutvā sataṃ dehi, sahassaṃ diṭṭha {note:daṭṭhu (sī. pī.)} soṇakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ te soṇakakkhissaṃ {note:ahaṃ soṇakamakkhissaṃ (sī. pī.), ahaṃ te soṇakamakkhissaṃ (syā.)}, sahāyaṃ paṃsukīḷitaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Katamasmiṃ {note:katarasmiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} so janapade, raṭṭhesu nigamesu ca;
::

::gathalast
Kattha soṇakamaddakkhi {note:kattha te soṇako diṭṭho (sī. pī.)}, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito’’.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taveva deva vijite, tavevuyyānabhūmiyā;
::

::gathalast
Ujuvaṃsā mahāsālā, nīlobhāsā manoramā.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṭṭhanti meghasamānā, rammā aññoññanissitā;
::

::gatha2
Tesaṃ mūlamhi {note:mūlasmiṃ (sī. pī.), mūlasmi (syā.)} soṇako, jhāyatī anupādano {note:anupādino (syā.), anupādāno (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Upādānesu lokesu, ḍayhamānesu nibbuto.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato ca rājā pāyāsi, senāya caturaṅgiyā;
::

::gathalast
Kārāpetvā samaṃ maggaṃ, agamā yena soṇako.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uyyānabhūmiṃ gantvāna, vicaranto brahāvane;
::

::gathalast
Āsīnaṃ {pb:T:2.0032} soṇakaṃ dakkhi, ḍayhamānesu nibbutaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kapaṇo vatayaṃ bhikkhu, muṇḍo saṅghāṭipāruto;
::

::gathalast
Amātiko apitiko, rukkhamūlasmi jhāyati’’.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imaṃ vākyaṃ nisāmetvā, soṇako etadabravi;
::

::gathalast
‘Na rāja kapaṇo hoti, dhammaṃ kāyena phassayaṃ {note:phusayaṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘Yo {pb:M:2.0054} ca {note:yodha (sī. syā.)} dhammaṃ niraṃkatvā {note:nirākatvā (?)}, adhammamanuvattati;
::

::gathalast
Sa rāja kapaṇo hoti, pāpo pāpaparāyano’’’.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Arindamoti {pb:V:2.0035} me nāmaṃ, kāsirājāti maṃ vidū;
::

::gathalast
Kacci bhoto sukhasseyyā {note:sukhā seyyā (pī.), sukhaseyyo (ka.)}, idha pattassa soṇaka’’’.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sadāpi bhadramadhanassa, anāgārassa bhikkhuno;
::

::gatha2
Na tesaṃ koṭṭhe openti, na kumbhiṃ na khaḷopiyaṃ {note:na kumbhe na kaḷopiyā (syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Paraniṭṭhitamesānā, tena yāpenti subbatā.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dutiyampi bhadramadhanassa, anāgārassa bhikkhuno;
::

::gathalast
Anavajjapiṇḍo {note:anavajjo piṇḍā (pī.)} bhottabbo, na ca kocūparodhati.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatiyampi bhadramadhanassa, anāgārassa bhikkhuno;
::

::gathalast
Nibbuto piṇḍo bhottabbo, na ca kocūparodhati.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catutthampi {note:catutthaṃ (pī.)} bhadramadhanassa, anāgārassa bhikkhuno;
::

::gathalast
Muttassa raṭṭhe carato, saṅgo yassa na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcamampi {note:pañcamaṃ (pī.)} bhadramadhanassa, anāgārassa bhikkhuno;
::

::gathalast
Nagaramhi ḍayhamānamhi, nāssa kiñci aḍayhatha.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chaṭṭhampi {pb:T:2.0033} {note:chaṭṭhaṃ (pī.)} bhadramadhanassa, anāgārassa bhikkhuno;
::

::gathalast
Raṭṭhe vilumpamānamhi {note:viluppamānamhi (ka.)}, nāssa kiñci ahīratha {note:ahāratha (sī. syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattamampi {note:sattamaṃ (pī.)} bhadramadhanassa, anāgārassa bhikkhuno;
::

::gatha2
Corehi rakkhitaṃ maggaṃ, ye caññe paripanthikā;
::

::gathalast
Pattacīvaramādāya, sotthiṃ gacchati subbato.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhamampi {note:aṭṭhamaṃ (pī.)} bhadramadhanassa, anāgārassa bhikkhuno;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yaṃ disaṃ pakkamati, anapekkhova gacchati’’.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahūpi bhadrā {note:bahūni samaṇabhadrāni (sī.), bahūpi bhadrakā ete (pī.)} etesaṃ, yo tvaṃ bhikkhu pasaṃsasi;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca giddho kāmesu, kathaṃ kāhāmi soṇaka.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyā {pb:M:2.0055} me mānusā kāmā, atho dibyāpi me piyā;
::

::gathalast
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, ubho loke labhāmase’’.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāme giddhā {note:kāmesu giddhā (sī. pī.)} kāmaratā, kāmesu adhimucchitā;
::

::gathalast
Narā pāpāni katvāna, upapajjanti duggatiṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye ca kāme pahantvāna {note:pahatvāna (sī. pī.)}, nikkhantā akutobhayā;
::

::gathalast
Ekodibhāvādhigatā, na te gacchanti duggatiṃ.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upamaṃ te karissāmi, taṃ suṇohi arindama;
::

::gathalast
Upamāya midhekacce {note:pidhekacce (sī. pī.)}, atthaṃ jānanti paṇḍitā.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gaṅgāya {pb:V:2.0036} kuṇapaṃ disvā, vuyhamānaṃ mahaṇṇave;
::

::gathalast
Vāyaso samacintesi, appapañño acetaso.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Yānañca {pb:T:2.0034} vatidaṃ laddhaṃ, bhakkho cāyaṃ anappako’;
::

::gathalast
Tattha rattiṃ tattha divā, tattheva nirato mano.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khādaṃ nāgassa maṃsāni, pivaṃ bhāgīrathodakaṃ {note:bhāgirasodakaṃ (sī. syā. pī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Sampassaṃ vanacetyāni, na palettha {note:paletvā (ka.)} vihaṅgamo.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañca {note:taṃva (pī.)} otaraṇī gaṅgā, pamattaṃ kuṇape rataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samuddaṃ ajjhagāhāsi {note:ajjhagāhayi (pī.)}, agatī yattha pakkhinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So ca bhakkhaparikkhīṇo, udapatvā {note:uppatitvā (sī. syā.), udāpatvā (pī.)} vihaṅgamo.
::

::gathalast
Na pacchato na purato, nuttaraṃ nopi dakkhiṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dīpaṃ so najjhagāgañchi {note:na ajjhagañchi (sī.), na ajjhagacchi (pī.)}, agatī yattha pakkhinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So ca tattheva pāpattha, yathā dubbalako tathā.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañca sāmuddikā macchā, kumbhīlā makarā susū;
::

::gathalast
Pasayhakārā khādiṃsu, phandamānaṃ vipakkhakaṃ {note:vipakkhinaṃ (sī. pī.), vipakkhikaṃ (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evameva {pb:M:2.0056} tuvaṃ rāja, ye caññe kāmabhogino;
::

::gathalast
Giddhā ce na vamissanti, kākapaññāva {note:kākapaññāya (sī. syā. pī.)} te vidū.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esā te upamā rāja, atthasandassanī katā;
::

::gathalast
Tvañca paññāyase tena, yadi kāhasi vā na vā.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekavācampi dvivācaṃ, bhaṇeyya anukampako;
::

::gathalast
Tatuttariṃ na bhāseyya, dāsovayyassa {note:dāso ayyassa (sī.), dāso ayirassa (pī.)} santike’’.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna pakkāmi, soṇako amitabuddhimā {note:soṇako’mitabuddhimā (?)};
::

::gathalast
Vehāse antalikkhasmiṃ, anusāsitvāna khattiyaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko {pb:T:2.0035} nume rājakattāro, suddā veyyattamāgatā {note:sūtā veyyattimāgatā (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Rajjaṃ niyyādayissāmi, nāhaṃ rajjena matthiko.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjeva pabbajissāmi, ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suve;
::

::gathalast
Māhaṃ kākova dummedho, kāmānaṃ vasamanvagaṃ’’ {note:vasamannagā (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthi te daharo putto, dīghāvu raṭṭhavaḍḍhano;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ rajje abhisiñcassu, so no rājā bhavissati’’.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khippaṃ kumāramānetha, dīghāvuṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ rajje abhisiñcissaṃ, so vo rājā bhavissati’’.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:V:2.0037} kumāramānesuṃ, dīghāvuṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ disvā ālapī rājā, ekaputtaṃ manoramaṃ.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

42\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Māhaṃ kākova dummedho, kāmānaṃ vasamanvagaṃ {note:vasamannagā (pī.)}.

::gatha1
‘‘Daharasseva {pb:M:2.0058} me tāta, mātā matāti me sutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tayā vinā ahaṃ tāta, jīvitumpi na ussahe.

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā āraññakaṃ nāgaṃ, poto anveti pacchato;
::

::gathalast
Jessantaṃ giriduggesu, samesu visamesu ca.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ taṃ anugacchāmi, puttamādāya {note:pattamādāya (pī.)} pacchato;
::

::gathalast
Subharo te bhavissāmi, na te hessāmi dubbharo’’.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā sāmuddikaṃ nāvaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vohāro tattha gaṇheyya, vāṇijā byasanī {note:byasanaṃ (ka.)} siyā.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evamevāyaṃ puttakali {note:puttaka (syā.)}, antarāyakaro mama {note:mamaṃ (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Imaṃ kumāraṃ pāpetha, pāsādaṃ rativaḍḍhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha kambusahatthāyo, yathā sakkaṃva accharā;
::

::gathalast
Tā naṃ tattha ramessanti {note:ramissanti (syā. ka.)}, tāhi ceso {note:meso (pī.)} ramissati.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato kumāraṃ pāpesuṃ, pāsādaṃ rativaḍḍhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ disvā avacuṃ kaññā, dīghāvuṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devatā nusi gandhabbo, adu {note:ādu (sī. pī.)} sakko purindado;
::

::gathalast
Ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Namhi devo na gandhabbo, nāpi {note:namhi (ka.)} sakko purindado;
::

::gatha2
Kāsirañño ahaṃ putto, dīghāvu raṭṭhavaḍḍhano;
::

::gathalast
Mamaṃ {note:mama (pī.)} bharatha bhaddaṃ vo {note:bhaddante (ka.)}, ahaṃ bhattā bhavāmi vo’’.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:T:2.0038} tattha avacuṃ kaññā, dīghāvuṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
‘Kuhiṃ rājā anuppatto, ito rājā kuhiṃ gato’’’.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṅkaṃ rājā atikkanto, thale rājā patiṭṭhito;
::

::gathalast
Akaṇṭakaṃ agahanaṃ, paṭipanno mahāpathaṃ.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahañca paṭipannosmi, maggaṃ duggatigāminaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakaṇṭakaṃ sagahanaṃ, yena gacchanti duggatiṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa {pb:V:2.0039}{pb:M:2.0059} te svāgataṃ rāja, sīhasseva giribbajaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anusāsa mahārāja, tvaṃ no sabbāsamissaro’’ti.
::

::centre
Soṇakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 530. Saṃkiccajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvā nisinnaṃ rājānaṃ, brahmadattaṃ rathesabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Athassa paṭivedesi, yassāsi anukampako.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṃkiccāyaṃ anuppatto, isīnaṃ sādhusammato;
::

::gathalast
Taramānarūpo niyyāhi, khippaṃ passa mahesinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato ca rājā taramāno, yuttamāruyha sandanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mittāmaccaparibyūḷho {note:paribbūḷho (sī. pī.)}, agamāsi rathesabho.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nikkhippa pañca kakudhāni, kāsīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano;
::

::gathalast
Vāḷabījani {note:vā ḷavījanī (sī. pī.)} muṇhīsaṃ, khaggaṃ chattañcupāhanaṃ;
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Oruyha rājā yānamhā, ṭhapayitvā paṭicchadaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āsīnaṃ {pb:T:2.0039} dāyapassasmiṃ, saṃkiccamupasaṅkami.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upasaṅkamitvā so rājā, sammodi isinā saha;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ kathaṃ vītisāretvā, ekamantaṃ upāvisi.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekamantaṃ nisinnova, atha kālaṃ amaññatha;
::

::gathalast
Tato pāpāni kammāni, pucchituṃ paṭipajjatha.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Isiṃ pucchāma {note:pucchāmi (sī. pī.)} saṃkiccaṃ, isīnaṃ sādhusammataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āsīnaṃ dāyapassasmiṃ, isisaṅghapurakkhataṃ {note:purakkhitaṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṃ gatiṃ pecca gacchanti, narā dhammāticārino;
::

::gathalast
Aticiṇṇo mayā dhammo, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Isī avaca saṃkicco, kāsīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āsīnaṃ dāyapassasmiṃ, mahārāja suṇohi me.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uppathena {pb:M:2.0060} vajantassa, yo maggamanusāsati;
::

::gathalast
Tassa ce vacanaṃ kayirā, nāssa maggeyya kaṇṭako.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhammaṃ {pb:V:2.0040} paṭipannassa, yo dhammamanusāsati;
::

::gathalast
Tassa ce vacanaṃ kayirā, na so gaccheyya duggatiṃ.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammo patho mahārāja, adhammo pana uppatho;
::

::gathalast
Adhammo nirayaṃ neti, dhammo pāpeti suggatiṃ.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhammacārino rāja, narā visamajīvino;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ gatiṃ pecca gacchanti, niraye te suṇohi me.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sañjīvo kāḷasutto ca, saṅghāto {note:saṅkhāṭo (syā. ka.)} dve ca roruvā;
::

::gathalast
Athāparo {pb:T:2.0040} mahāvīci, tāpano {note:tapano (sī. pī.)} ca patāpano.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iccete aṭṭha nirayā, akkhātā duratikkamā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kadariyatāpanā {note:kadariyatapanā (sī. pī.)} ghorā, accimanto {note:accimantā (pī.)} mahabbhayā;
::

::gathalast
Lomahaṃsanarūpā ca, bhesmā paṭibhayā dukhā.

::hangnum
86\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesaṃ ayomayā bhūmi, jalitā tejasā yutā;
::

::gathalast
Samantā yojanasataṃ, phuṭā {note:pharitvā (a. ni. 3.36; pe. va. 71)} tiṭṭhanti sabbadā.

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
89\.

::gatha1

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum
91\.

::gatha1
‘‘Puratthimena {pb:M:2.0061} dhāvanti, tato dhāvanti pacchato;
::

::gatha2

::gathalast
Yaṃ yañhi dvāraṃ gacchanti, taṃ tadeva pidhīyare {note:pithiyyati (sī.), pithiyyare (syā.), pithīyare (pī.)}.

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum
97\.

::gatha1

Vikkhambhamādāya vibandha {note:vibaddha (sī.), vibhajja (syā. pī.)} rajjubhi, vivaṭe mukhe sampavisanti {note:saṃcavanti (sī. syā. pī.)} rakkhasā.

::gathalast

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
129\.

::gatha1
‘‘Sattīhi lohakūṭehi, nettiṃsehi usūhi ca;

::gathalast
Haññamānā khāranadiṃ, papatanti {note:sampatanti (ka.)} avaṃsirā.
::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāyaṃ pāto kūṭakārī, ayokūṭehi haññati;
::

::gathalast
Tato vantaṃ durattānaṃ, paresaṃ bhuñjare {note:bhuñjate (sī. syā. pī.)} sadā.
::

::hangnum
131\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Vipphandamānaṃ khādanti, naraṃ kibbisakārakaṃ {note:kibbisakārinaṃ (pī.)}.

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye migena migaṃ hanti, pakkhiṃ vā pana pakkhinā;
::

::gathalast
Asanto rajasā channā, gantā {note:gatā (ka.)} te nirayussadaṃ {note:nirayaṃ adho (pī.)}.

::hangnum
133\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Santo {pb:M:2.0065} ca {note:santova (syā.)} uddhaṃ gacchanti, suciṇṇenidha kammunā;
::

::gathalast
Suciṇṇassa phalaṃ passa, saindā {note:sahindā (sī.)} devā sabrahmakā.
::

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:V:2.0044} taṃ brūmi mahārāja, dhammaṃ raṭṭhapatī cara;
::

::gathalast
Tathā {note:tathā tathā (sī. syā. pī.)} rāja carāhi dhammaṃ, yathā taṃ suciṇṇaṃ nānutappeyya pacchā’’ti.

Saṃkiccajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

::centre
Saṭṭhinipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha saṭṭhinipātamhi, suṇātha mama bhāsitaṃ;

::gatha2
Jātakasavhayano {pb:T:2.0046} pavaro, soṇakaarindamasavhayano;

::gathalast
Tathā vuttarathesabhakiccavaroti.
