### 20. Sattatinipāto

#### 531. Kusajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:T:2.0047}{pb:V:2.0045}{pb:M:2.0066} te raṭṭhaṃ sadhanaṃ sayoggaṃ, sakāyuraṃ sabbakāmūpapannaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idaṃ te rajjaṃ {note:raṭṭhaṃ (ka.)} anusāsa amma, gacchāmahaṃ yattha piyā pabhāvatī’’.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anujjubhūtena haraṃ mahantaṃ, divā ca ratto ca nisīthakāle {note:nisīda kāle (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Paṭigaccha tvaṃ khippaṃ kusāvatiṃ kusa {note:kusāvatiṃ (syā. ka.)}, nicchāmi dubbaṇṇamahaṃ vasantaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ gamissāmi ito kusāvatiṃ, pabhāvatī vaṇṇapalobhito tava;
::

::gathalast
Ramāmi maddassa niketaramme, hitvāna raṭṭhaṃ tava dassane rato.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabhāvatī vaṇṇapalobhito tava, sammūḷharūpo vicarāmi mediniṃ {note:medaniṃ (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Disaṃ na jānāmi kutomhi āgato, tayamhi matto migamandalocane.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suvaṇṇacīravasane, jātarūpasumekhale;
::

::gathalast
Sussoṇi {pb:T:2.0048} tava kāmā hi {note:kāmehi (sī. syā. pī.)}, nāhaṃ rajjena matthiko’’.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abbhūti {note:abbhū hi (sī.), abhūti (syā.), abbhu hi (pī.)} tassa bho hoti, yo anicchantamicchati;
::

::gathalast
Akāmaṃ rāja kāmesi {note:kāmehi (sī. pī.)}, akantaṃ kantu {note:akanto kanta (sī. syā. pī.)} micchasi’’.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akāmaṃ vā sakāmaṃ vā, yo naro labhate piyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Lābhamettha pasaṃsāma, alābho tattha pāpako’’.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāsāṇasāraṃ {pb:M:2.0067} khaṇasi, kaṇikārassa dārunā;
::

::gathalast
Vātaṃ jālena bādhesi, yo anicchantamicchasi’’.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāsāṇo nūna te hadaye, ohito mudulakkhaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Yo te sātaṃ na vindāmi, tirojanapadāgato.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā maṃ bhakuṭiṃ {note:bhūkuṭiṃ (sī. pī.)} katvā, rājaputtī udikkhati {note:rājaputti udikkhasi (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Āḷāriko tadā homi, rañño maddassantepure {note:maddassa thīpure (sī. pī.) evamuparipi}.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā umhayamānā maṃ, rājaputtī udikkhati {note:rājaputti udikkhasi (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Nāḷāriko tadā homi, rājā homi tadā kuso’’.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace {pb:V:2.0046} hi vacanaṃ saccaṃ, nemittānaṃ bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Neva me tvaṃ patī assa, kāmaṃ chindantu sattadhā’’.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace hi vacanaṃ saccaṃ, aññesaṃ yadi vā mamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Neva tuyhaṃ patī atthi, añño sīhassarā kusā’’.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nekkhaṃ gīvaṃ te kāressaṃ, patvā khujje kusāvatiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sace maṃ nāganāsūrū, olokeyya pabhāvatī.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nekkhaṃ {pb:T:2.0049} gīvaṃ te kāressaṃ, patvā khujje kusāvatiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sace maṃ nāganāsūrū, ālapeyya pabhāvatī.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nekkhaṃ gīvaṃ te kāressaṃ, patvā khujje kusāvatiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sace maṃ nāganāsūrū, umhāyeyya pabhāvatī.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nekkhaṃ gīvaṃ te kāressaṃ, patvā khujje kusāvatiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sace maṃ nāganāsūrū, pamhāyeyya pabhāvatī.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nekkhaṃ gīvaṃ te kāressaṃ, patvā khujje kusāvatiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sace me nāganāsūrū, pāṇīhi upasamphuse’’.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi nūnāyaṃ rājaputtī, kuse sātampi vindati;
::

::gathalast
Āḷārike bhate pose, vetanena anatthike’’.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi nūnāyaṃ sā {note:nūna ayaṃ (sī. syā.)} khujjā, labhati jivhāya chedanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sunisitena satthena, evaṃ dubbhāsitaṃ bhaṇaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā {pb:M:2.0068} naṃ rūpena pāmesi, ārohena pabhāvati;
::

::gathalast

::gatha1

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tava kāmā hi sussoṇi, pahu {note:bahu (syā.), bahū (pī.), bahuṃ (ka.)} dukkhaṃ titikkhisaṃ {note:titikkhissaṃ (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
75\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Atha dakkhatha me vegaṃ, vidhamantassa {note:vidhamentassa (sabbattha)} sattavo’’.

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
77\.

::gathalast

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa taṃ nadato sutvā, sīhassevitare migā;
::

::gathalast
Khattiyā {pb:T:2.0056} vipalāyiṃsu, kusasaddabhayaṭṭitā {note:kusasaddabhayaṭṭhitā (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
79\.

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
81\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jīvaggāhaṃ {note:jīvagāhaṃ (sī. pī.)} gahetvāna, bandhitvā satta khattiye;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbeva te vasaṃ gatā, amittā vihatā tava;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuyheva sattavo ete, na hi te mayha sattavo;
::

::gathalast
Tvaññeva no mahārāja, muñca vā te hanassu vā’’.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imā {pb:V:2.0051} te dhītaro satta, devakaññūpamā subhā;
::

::gathalast
Dadāhi nesaṃ ekekaṃ, hontu jāmātaro tava’’.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amhākañceva tāsañca, tvaṃ no sabbesamissaro;
::

::gathalast
Tvaññeva no mahārāja, dehi nesaṃ yadicchasi’’.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekamekassa ekekaṃ, adā sīhassaro kuso;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pīṇitā tena lābhena, tuṭṭhā sīhassare kuse;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabhāvatiñca ādāya, maṇiṃ verocanaṃ subhaṃ {note:tadā (pī.)};
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tyassu {pb:M:2.0074} ekarathe yantā, pavisantā kusāvatiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samānā vaṇṇarūpena, nāññamaññātirocisuṃ {note:nāññamaññamatirocayuṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mātā puttena saṅgacchi {note:saṅgañchi (sī. syā. pī.)}, ubhayo ca jayampatī;
::

::gathalast
Samaggā te tadā āsuṃ, phītaṃ dharaṇimāvasu’’nti.
::

::centre
Kusajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 532. Soṇanandajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devatā nusi gandhabbo, adu {note:ādu (sī. syā.)} sakko purindado;
::

::gathalast
Manussabhūto iddhimā, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāpi devo na gandhabbo, nāpi sakko purindado;
::

::gathalast
Manussabhūto iddhimā, evaṃ jānāhi bhāradha’’ {note:bhārabha (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Katarūpamidaṃ bhoto {note:bhoto (sī. pī.)}, veyyāvaccaṃ anappakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Devamhi vassamānamhi, anovassaṃ bhavaṃ akā.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato vātātape ghore, sītacchāyaṃ bhavaṃ akā;
::

::gathalast
Tato amittamajjhesu {note:amittamajjhe ca (sī.)}, saratāṇaṃ bhavaṃ akā.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato phītāni raṭṭhāni, vasino te bhavaṃ akā;
::

::gathalast
Tato ekasataṃ khatye, anuyante {note:anuyutte (pī.)} bhavaṃ akā.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Patītāssu {pb:T:2.0058}{pb:V:2.0052} mayaṃ bhoto, vada taṃ {note:vara taṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} bhañja {note:bhañña (sī. pī.), bhuñja (syā. ka.)} micchasi;
::

::gatha2
Hatthiyānaṃ assarathaṃ, nāriyo ca alaṅkatā;
::

::gathalast
Nivesanāni rammāni, mayaṃ bhoto dadāmase.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha vaṅge {note:atha vā saṅge (sī. pī.)} vā magadhe, mayaṃ bhoto dadāmase;
::

::gathalast
Atha vā assakāvantī {note:assakāvantiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, sumanā damma te mayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upaḍḍhaṃ vāpi rajjassa, mayaṃ bhoto dadāmase;
::

::gathalast
Sace te attho rajjena, anusāsa yadicchasi’’.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:2.0075} me atthopi rajjena, nagarena dhanena vā;
::

::gathalast
Athopi janapadena, attho mayhaṃ na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhotova raṭṭhe vijite, araññe atthi assamo;
::

::gathalast
Pitā mayhaṃ janettī ca, ubho sammanti assame.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesāhaṃ {note:tesvahaṃ (ka.)} pubbācariyesu, puññaṃ na labhāmi kātave;
::

::gathalast
Bhavantaṃ ajjhāvaraṃ katvā, soṇaṃ {note:sonaṃ (pī.)} yācemu saṃvaraṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Karomi te taṃ vacanaṃ, yaṃ maṃ bhaṇasi brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Etañca kho no akkhāhi, kīvanto hontu yācakā’’.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Parosataṃ jānapadā, mahāsālā ca brāhmaṇā;
::

::gatha2
Ime ca khattiyā sabbe, abhijātā yasassino;
::

::gathalast
Bhavañca rājā manojo, alaṃ hessanti yācakā’’.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthī asse ca yojentu, rathaṃ sannayha sārathi {note:naṃ rathi (pī.)};
::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast
Assamaṃ {pb:T:2.0059} taṃ gamissāmi, yattha sammati kosiyo’’.

::hangnum
106\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Labhetha mānaṃ pūjaṃ vā {note:pūjañca (pī.)}, pitā vā puttakāraṇā.
::

::hangnum
180\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yasmā ca saṅgahā {note:saṅgahe (dī. ni. 3.273; a. ni. 4.32) tadaṭṭhakathāyo oloketabbā} ete, sammapekkhanti {note:samavekkhanti (sī. syā. pī.) a. ni. 4.32} paṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā mahattaṃ papponti, pāsaṃsā ca bhavanti te.
::

::hangnum
181\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Brahmāti {pb:V:2.0058}{pb:M:2.0082} {note:brahmā hi (pī.)} mātāpitaro, pubbācariyāti vuccare;
::

::gathalast
Āhuneyyā {pb:T:2.0067} ca puttānaṃ, pajāya anukampakā.
::

::hangnum
182\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā hi ne namasseyya, sakkareyya ca paṇḍito;
::

::gatha2
Annena atho {note:matho (pī.), atha (a. ni. 4.63; itivu. 106)} pānena, vatthena sayanena ca;
::

::gathalast
Ucchādanena nhāpanena {note:nahāpanena (sī. pī.)}, pādānaṃ dhovanena ca.
::

::hangnum
183\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāya naṃ pāricariyāya {note:paricariyāya (pī.)}, mātāpitūsu paṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Idheva naṃ pasaṃsanti, pecca sagge pamodatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Soṇanandajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

::centre
Sattatinipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha sattatimamhi nipātavare, sabhāvantu kusāvatirājavaro;
::

::gathalast
Atha soṇasunandavaro ca puna, abhivāsitasattatimamhi suteti.
::

### 21. Asītinipāto

#### 533. Cūḷahaṃsajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumukha {pb:T:2.0068}{pb:V:2.0059}{pb:M:2.0083} anupacinantā, pakkamanti vihaṅgamā;
::

::gathalast
Gaccha tuvampi mā kaṅkhi, natthi baddhe {note:bandhe (syā. ka.)} sahāyatā’’.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gacche vāhaṃ na vā gacche, na tena amaro siyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sukhitaṃ taṃ upāsitvā, dukkhitaṃ taṃ kathaṃ jahe.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maraṇaṃ vā tayā saddhiṃ, jīvitaṃ vā tayā vinā;
::

::gathalast
Tadeva maraṇaṃ seyyo, yañce jīve tayā vinā.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nesa dhammo mahārāja, yaṃ taṃ evaṃ gataṃ jahe;
::

::gathalast
Yā gati tuyhaṃ sā mayhaṃ, ruccate vihagādhipa.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kā nu pāsena baddhassa {note:bandhassa (syā. ka.)}, gati aññā mahānasā;
::

::gathalast
Sā kathaṃ cetayānassa, muttassa tava ruccati.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṃ vā tvaṃ passase atthaṃ, mama tuyhañca pakkhima;
::

::gathalast
Ñātīnaṃ vāvasiṭṭhānaṃ, ubhinnaṃ jīvitakkhaye.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ na kañcanadepiñcha {note:depiccha (sī. pī.), dvepiccha (syā.)}, andhena tamasā gataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tādise sañcajaṃ pāṇaṃ, kamatthamabhijotaye’’.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ nu patataṃ seṭṭha, dhamme atthaṃ na bujjhasi {note:bujjhase (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Dhammo apacito santo, atthaṃ dasseti pāṇinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sohaṃ dhammaṃ apekkhāno, dhammā catthaṃ samuṭṭhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhattiñca {pb:T:2.0069} tayi sampassaṃ, nāvakaṅkhāmi jīvitaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā eso sataṃ dhammo, yo mitto mittamāpade;
::

::gathalast
Na caje jīvitassāpi, hetudhammamanussaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāyaṃ dhammo ca te ciṇṇo, bhatti ca viditā mayi;
::

::gathalast
Kāmaṃ karassu mayhetaṃ, gacchevānumato mayā’’.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Api {pb:V:2.0060}{pb:M:2.0084} tvevaṃ gate kāle, yaṃ khaṇḍaṃ {note:baddhaṃ (sī.), bandhaṃ (pī.)} ñātinaṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Tayā taṃ buddhisampannaṃ {note:buddhisampanna (sī. syā. pī.)}, assa paramasaṃvutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iccevaṃ {note:icceva (sī. pī.)} mantayantānaṃ, ariyānaṃ ariyavuttinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paccadissatha nesādo, āturānamivantako.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te sattumabhisañcikkha, dīgharattaṃ hitā dijā;
::

::gathalast
Tuṇhīmāsittha ubhayo, na sañcalesumāsanā {note:na ca sañcesu’māsanā (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhataraṭṭhe ca disvāna, samuḍḍente tato tato;
::

::gathalast
Abhikkamatha vegena, dijasattu dijādhipe.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So ca vegenabhikkamma, āsajja parame dije;
::

::gathalast
Paccakamittha {note:paccakampittha (sī. syā. pī.)} nesādo, baddhā iti vicintayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekaṃva baddhamāsīnaṃ, abaddhañca punāparaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āsajja baddhamāsīnaṃ, pekkhamānamadīnavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato so vimatoyeva, paṇḍare ajjhabhāsatha;
::

::gathalast
Pavaḍḍhakāye āsīne, dijasaṅghagaṇādhipe.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ nu pāsena mahatā, baddho na kurute disaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atha {pb:T:2.0070} kasmā abaddho tvaṃ, balī pakkhi na gacchasi.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kinnu tyāyaṃ {note:tā’yaṃ (sī. pī. ka.)} dijo hoti, mutto baddhaṃ upāsasi;
::

::gathalast
Ohāya sakuṇā yanti, kiṃ eko avahīyasi’’.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājā me so dijāmitta, sakhā pāṇasamo ca me;
::

::gathalast
Neva naṃ vijahissāmi, yāva kālassa pariyāyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ panāyaṃ vihaṅgo, nāddasa pāsamoḍḍitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Padañhetaṃ mahantānaṃ, boddhumarahanti āpadaṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā parābhavo hoti, poso jīvitasaṅkhaye;
::

::gathalast
Atha jālañca pāsañca, āsajjāpi na bujjhati.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Api {pb:M:2.0085} tveva mahāpañña, pāsā bahuvidhā tatā {note:tatā (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Guyhamāsajja {note:gūḷhamāsajja (sī. pī.)} bajjhanti, athevaṃ jīvitakkhaye’’.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Api nāyaṃ tayā saddhiṃ, saṃvāsassa {note:sambhāsassa (sī. pī.)} sukhudrayo;
::

::gathalast
Api no anumaññāsi, api no jīvitaṃ dade’’.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na ceva me tvaṃ baddhosi, napi icchāmi te vadhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāmaṃ khippamito gantvā, jīva tvaṃ anigho ciraṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nevāhametamicchāmi{pb:V:2.0061}, aññatretassa jīvitā;
::

::gathalast
Sace ekena tuṭṭhosi, muñcetaṃ mañca bhakkhaya.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ārohapariṇāhena, tulyāsmā {note:tulyāmhā (ka.)} vayasā ubho;
::

::gathalast
Na te lābhena jīvatthi {note:jīnatthi (sī. syā. pī.)}, etena niminā tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadiṅgha {pb:T:2.0071} samapekkhassu {note:samavekkhasu (sī. pī.)}, hotu giddhi tavamhasu {note:tavasmasu (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Maṃ pubbe bandha pāsena, pacchā muñca dijādhipaṃ.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāvadeva ca te lābho, katāssa {note:katassā (sī. pī.)} yācanāya ca;
::

::gathalast
Mitti ca dhataraṭṭhehi, yāvajīvāya te siyā’’.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Passantu no mahāsaṅghā, tayā muttaṃ ito gataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mittāmaccā ca bhaccā ca, puttadārā ca bandhavā.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na ca te tādisā mittā, bahūnaṃ {note:bahunnaṃ (sī. pī.)} idha vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Yathā tvaṃ dhataraṭṭhassa, pāṇasādhāraṇo sakhā.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So te sahāyaṃ muñcāmi, hotu rājā tavānugo;
::

::gathalast
Kāmaṃ khippamito gantvā, ñātimajjhe virocatha’’.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So patīto pamuttena, bhattunā {note:bhattuno (syā.)} bhattugāravo;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhabhāsatha vakkaṅgo {note:vaṅkaṅgo (syā.)}, vācaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ bhaṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Yathāhamajja nandāmi, muttaṃ disvā dijādhipaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ehi {pb:M:2.0086} taṃ anusikkhāmi, yathā tvamapi lacchase;
::

::gathalast
Lābhaṃ tavāyaṃ {note:yathāyaṃ (sī. pī.)} dhataraṭṭho, pāpaṃ kiñci {note:kañci (sī.)} na dakkhati.
::

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::gathalast

::gathalast

::gathalast

::gatha1

::gathalast

::gatha1

::hangnum
44\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
45\.

::gatha1

::gathalast
Bhatturatthe parakkanto, dhammayutto {note:dhamme yutto (sī. pī.)} vihaṅgamo.

::hangnum
46\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
47\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::gatha1

54\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Ettheva hi ime āsuṃ {note:assu (sī. syā. pī.)}, ubho anumatā mayā.

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
56\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Sabbasākuṇikāgāme, taṃ passa manujādhipa’’.

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvā nisinnaṃ rājānaṃ, pīṭhe sovaṇṇaye subhe;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhabhāsatha vakkaṅgo, vācaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ bhaṇaṃ.

::hangnum
58\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Kacci raṭṭhamidaṃ phītaṃ, dhammena manusāsasi’’.

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusalañceva me haṃsa, atho haṃsa anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atho raṭṭhamidaṃ phītaṃ, dhammena manusāsahaṃ’’ {note:manusissati (sī. pī.)}.

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci bhoto amaccesu, doso koci na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Kacci ca {note:kaccinnu (sī. pī.)} te tavatthesu, nāvakaṅkhanti jīvitaṃ’’.

::hangnum
61\.

::gatha1
‘‘Athopi {pb:M:2.0088} me amaccesu, doso koci na vijjati;

::hangnum
62\.

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci te sādisī bhariyā, assavā piyabhāṇinī;
::

::gathalast
Puttarūpayasūpetā, tava chandavasānugā’’.

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atho me sādisī bhariyā, assavā piyabhāṇinī;
::

::gathalast
Puttarūpayasūpetā, mama chandavasānugā’’.

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhavantaṃ {note:bhavaṃ tu (sī. pī.), bhavannu (syā.)} kacci nu mahā-sattuhatthattataṃ {note:hatthatthataṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} gato;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhamāpajji vipulaṃ, tasmiṃ paṭhamamāpade.

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci yantāpatitvāna, daṇḍena samapothayi;
::

::gathalast
Evametesaṃ jammānaṃ, pātikaṃ {note:pākatikaṃ (sī. pī.)} bhavati tāvade’’.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khemamāsi mahārāja, evamāpadiyā sati {note:evamāpadi saṃsati (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Na cāyaṃ kiñci rasmāsu, sattūva samapajjatha.

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paccagamittha nesādo, pubbeva ajjhabhāsatha;
::

::gathalast
Tadāyaṃ sumukhoyeva, paṇḍito paccabhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa {pb:T:2.0075} taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, pasādamayamajjhagā;
::

::gathalast
Tato maṃ pāmucī pāsā, anuññāsi sukhena ca.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idañca sumukheneva, etadatthāya cintitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhoto sakāsegamanaṃ {note:sakāse + āgamanaṃ}, etassa dhanamicchatā’’.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgatañcevidaṃ bhavataṃ, patīto casmi dassanā;
::

::gathalast
Eso cāpi bahuṃ vittaṃ, labhataṃ yāvadicchati’’ {note:yāvaticchati (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Santappayitvā {pb:V:2.0064} nesādaṃ, bhogehi manujādhipo;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhabhāsatha vakkaṅgaṃ, vācaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ bhaṇaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ khalu dhammamādhīnaṃ, vaso vattati kiñcanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbatthissariyaṃ tava {note:sabbatthissariyaṃ bhavataṃ (sī. syā. pī.), sabbissariyaṃ bhavataṃ (syā. ka.)}, taṃ pasāsa {note:pasāsatha (sī. syā. pī.)} yadicchatha.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dānatthaṃ {pb:M:2.0089} upabhottuṃ vā, yaṃ caññaṃ upakappati;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ dadāmi vo vittaṃ, issariyaṃ {note:isseraṃ (sī.), issaraṃ (pī.)} vissajāmi vo’’.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā ca myāyaṃ sumukho, ajjhabhāseyya paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Kāmasā buddhisampanno, taṃ myāssa paramappiyaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ khalu mahārāja, nāgarājārivantaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paṭivattuṃ na sakkomi, na me so vinayo siyā.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amhākañceva so {note:yo (sī. pī.)} seṭṭho, tvañca uttamasattavo;
::

::gathalast
Bhūmipālo manussindo, pūjā bahūhi hetuhi.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesaṃ ubhinnaṃ bhaṇataṃ, vattamāne vinicchaye;
::

::gathalast
Nantaraṃ {note:nāntaraṃ (sī. pī.)} paṭivattabbaṃ, pessena {note:pesena (ka.)} manujādhipa’’.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammena {pb:T:2.0076} kira nesādo, paṇḍito aṇḍajo iti;
::

::gathalast
Na heva akatattassa, nayo etādiso siyā.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ aggapakatimā, evaṃ uttamasattavo;
::

::gathalast
Yāvatatthi mayā diṭṭhā, nāññaṃ passāmi edisaṃ.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuṭṭhosmi vo pakatiyā, vākyena madhurena ca;
::

::gathalast
Eso cāpi mamacchando, ciraṃ passeyya vo ubho’’.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kiccaṃ {note:yaṃkiñci (pī.)} parame mitte, katamasmāsu {note:rasmāsu (sī. pī.)} taṃ tayā;
::

::gathalast
Pattā nissaṃsayaṃ tyāmhā {note:tyamhā (pī.)}, bhattirasmāsu yā tava.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aduñca nūna sumahā, ñātisaṅghassa mantaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Adassanena asmākaṃ {note:amhākaṃ (sī. pī.)}, dukkhaṃ bahūsu pakkhisu.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesaṃ sokavighātāya, tayā anumatā mayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ padakkhiṇato katvā, ñātiṃ {note:ñātī (sī. syā. pī.)} passemurindama {note:passemarindama (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhāhaṃ vipulaṃ pītiṃ, bhavataṃ vindāmi dassanā;
::

::gathalast
Eso cāpi mahā attho, ñātivissāsanā siyā’’.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:M:2.0090} vatvā dhataraṭṭho {note:dhataraṭṭhā (sī.)}, haṃsarājā narādhipaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uttamaṃ javamanvāya {note:uttamajavamattāya (sī. pī.)}, ñātisaṅghaṃ upāgamuṃ.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te {pb:V:2.0065} aroge anuppatte, disvāna parame dije;
::

::gathalast
Kekāti makaruṃ haṃsā, puthusaddo ajāyatha.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te patītā pamuttena, bhattunā bhattugāravā;
::

::gathalast
Samantā parikiriṃsu {note:parikariṃsu (sī. syā. pī.)}, aṇḍajā laddhapaccayā’’.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ {pb:T:2.0077} mittavataṃ atthā, sabbe honti padakkhiṇā;
::

::gathalast
Haṃsā yathā dhataraṭṭhā, ñātisaṅghaṃ upāgamu’’nti.
::

::centre
Cūḷa {note:culla (sī. syā. pī.)} haṃsajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 534. Mahāhaṃsajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ete haṃsā pakkamanti, vakkaṅgā bhayameritā;
::

::gathalast
Harittaca hemavaṇṇa, kāmaṃ sumukha pakkama.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ohāya maṃ ñātigaṇā, ekaṃ pāsavasaṃ gataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anapekkhamānā gacchanti, kiṃ eko avahīyasi.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pateva patataṃ seṭṭha, natthi baddhe sahāyatā;
::

::gathalast
Mā anīghāya hāpesi, kāmaṃ sumukha pakkama’’.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ dukkhaparetopi {note:dukkhapareto’’ti (jā. 1.15.136) aṭṭhakathāyo oloketabbā}, dhataraṭṭha tuvaṃ {note:tavaṃ (sī. pī.)} jahe;
::

::gathalast
Jīvitaṃ maraṇaṃ vā me, tayā saddhiṃ bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ dukkhaparetopi, dhataraṭṭha tuvaṃ jahe;
::

::gathalast
Na maṃ anariyasaṃyutte, kamme yojetumarahasi.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakumāro sakhā tyasmi, sacitte casmi te {note:samite (pī.), tyasmi te (ka.)} ṭhito;
::

::gathalast
Ñāto senāpati tyāhaṃ, haṃsānaṃ pavaruttama.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ {pb:M:2.0091} ahaṃ vikatthissaṃ {note:vikattissaṃ (pī.)}, ñātimajjhe ito gato;
::

::gatha2
Taṃ hitvā patataṃ seṭṭha, kiṃ te vakkhāmito gato;
::

::gathalast
Idha pāṇaṃ cajissāmi, nānariyaṃ {note:na anariyaṃ (pī.)} kattumussahe’’.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Eso {pb:T:2.0078} hi dhammo sumukha, yaṃ tvaṃ ariyapathe ṭhito;
::

::gathalast
Yo bhattāraṃ sakhāraṃ maṃ, na pariccattumussahe.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañhi me pekkhamānassa, bhayaṃ natveva jāyati;
::

::gathalast
Adhigacchasi tvaṃ mayhaṃ, evaṃ bhūtassa jīvitaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iccevaṃ {pb:V:2.0066} {note:icceva (sī. pī.)} mantayantānaṃ, ariyānaṃ ariyavuttinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Daṇḍamādāya nesādo, āpatī {note:āpadī (ka.)} turito bhusaṃ.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamāpatantaṃ disvāna, sumukho atibrūhayi {note:aparibrūhayi (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭhāsi purato rañño, haṃso vissāsayaṃ byadhaṃ {note:byathaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā bhāyi patataṃ seṭṭha, na hi bhāyanti tādisā;
::

::gatha2
Ahaṃ yogaṃ payuñjissaṃ, yuttaṃ dhammūpasaṃhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena pariyāpadānena {note:pariyādānena (ka.)}, khippaṃ pāsā pamokkhasi’’.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, sumukhassa subhāsitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pahaṭṭhalomo nesādo, añjalissa paṇāmayi.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na me sutaṃ vā diṭṭhaṃ vā, bhāsanto mānusiṃ dijo;
::

::gathalast
Ariyaṃ bruvāno {note:brūhanto (syā. ka.)} vakkaṅgo, cajanto mānusiṃ giraṃ.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kinnu tāyaṃ dijo hoti, mutto baddhaṃ upāsasi;
::

::gathalast
Ohāya sakuṇā yanti, kiṃ eko avahīyasi’’.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājā me so dijāmitta, senāpaccassa kārayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tamāpade pariccattuṃ, nussahe vihagādhipaṃ.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāgaṇāya bhattā me, mā eko byasanaṃ agā;
::

::gathalast
Tathā {pb:T:2.0079} taṃ samma nesāda, bhattāyaṃ abhito rame’’.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ariyavattasi {pb:M:2.0092} vakkaṅga, yo piṇḍamapacāyasi;
::

::gathalast
Cajāmi te taṃ bhattāraṃ, gacchathūbho {note:gacchatu bho (pī.)} yathāsukhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace attappayogena, ohito haṃsapakkhinaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘No ce attappayogena, ohito haṃsapakkhinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anissaro muñcamamhe, theyyaṃ kayirāsi luddaka’’.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa tvaṃ bhatako {note:bhaṭako (ka.)} rañño, kāmaṃ tasseva pāpaya;
::

::gathalast
Tattha saṃyamano {note:saṃyamāno (pī.)} rājā, yathābhiññaṃ karissati’’.
::

::hangnum
110\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te pañjaragate pakkhī, ubho bhassaravaṇṇine;
::

::gathalast
Sumukhaṃ dhataraṭṭhañca, luddo ādāya pakkami’’.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Harīyamāno {pb:V:2.0067} dhataraṭṭho, sumukhaṃ etadabravi;
::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Koñcī samuddatīreva, kapaṇā nūna rucchati’’.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ mahanto lokassa, appameyyo mahāgaṇī;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avinicchayaññu atthesu, mandova paṭibhāsi {note:paṭibhāti (ka.)} maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiccākiccaṃ na jānāsi, sampatto kālapariyāyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Māyā {pb:M:2.0093} cesā marīcī ca, soko rogo cupaddavo;
::

::gatha2
Kharā ca bandhanā cetā, maccupāsā guhāsayā {note:paccupāso guhāsayo (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tāsu yo vissase poso, so naresu narādhamo’’.
::

::hangnum
119\.

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ vuddhehi upaññātaṃ, ko taṃ ninditumarahati;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast
Tāsu ko nibbide {note:nibbije (ka.)} poso, pāṇamāsajja pāṇibhi {note:pāṇahi (sī.)}.

::hangnum
121\.

::gatha1
‘‘Tvameva nañño sumukha, thīnaṃ atthesu yuñjasi;

::hangnum
122\.

::gatha1

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gathalast

126\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast
Tava pariyāpadānena, mama pāṇesanaṃ cara’’.

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum
148\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
149\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
150\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appevatthavatiṃ vācaṃ, byāhareyyuṃ {note:byākareyyuṃ (sī. pī.)} idhāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Tathā taṃ samma nesādo, vutto sumukha maggahi’’.
::

::hangnum
151\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Neva bhītā {note:bhūtā (syā. ka.)} kāsipati, upanītasmi jīvite;
::

::gathalast
Bhāsematthavatiṃ vācaṃ, sampattā kālapariyāyaṃ.

::hangnum

::gatha1

#### 535. Sudhābhojanajātakaṃ (3)

::gatha1

::gatha1

215\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
216\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
217\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
218\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
219\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
220\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

221\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast
Sace na jānātha idhuttamādhamaṃ’’.

::gathalast

::hangnum
224\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum
227\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
228\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ {pb:T:2.0094}{pb:M:2.0104} mahindena mahesi pesito, sudhābhihāsiṃ turito mahāmuni;
::

::gathalast
Jānāsi maṃ mātali devasārathi, bhuñjassu bhattuttama mābhivārayi {note:mā vicārayi (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
229\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhuttā ca sā dvādasa hanti pāpake, khudaṃ pipāsaṃ aratiṃ daraklamaṃ {note:darathaṃ kilaṃ (syā.), darathakkhamaṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Kodhūpanāhañca vivādapesuṇaṃ, sītuṇhatandiñca rasuttamaṃ idaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
230\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na kappatī mātali mayha bhuñjituṃ, pubbe adatvā iti me vatuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na cāpi ekāsnamarīyapūjitaṃ {note:ekāsanaṃ ariyapūjitaṃ (sī. pī.)}, asaṃvibhāgī ca sukhaṃ na vindati’’.
::

::hangnum
231\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Thīghātakā ye cime pāradārikā, mittadduno ye ca sapanti subbate;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gathalast
Āsā ca saddhā ca sirī tato hirī {note:sirī hirī tato (pī.)}, taṃ assamaṃ āgamu {note:āgamuṃ (sī. pī. ka.)} yattha kosiyo.

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
287\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
288\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hirī {pb:M:2.0113} uppalavaṇṇāsi, kosiyo dānapati bhikkhu;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
289\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sūriyo kassapo bhikkhu, moggallānosi candimā;
::

::gathalast
Nārado {pb:T:2.0106} sāriputtosi, sambuddho āsi vāsavo’’ti.
::

::centre
Sudhābhojanajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 536. Kuṇālajātakaṃ (4)

Evamakkhāyati, evamanusūyati {note:suyyati (ka.)}. Sabbosadhadharaṇidhare nekapupphamālyavitate gaja-gavaja mahiṃsa-ruru-camara-pasada-khagga-gokaṇṇa-sīha-byaggha-dīpi-accha-koka-taraccha-uddāra-kadalimiga- biḷāra-sasa-kaṇṇikānucariteākiṇṇanelamaṇḍalamahāvarāhanāgakulakareṇu {note:kaṇeru (sī. pī.)} -saṅghādhivuṭṭhe {note:vutthe (sī. pī.)} issamiga- sākhamiga-sarabhamiga-eṇīmiga-vātamiga-pasadamiga-purisālu {note:purisallu (sī. pī.)} -kimpurisa-yakkha-rakkhasanisevite amajjavamañjarīdhara-pahaṭṭha {note:brahaṭṭha (sī. pī.)} -pupphaphusitaggā {note:pupphitagga (sī. pī.)} nekapādapagaṇavitatekurara-cakora-vāraṇa-mayūra-parabhata- jīvañjīvaka-celāvakā-bhiṅkāra-karavīkamattavihaṅgagaṇa-satata {note:vihaṅgasata (sī. pī.)} sampaghuṭṭheañjana-manosilā-haritāla- hiṅgulakahema-rajatakanakānekadhātusatavinaddhapaṭimaṇḍitappadese {pb:V:2.0080} evarūpe khalu, bho, ramme vanasaṇḍe **kuṇālo** nāma sakuṇo paṭivasati ativiya citto ativiya cittapattacchadano.

Tasseva khalu, bho, kuṇālassa sakuṇassa aḍḍhuḍḍhāni itthisahassāni paricārikā dijakaññāyo. Atha khalu, bho, dve dijakaññāyo kaṭṭhaṃ mukhena ḍaṃsitvā {note:ḍasitvā (sī. pī.) evamuparipi} taṃ kuṇālaṃ sakuṇaṃ majjhe nisīdāpetvā uḍḍenti {note:ḍenti (sī. pī.) evamuparipi} – ‘‘mā naṃ kuṇālaṃ sakuṇaṃ addhānapariyāyapathe kilamatho ubbāhetthā’’ti {note:ubbāhethāti (syā. ka.)}.

Pañcasatā {note:pañcasata (pī.)} dijakaññāyo heṭṭhato heṭṭhato uḍḍenti – {note:ḍenti (sī. pī.) evamuparipi} ‘‘sacāyaṃ kuṇālo {pb:T:2.0107} sakuṇo āsanā paripatissati, mayaṃ taṃ pakkhehi paṭiggahessāmāti.

Pañcasatā dijakaññāyo uparūpari uḍḍenti – {note:ḍenti (sī. pī.) evamuparipi} ‘‘mā naṃ kuṇālaṃ sakuṇaṃ ātapo paritāpesī’’ti {note:parikāpīti (sī. pī.)}.

Pañcasatā {pb:M:2.0114} pañcasatā {note:sī. pī. potthakesu ‘‘pañcasatā’’ti sakideva āgataṃ} dijakaññāyo ubhatopassena uḍḍenti – {note:ḍenti (sī. pī.) evamuparipi} ‘‘mā naṃ kuṇālaṃ sakuṇaṃ sītaṃ vā uṇhaṃ vā tiṇaṃ vā rajo vā vāto vā ussāvo vā upapphusī’’ti.

Pañcasatā dijakaññāyo purato purato uḍḍenti – ‘‘mā naṃ kuṇālaṃ sakuṇaṃ gopālakā vā pasupālakā vā tiṇahārakā vā kaṭṭhahārakā vā vanakammikā vā kaṭṭhena vā kaṭhalena vā {note:kathalāya vā (ka.)} pāṇinā vā ( ) {note:(pāsāṇena vā) (syā.)} leḍḍunā vā daṇḍena vā satthena vā sakkharāhi vā {note:sakkharāya vā (sī.)} pahāraṃ adaṃsu. Māyaṃ kuṇālo sakuṇo gacchehi vā latāhi vā rukkhehi vā sākhāhi vā {note:idaṃ padadvayaṃ sī. pī. potthakesu natthi} thambhehi vā pāsāṇehi vā balavantehi vā pakkhīhi saṅgamesī’’ti {note:saṅgāmesīti (sī. pī.)}.

Pañcasatā dijakaññāyo pacchato pacchato uḍḍenti saṇhāhi sakhilāhi mañjūhi madhurāhi vācāhi samudācarantiyo – ‘‘māyaṃ kuṇālo sakuṇo āsane pariyukkaṇṭhī’’ti.

Pañcasatā dijakaññāyo disodisaṃ uḍḍenti anekarukkhavividhavikatiphalamāharantiyo – ‘‘māyaṃ kuṇālo sakuṇo khudāya parikilamitthā’’ti.

Atha khalu, bho, tā {note:natthi sī. pī. potthakesu} dijakaññāyo taṃ kuṇālaṃ sakuṇaṃ ārāmeneva ārāmaṃ uyyāneneva uyyānaṃ {pb:V:2.0081} nadītittheneva nadītitthaṃ pabbatasikhareneva pabbatasikharaṃ ambavaneneva ambavanaṃ jambuvaneneva jambuvanaṃ labujavaneneva labujavanaṃ nāḷikerasañcāriyeneva {note:sañjādiyeneva (pī.)} nāḷikerasañcāriyaṃ khippameva abhisambhonti {pb:T:2.0108} ratitthāya {note:ratatthāya (sī. pī.)}.

Atha khalu, bho, kuṇālo sakuṇo tāhi dijakaññāhi divasaṃ paribyūḷho evaṃ apasādeti – ‘‘nassatha tumhe vasaliyo, vinassatha tumhe vasaliyo, coriyo dhuttiyo asatiyo lahucittāyo katassa appaṭikārikāyo anilo viya yenakāmaṃgamāyo’’ti.

Tasseva khalu, bho, himavato pabbatarājassa puratthimadisābhāge susukhumasunipuṇagirippabhava {note:ppabhavā (sī. pī.)} – haritupayantiyo.

Uppala {pb:M:2.0115} paduma kumuda naḷina satapatta sogandhika mandālaka {note:mandālava (sī. pī.), mandārava (ka.)} sampativirūḷhasucigandha manuññamāvakappadese {note:pāvakappadese (sī. pī.)}.

Kuravaka-mucalinda-ketaka-vedisa-vañjula {note:vetasamañjula (sī.)} -punnāgabakula-tilaka-piyaka-hasanasāla-saḷalacampaka asoka-nāgarukkha-tirīṭi-bhujapatta-lodda-candanoghavanekāḷāgaru-padmaka-piyaṅgu-devadārukacocagahane kakudhakuṭajaaṅkola-kaccikāra {note:kacchikāra (ka.)} -kaṇikāra-kaṇṇikāra-kanavera-koraṇḍaka-koviḷāra-kiṃsuka-yodhika vanamallika {note:navamallika (sī. pī.)} -manaṅgaṇa-manavajja-bhaṇḍi-surucira-bhaginimālāmalyadhare jātisumanamadhugandhika- {note:madhukabandhuka (ka.)} dhanutakkāri {note:dhanukāri (sī.), dhanukārika (pī.)} tālīsa-tagaramusīrakoṭṭha-kacchavitate atimuttakasaṃkusumitalatāvitatapaṭimaṇḍitappadese haṃsa-pilava-kādamba-kāraṇḍavābhinadite vijjādhara-siddha {note:sindhava (sī. pī.)} -samaṇa-tāpasagaṇādhivuṭṭhe varadeva-yakkha-rakkhasa-dānava-gandhabba-kinnaramahoragānuciṇṇappadese evarūpe khalu, bho, ramme vanasaṇḍe **puṇṇamukho** nāma phussakokilo paṭivasati ativiya madhuragiro vilāsitanayano mattakkho {note:savilāsitanayanamattakkho (ka.)}.

Tasseva khalu, bho, puṇṇamukhassa phussakokilassa aḍḍhuḍḍhāni itthisatāni paricārikā dijakaññāyo. Atha khalu, bho, dve dijakaññāyo kaṭṭhaṃ mukhena ḍaṃsitvā taṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ majjhe nisīdāpetvā uḍḍenti {pb:T:2.0109} – ‘‘mā naṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ addhānapariyāyapathe kilamatho ubbāhetthā’’ti.

Paññāsa {pb:V:2.0082} dijakaññāyo heṭṭhato heṭṭhato uḍḍenti – ‘‘sacāyaṃ puṇṇamukho phussakokilo āsanā paripatissati, mayaṃ taṃ pakkhehi paṭiggahessāmā’’ti.

Paññāsa dijakaññāyo uparūpari uḍḍenti – ‘‘mā naṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ ātapo paritāpesī’’ti.

Paññāsa paññāsa dijakaññāyo ubhatopassena uḍḍenti – ‘‘mā naṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ sītaṃ vā uṇhaṃ vā tiṇaṃ vā rajo vā vāto vā ussāvo vā upapphusī’’ti.

Paññāsa {pb:M:2.0116} dijakaññāyo purato purato uḍḍenti – ‘‘mā naṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ gopālakā vā pasupālakā vā tiṇahārakā vā kaṭṭhahārakā vā vanakammikā vā kaṭṭhena vā kathalāya vā pāṇinā vā leḍḍunā vā daṇḍena vā satthena vā sakkharāhi vā pahāraṃ adaṃsu. Māyaṃ puṇṇamukho phussakokilo gacchehi vā latāhi vā rukkhehi vā sākhāhi vā thambhehi vā pāsāṇehi vā balavantehi vā pakkhīhi saṅgāmesī’’ti.

Paññāsa dijakaññāyo pacchato pacchato uḍḍenti saṇhāhi sakhilāhi mañjūhi madhurāhi vācāhi samudācarantiyo – ‘‘māyaṃ puṇṇamukho phussakokilo āsane pariyukkaṇṭhī’’ti.

Paññāsa dijakaññāyo disodisaṃ uḍḍenti anekarukkhavividhavikatiphalamāharantiyo – ‘‘māyaṃ puṇṇamukho phussakokilo khudāya parikilamitthā’’ti.

Atha khalu, bho, tā dijakaññāyo taṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ {pb:T:2.0110} ārāmeneva ārāmaṃ uyyāneneva uyyānaṃ nadītittheneva nadītitthaṃ pabbatasikhareneva pabbatasikharaṃ ambavaneneva ambavanaṃ jambuvaneneva jambuvanaṃ labujavaneneva labujavanaṃ nāḷikerasañcāriyeneva nāḷikerasañcāriyaṃ khippameva abhisambhonti ratitthāya.

Atha khalu, bho, puṇṇamukho phussakokilo tāhi dijakaññāhi divasaṃ paribyūḷho evaṃ pasaṃsati – ‘‘sādhu, sādhu, bhaginiyo, etaṃ kho, bhaginiyo, tumhākaṃ patirūpaṃ kuladhītānaṃ, yaṃ tumhe bhattāraṃ paricareyyāthā’’ti.

Atha {pb:V:2.0083} khalu, bho, puṇṇamukho phussakokilo yena kuṇālo sakuṇo tenupasaṅkami. Addasaṃsu kho kuṇālassa sakuṇassa paricārikā dijakaññāyo taṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ dūratova āgacchantaṃ; disvāna yena puṇṇamukho phussakokilo tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā taṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘ayaṃ, samma puṇṇamukha, kuṇālo sakuṇo ativiya pharuso ativiya pharusavāco, appevanāma tavampi āgamma piyavācaṃ labheyyāmā’’ti. ‘‘Appevanāma, bhaginiyo’’ti vatvā yena kuṇālo sakuṇo tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā kuṇālena {pb:M:2.0117} sakuṇena saddhiṃ paṭisammoditvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho puṇṇamukho phussakokilo taṃ kuṇālaṃ sakuṇaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kissa tvaṃ, samma kuṇāla, itthīnaṃ sujātānaṃ kuladhītānaṃ sammāpaṭipannānaṃ micchāpaṭipanno’si {note:paṭipanno (sī. pī.)}? Amanāpabhāṇīnampi kira, samma kuṇāla, itthīnaṃ manāpabhāṇinā bhavitabbaṃ, kimaṅga pana manāpabhāṇīna’’nti!

Evaṃ vutte, kuṇālo sakuṇo taṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ evaṃ apasādesi – ‘‘nassa tvaṃ, samma jamma vasala, vinassa tvaṃ, samma jamma vasala, ko nu tayā viyatto jāyājinenā’’ti. Evaṃ apasādito ca pana puṇṇamukho phussakokilo tatoyeva {note:tato heva (sī. pī.)} paṭinivatti.

Atha khalu, bho, puṇṇamukhassa phussakokilassa aparena samayena nacirasseva {note:acirasseva accayena (ka.)} kharo ābādho uppajji lohitapakkhandikā. Bāḷhā vedanā vattanti māraṇantikā {note:maraṇantikā (syā.)}. Atha khalu, bho, puṇṇamukhassa phussakokilassa paricārikānaṃ dijakaññānaṃ etadahosi – ‘‘ābādhiko kho ayaṃ puṇṇamukho phussakokilo, appevanāma imamhā ābādhā vuṭṭhaheyyā’’ti ekaṃ adutiyaṃ ohāya yena kuṇālo sakuṇo tenupasaṅkamiṃsu. Addasā kho kuṇālo sakuṇo tā dijakaññāyo dūratova āgacchantiyo, disvāna tā dijakaññāyo etadavoca – ‘‘kahaṃ pana tumhaṃ vasaliyo bhattā’’ti? ‘‘Ābādhiko kho, samma kuṇāla, puṇṇamukho phussakokilo appevanāma tamhā ābādhā vuṭṭhaheyyā’’ti. Evaṃ vutte, kuṇālo sakuṇo tā dijakaññāyo evaṃ apasādesi – ‘‘nassatha tumhe vasaliyo, vinassatha tumhe vasaliyo, coriyo dhuttiyo asatiyo lahucittāyo katassa appaṭikārikāyo anilo viya yenakāmaṃgamāyo’’ti; vatvā yena puṇṇamukho phussakokilo tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā taṃ {pb:T:2.0112} puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘haṃ, samma, puṇṇamukhā’’ti. ‘‘Haṃ, samma, kuṇālā’’ti.

Atha khalu, bho kuṇālo sakuṇo taṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ phussakokilaṃ pakkhehi ca mukhatuṇḍakena {pb:V:2.0084} ca pariggahetvā vuṭṭhāpetvā nānābhesajjāni pāyāpesi. Atha khalu, bho, puṇṇamukhassa phussakokilassa so ābādho paṭippassambhīti. Atha khalu, bho, kuṇālo sakuṇo taṃ puṇṇamukhaṃ {pb:M:2.0118} phussakokilaṃ gilānavuṭṭhitaṃ {note:gilānāvuṭṭhitaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} aciravuṭṭhitaṃ gelaññā etadavoca –

‘‘Diṭṭhā mayā, samma puṇṇamukha, kaṇhā dvepitikā pañcapatikāya chaṭṭhe purise cittaṃ paṭibandhantiyā, yadidaṃ kabandhe {note:kavandhe (sī. pī.)} pīṭhasappimhīti. Bhavati ca panuttarettha {note:punuttacettha (ka.) evamuparipi} vākyaṃ –

::hangnum
290\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athajjuno nakulo bhīmaseno {note:bhimmaseno (sī. syā. pī.)}, yudhiṭṭhilo sahadevo {note:sīhadevo (ka.)} ca rājā;
::

::gathalast
Ete patī pañca matticca nārī, akāsi khujjavāmanakena {note:khujjavāmanena (pī.)} pāpa’’nti.
::

‘‘Diṭṭhā mayā, samma puṇṇamukha, saccatapāpī {note:saccatapāvī (sī. pī.), pañcatapāvī (syā.)} nāma samaṇī susānamajjhe vasantī catutthabhattaṃ pariṇāmayamānā surādhuttakena {note:tulāputtakena (sī. pī.), sā surādhuttakena (ka.)} pāpamakāsi.

‘‘Diṭṭhā mayā, samma puṇṇamukha, kākavatī {note:kākātī (sī.), kākāti (pī.)} nāma devī samuddamajjhe vasantī bhariyā venateyyassa naṭakuverena pāpamakāsi.

Diṭṭhā mayā, samma puṇṇamukha, kuruṅgadevī {note:kuraṅgavī (sī. pī.)} nāma lomasuddarī {note:lomasundarī (sī. syā. pī.)} eḷikakumāraṃ {note:eḷamārakaṃ (sī.), eḷakakumāraṃ (syā.), eḷakamāraṃ (pī.)} kāmayamānā chaḷaṅgakumāradhanantevāsinā pāpamakāsi.

Evañhetaṃ {pb:T:2.0113} mayā ñātaṃ, brahmadattassa mātaraṃ {note:mātukā (syā.)} ohāya kosalarājaṃ pañcālacaṇḍena pāpamakāsi.

::hangnum
291\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etā ca aññā ca akaṃsu pāpaṃ, tasmāhamitthīnaṃ na vissase nappasaṃse;
::

::gatha2
Mahī yathā jagati samānarattā, vasundharā itarītarāpatiṭṭhā {note:itarītarānaṃ patiṭṭhā (syā.), ittarītarappatiṭṭhā (?)};
::

::gathalast
Sabbasahā aphandanā akuppā, tathitthiyo tāyo na vissase naro.
::

::hangnum
292\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīho {pb:M:2.0119} yathā lohitamaṃsabhojano, vāḷamigo pañcāvudho {note:pañcahattho (sī. pī.)} suruddho;
::

::gathalast
Pasayhakhādī parahiṃsane rato, tathitthiyo tāyo na vissase naro.
::

‘‘Na khalu {note:na khalu bho (syā. ka.)}, samma puṇṇamukha, vesiyo nāriyo gamaniyo, na hetā bandhakiyo nāma, vadhikāyo nāma etāyo, yadidaṃ vesiyo nāriyo gamaniyo’’ti.

‘‘Coro {pb:V:2.0085} {note:corā (sī. syā. pī.)} viya veṇikatā, madirāva {note:madirā viya (sī. syā.), madiriva (pī.)} diddhā {note:diṭṭhā (ka.), visaduṭṭhā (syā.)} vāṇijo {note:vāṇijā (pī.)} viya vācāsanthutiyo, issasiṅghamiva viparivattāyo {note:parivattāyo (pī.), viparivattāro (ka.)}, uragāmiva dujivhāyo, sobbhamiva paṭicchannā, pātālamiva duppūrā rakkhasī viya duttosā, yamovekantahāriyo, sikhīriva sabbabhakkhā, nadīriva sabbavāhī, anilo viya yenakāmaṃcarā, neru viya avisesakarā, visarukkho viya niccaphalitāyo’’ti. Bhavati ca panuttarettha vākyaṃ –

::hangnum
293\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā {pb:T:2.0114} coro yathā diddho, vāṇijova vikatthanī;
::

::gathalast
Issasiṅghamiva parivattā {note:mivāvaṭṭo (sī.), mivāvattā (pī.)}, dujivhā {note:dujjivha (pī.)} urago viya.
::

::hangnum
294\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sobbhamiva paṭicchannā, pātālamiva duppurā;
::

::gathalast
Rakkhasī viya duttosā, yamovekantahāriyo.
::

::hangnum
295\.
::

::gatha1
{note:yathā sikhī nadīvāho, anilo kāmacāravā;§nerūva avisesā ca, visarukkho viya niccaphalā;§nāsayanti ghare bhogaṃ, ratanānantakaritthi yoti; (sī. syā.)}
::

‘‘Yathā sikhī nadī vāto, nerunāva samāgatā.

::gatha2
Visarukkho viya niccaphalā, nāsayanti ghare bhogaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ratanantakaritthiyo’’ti {note:yathā sikhī nadīvāho, anilo kāmacāravā;§nerūva avisesā ca, visarukkho viya niccaphalā;§nāsayanti ghare bhogaṃ, ratanānantakaritthi yoti; (sī. syā.)}.
::

‘‘Cattārimāni, samma puṇṇamukha, yāni (vatthūni kicce jāte anatthacarāni bhavanti; tāni) {note:( ) sī. syā. potthakesu na dissati} parakule na vāsetabbāni – goṇaṃ dhenuṃ yānaṃ bhariyā. Cattāri etāni paṇḍito dhanāni {note:yāni (sī. syā. pī.)} gharā na vippavāsaye.

::hangnum
296\.
::

::gatha1
‘Goṇaṃ {pb:M:2.0120} dhenuñca yānañca, bhariyaṃ ñātikule na vāsaye;
::

::gatha2
Bhañjanti rathaṃ ayānakā, ativāhena hananti puṅgavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dohena hananti vacchakaṃ, bhariyā ñātikule padussatī’’’ti.
::

‘‘Cha imāni, samma puṇṇamukha, yāni (vatthūni) {note:( ) sī. pī. potthakesu nu dissati} kicce jāte anatthacarāni bhavanti –

::hangnum
297\.
::

::gatha1
‘Aguṇaṃ dhanu ñātikule ca bhariyā, pāraṃ nāvā akkhabhaggañca yānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dūre {pb:T:2.0115} mitto pāpasahāyako ca, kicce jāte anatthacarāni bhava’’’nti.
::

‘‘Aṭṭhahi khalu, samma puṇṇamukha, ṭhānehi itthī sāmikaṃ avajānāti. Daliddatā, āturatā, jiṇṇatā, surāsoṇḍatā, muddhatā, pamattatā, sabbakiccesu anuvattanatā, sabbadhanaanuppadānena {pb:V:2.0086} – imehi khalu, samma puṇṇamukha, aṭṭhahi ṭhānehi itthī sāmikaṃ avajānāti. Bhavati ca panuttarettha vākyaṃ –

::hangnum
298\.
::

::gatha1
‘Daliddaṃ āturañcāpi, jiṇṇakaṃ surasoṇḍakaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Pamattaṃ muddhapattañca, sabbakiccesu {note:rattaṃ kiccesu (sī. pī.)} hāpanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbakāmappadānena {note:sabbakāmapaṇidhānena (syā)}, avajānāti {note:avajānanti (sī. pī.)} sāmika’’’nti.
::

‘‘Navahi khalu, samma puṇṇamukha, ṭhānehi itthī padosamāharati. Ārāmagamanasīlā ca hoti, uyyānagamanasīlā ca hoti, nadītitthagamanasīlā ca hoti, ñātikulagamanasīlā ca hoti, parakulagamanasīlā ca hoti, ādāsadussamaṇḍanānuyogamanuyuttasīlā ca hoti, majjapāyinī ca hoti, nillokanasīlā ca hoti, sadvāraṭhāyinī {note:padvāraṭṭhāyinī (sī. syā. pī.)} ca hoti – imehi khalu, samma puṇṇamukha, navahi ṭhānehi itthī padosamāharatīti. Bhavati ca panuttarettha vākyaṃ –

::hangnum
299\.
::

::gatha1
‘Ārāmasīlā ca {note:ārāmasīlā (sī. pī.)} uyyānaṃ, nadī ñāti parakulaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ādāsadussamaṇḍanamanuyuttā, yā {pb:T:2.0116} citthī majjapāyinī.
::

::hangnum
300\.
::

::gatha1
‘Yā {pb:M:2.0121} ca nillokanasīlā, yā ca sadvāraṭhāyinī;
::

::gathalast
Navahetehi ṭhānehi, padosamāharanti itthiyo’’’ti.
::

‘‘Cattālīsāya {note:cattālīsāyi (pī. ka.)} khalu, samma puṇṇamukha, ṭhānehi itthī purisaṃ accācarati {note:accāvadati (sī. syā. pī.)}. Vijambhati, vinamati, vilasati, vilajjati, nakhena nakhaṃ ghaṭṭeti, pādena pādaṃ akkamati, kaṭṭhena pathaviṃ vilikhati {note:likhati (sī. pī.)}, dārakaṃ ullaṅghati ullaṅghāpeti {note:dārakaṃ ullaṅgheti olaṅgheti (sī. pī.)}, kīḷati kīḷāpeti, cumbati cumbāpeti, bhuñjati bhuñjāpeti, dadāti, yācati, katamanukaroti, uccaṃ bhāsati, nīcaṃ bhāsati, aviccaṃ bhāsati, viviccaṃ bhāsati, naccena gītena vāditena rodanena {note:roditena (sī. pī.)} vilasitena vibhūsitena jagghati, pekkhati, kaṭiṃ cāleti, guyhabhaṇḍakaṃ sañcāleti, ūruṃ vivarati, ūruṃ pidahati, thanaṃ dasseti, kacchaṃ dasseti, nābhiṃ dasseti, akkhiṃ nikhanati, bhamukaṃ ukkhipati, oṭṭhaṃ upalikhati {note:oṭṭhaṃ palikhati jivhaṃ palikhati (sī. pī.)}, jivhaṃ nillāleti, dussaṃ muñcati, dussaṃ paṭibandhati, sirasaṃ muñcati, sirasaṃ bandhati – imehi khalu, samma puṇṇamukha, cattālīsāya ṭhānehi itthī purisaṃ accācarati.

‘‘Pañcavīsāya {note:pañcavīsāhi (pī. ka.)} khalu, samma puṇṇamukha, ṭhānehi itthī paduṭṭhā veditabbā bhavati. Sāmikassa pavāsaṃ vaṇṇeti, pavuṭṭhaṃ na {pb:T:2.0117} sarati, āgataṃ nābhinandati, avaṇṇaṃ tassa bhaṇati, vaṇṇaṃ {pb:V:2.0087} tassa na bhaṇati, anatthaṃ tassa carati, atthaṃ tassa na carati, akiccaṃ tassa karoti, kiccaṃ tassa na karoti, paridahitvā sayati, parammukhī nipajjati, parivattakajātā kho pana hoti kuṅkumiyajātā, dīghaṃ assasati, dukkhaṃ vedayati, uccārapassāvaṃ abhiṇhaṃ gacchati, vilomamācarati, parapurisasaddaṃ sutvā kaṇṇasotaṃ vivaramodahati {note:vivarati kamodahati (pī.)}, nihatabhogā kho pana hoti, paṭivissakehi santhavaṃ karoti, nikkhantapādā kho pana hoti, visikhānucārinī aticārinī kho pana hoti, niccaṃ {note:natthi sī. syā. pī. potthakesu} sāmike agāravā paduṭṭhamanasaṅkappā, abhiṇhaṃ dvāre tiṭṭhati, kacchāni aṅgāni thanāni dasseti, disodisaṃ gantvā pekkhati – imehi khalu, samma puṇṇamukha, pañcavīsāya {note:pañcavīsāhi (ka.)} ṭhānehi itthī paduṭṭhā veditabbā bhavati. Bhavati ca panuttarettha vākyaṃ –

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Tā gilanti purisassa pābhataṃ, sāgareva makaraṃ timiṅgalo {note:timiṅgilo (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
354\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcakāmaguṇasātagocarā, uddhatā aniyatā asaññatā;
::

::gathalast
Osaranti pamadā pamādinaṃ, loṇatoyavatiyaṃva āpakā.
::

::hangnum
355\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ naraṃ upalapenti {note:uparamanti (sī. pī.), palāpenti (ka.)} nāriyo, chandasā va {pb:T:2.0127} ratiyā dhanena vā;
::

::gathalast
Jātavedasadisampi tādisaṃ, rāgadosavadhiyo {note:rāgadosavatiyo (sī. pī.)} dahanti naṃ.
::

::hangnum
356\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aḍḍhaṃ ñatvā purisaṃ mahaddhanaṃ, osaranti sadhanā sahattanā;
::

::gathalast
Rattacittamativeṭhayanti naṃ, sāla māluvalatāva kānane.
::

::hangnum
357\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tā upenti vividhena chandasā, citrabimbamukhiyo alaṅkatā;
::

::gathalast
Uhasanti {note:ūhasanti (sī. pī.), ohasanti (syā.)} pahasanti nāriyo, sambarova {note:saṃvarova (syā. pī. ka.)} satamāyakovidā.
::

::hangnum
358\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātarūpamaṇimuttabhūsitā, sakkatā patikulesu nāriyo;
::

::gathalast
Rakkhitā aticaranti sāmikaṃ, dānavaṃva hadayantarassitā {note:hadayantanissitā (ka.), hadayantaranissitā (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
359\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tejavāpi {pb:M:2.0130} hi naro vicakkhaṇo, sakkato bahujanassa pūjito;
::

::gathalast
Nārinaṃ vasagato na bhāsati, rāhunā upahatova candimā.
::

::hangnum
360\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kareyya kupito diso disaṃ, duṭṭhacitto {pb:T:2.0128} vasamāgataṃ ariṃ {note:ari (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tena bhiyyo byasanaṃ nigacchati, nārinaṃ vasagato apekkhavā.
::

::hangnum
361\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kesalūnanakhachinnatajjitā, pādapāṇikasadaṇḍatāḷitā;
::

::gathalast
Hīnamevupagatā hi nāriyo, tā ramanti kuṇapeva makkhikā.
::

::hangnum
362\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tā kulesu visikhantaresu vā, rājadhāninigamesu vā puna {note:vā pana (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Oḍḍitaṃ namucipāsavākaraṃ {note:vāguraṃ (syā.)}, cakkhumā parivajje sukhatthiko.
::

::hangnum
363\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ossajitva {pb:V:2.0092} kusalaṃ tapoguṇaṃ, yo anariyacaritāni mācari;
::

::gathalast
Devatāhi nirayaṃ nimissati, chedagāmimaṇiyaṃva vāṇijo.
::

::hangnum
364\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So idha garahito parattha ca, dummatī upahato {note:upagato (sī. pī.)} sakammunā;
::

Gacchatī aniyato gaḷāgaḷaṃ, duṭṭhagadrabharathova uppathe.

::hangnum
365\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So upeti nirayaṃ patāpanaṃ, sattisimbalivanañca {pb:T:2.0129} āyasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āvasitvā tiracchānayoniyaṃ, petarājavisayaṃ na muñcati {note:muccati (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
366\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dibyakhiḍḍaratiyoṃ {pb:M:2.0131} ca nandane, cakkavatticaritañca mānuse;
::

::gathalast
Nāsayanti pamadā pamādinaṃ, duggatiñca paṭipādayanti naṃ.
::

::hangnum
367\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dibyakhiḍḍaratiyo na dullabhā, cakkavatticaritañca mānuse;
::

::gathalast
Soṇṇabyamhanilayā {note:suvaṇṇabyamhanilayā (syā. ka.), sovaṇṇabyamhanilayā (pī.)} ca accharā, ye caranti pamadāhanatthikā.
::

::hangnum
368\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāmadhātusamatikkamā gati, rūpadhātuyā bhāvo {note:rūpadhātuyā bhavo (sī.), rūpadhātusambhavo (syā.)} na dullabho;
::

::gathalast
Vītarāgavisayūpapattiyā, ye caranti pamadāhanatthikā.
::

::hangnum
369\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbadukkhasamatikkamaṃ sivaṃ, accantamacalitaṃ asaṅkhataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nibbutehi sucihī na dullabhaṃ, ye caranti pamadāhanatthikā’’ti.
::

::hangnum
370\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuṇālohaṃ tadā āsiṃ, udāyī phussakokilo;
::

::gatha2
Ānando {pb:T:2.0130} gijjharājāsi, sāriputto ca nārado;
::

::gathalast
Parisā buddhaparisā, evaṃ dhāretha jātaka’’nti.
::

::centre
Kuṇālajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 537. Mahāsutasomajātakaṃ (5)

::hangnum
371\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kasmā tuvaṃ rasaka edisāni, karosi kammāni sudāruṇāni;
::

::gathalast
Hanāsi itthī purise ca mūḷho, maṃsassa hetu adu {note:ādu (sī. syā.)} dhanassa kāraṇā’’.
::

::hangnum
372\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Naṃ {pb:M:2.0132} attahetū na dhanassa kāraṇā, na puttadārassa sahāyañātinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhattā ca me bhagavā bhūmipālo, so khādati maṃsaṃ bhadantedisaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
373\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace tuvaṃ bhatturatthe payutto, karosi kammāni sudāruṇāni;
::

::gathalast
Pātova antepuraṃ pāpuṇitvā, lapeyyāsi me rājino sammukhe taṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
374\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tathā karissāmi ahaṃ bhadante, yathā tuvaṃ {note:yameva tvaṃ (sī.)} bhāsasi kāḷahatthi;
::

::gathalast
Pātova antepuraṃ pāpuṇitvā, vakkhāmi {pb:T:2.0131} te rājino sammukhe taṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
375\.
::

::gatha1
Tato {pb:V:2.0093} ratyā vivasāne {note:vivasane (sī. syā. pī.)}, sūriyuggamanaṃ pati;
::

::gatha2
Kāḷo rasakamādāya, rājānaṃ upasaṅkami;
::

::gathalast
Upasaṅkamma {note:upasaṅkamitvā (sī. syā. pī.)} rājānaṃ, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
376\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saccaṃ kira mahārāja, rasako pesito tayā;
::

::gathalast
Hanati itthipurise, tuvaṃ maṃsāni khādasi’’.
::

::hangnum
377\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evameva tathā kāḷa, rasako pesito mayā;
::

::gathalast
Mama atthaṃ karontassa, kimetaṃ paribhāsasi’’.
::

::hangnum
378\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ānando sabbamacchānaṃ, khāditvā rasagiddhimā;
::

::gathalast
Parikkhīṇāya parisāya, attānaṃ khādiyā mato.
::

::hangnum
379\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ pamatto rasagārave ratto {note:rato (sī. syā. pī.)}, bālo yadī āyati nāvabujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Vidhamma putte caji {note:cajitvā (ka.)} ñātake ca, parivattiya attānaññeva {note:attānameva (sī. pī.)} khādati.
::

::hangnum
380\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:M:2.0133} te sutvāna vigetu {note:vihetu (sī. pī.)} chando, mā bhakkhayī {note:mā bhakkhasī (sī. pī.)} rāja manussamaṃsaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mā tvaṃ imaṃ kevalaṃ vārijova, dvipadādhipa {note:dipadādipa (sī. pī.) evamuparipi} suññamakāsi raṭṭhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
381\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sujāto nāma nāmena, oraso tassa atrajo {note:tassa orasa atrajo (sī.), tassa atraja oraso (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Jambupesimaladdhāna, mato so tassa saṅkhaye.
::

::hangnum
382\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evameva {pb:T:2.0132} ahaṃ kāḷa, bhutvā bhakkhaṃ rasuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aladdhā mānusaṃ maṃsaṃ, maññe hissāmi {note:hessāmi (sī. syā.), hassāmi (pī.)} jīvitaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
383\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Māṇava abhirūposi, kule jātosi sotthiye;
::

::gathalast
Na tvaṃ arahasi tāta, abhakkhaṃ bhakkhayetave’’.
::

::hangnum
384\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rasānaṃ aññataraṃ etaṃ, kasmā {note:yasmā (sī. pī.)} maṃ tvaṃ nivāraye;
::

::gathalast
Sohaṃ tattha gamissāmi, yattha lacchāmi edisaṃ.
::

::hangnum
385\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sovāhaṃ nippatissāmi, na te vacchāmi santike;
::

::gathalast
Yassa me dassanena tvaṃ, nābhinandasi brāhmaṇa’’.
::

::hangnum
386\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā aññepi dāyāde, putte lacchāma māṇava;
::

::gathalast
Tvañca jamma vinassassu, yattha pattaṃ na taṃ suṇe’’.
::

::hangnum
387\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evameva tuvaṃ rāja, dvipadinda suṇohi me;
::

::gathalast
Pabbājessanti taṃ raṭṭhā, soṇḍaṃ māṇavakaṃ yathā’’.
::

::hangnum
388\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sujāto nāma nāmena, bhāvitattāna sāvako;
::

::gathalast
Accharaṃ kāmayantova, na so bhuñji na so pivi.
::

::hangnum
389\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusaggenudakamādāya {pb:V:2.0094} {note:kusagge udakamādāya (sī. pī.)}, samudde udakaṃ mine;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ mānusakā kāmā, dibbakāmāna santike.
::

::hangnum
390\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evameva ahaṃ kāḷa, bhutvā bhakkhaṃ rasuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aladdhā mānusaṃ maṃsaṃ, maññe hissāmi jīvitaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
391\.

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāpi {pb:M:2.0134} te dhataraṭṭhā, haṃsā vehāyasaṅgamā;
::

::gathalast
Abhuttaparibhogena {note:avuttiparibhogena (sī. pī.), ayuttaparibhogena (syā.)}, sabbe abbhatthataṃ gatā.
::

::hangnum
392\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evameva {pb:T:2.0133} tuvaṃ rāja, dvipadinda suṇohi me;
::

::gathalast
Abhakkhaṃ rāja bhakkhesi, tasmā pabbājayanti taṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
393\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tiṭṭhāhīti mayā vutto, so tvaṃ gacchasi pammukho {note:pāmukho (ka.)};
::

::gatha2
Aṭṭhito tvaṃ ṭhitomhīti, lapasi brahmacārini;
::

::gathalast
Idaṃ te samaṇāyuttaṃ, asiñca me maññasi kaṅkapattaṃ’’ {note:kaṅkhapattaṃ (syā. ka.)}.

::hangnum
394\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ṭhitohamasmī sadhammesu rāja, na nāmagottaṃ parivattayāmi;
::

::gathalast
Corañca loke aṭhitaṃ vadanti, āpāyikaṃ nerayikaṃ ito cutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
395\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace tvaṃ saddahasi {note:sacepi sahasi (sī. pī.)} rāja, sutaṃ gaṇhāhi khattiya {note:khattiyaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Tena yaññaṃ yajitvāna, evaṃ saggaṃ gamissasi’’.
::

::hangnum
396\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kismiṃ nu raṭṭhe tava jātibhūmi {note:jātabhūmi (sī.)}, atha kena atthena idhānupatto;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi me brāhmaṇa etamatthaṃ, kimicchasī demi tayajja patthitaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
397\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gāthā catasso dharaṇīmahissara, sugambhiratthā varasāgarūpamā;
::

::gathalast
Taveva atthāya idhāgatosmi, suṇohi gāthā paramatthasaṃhitā’’.
::

::hangnum
398\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na ve rudanti matimanto sapaññā, bahussutā {pb:T:2.0134} ye bahuṭṭhānacintino;
::

::gathalast
Dīpañhi etaṃ paramaṃ narānaṃ, yaṃ paṇḍitā sokanudā bhavanti.
::

::hangnum
399\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Attānaṃ {pb:M:2.0135} ñātī udāhu {note:uda (sī. pī.)} puttadāraṃ, dhaññaṃ dhanaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kimeva tvaṃ {note:kimo nu tvaṃ (sī. pī.)} sutasomānutappe, korabyaseṭṭha vacanaṃ suṇoma tetaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
400\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nevāhamattānamanutthunāmi, na puttadāraṃ na dhanaṃ na raṭṭhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Satañca dhammo carito purāṇo, taṃ saṅkaraṃ {note:saṅgaraṃ (sī. syā. pī.) evamuparipi} brāhmaṇassānutappe.
::

::hangnum
401\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kato mayā saṅkaro brāhmaṇena, raṭṭhe sake issariye ṭhitena;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ saṅkaraṃ brāhmaṇasappadāya, saccānurakkhī punarāvajissaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
402\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nevāhametaṃ abhisaddahāmi, sukhī naro maccumukhā pamutto;
::

::gathalast
Amittahatthaṃ punarāvajeyya, korabyaseṭṭha na hi maṃ upesi.
::

::hangnum
403\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mutto {pb:V:2.0095} tuvaṃ porisādassa hatthā, gantvā {pb:T:2.0135} sakaṃ mandiraṃ kāmakāmī;
::

::gathalast
Madhuraṃ piyaṃ jīvitaṃ laddha rāja, kuto tuvaṃ ehisi me sakāsaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
404\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mataṃ vareyya parisuddhasīlo, na jīvitaṃ {note:na hi jīvitaṃ (sī.)} garahito pāpadhammo;
::

::gathalast
Na hi taṃ naraṃ tāyati {note:tāyate (sī. syā. pī. ka.)} duggatīhi, yassāpi hetu alikaṃ bhaṇeyya.
::

::hangnum
405\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sacepi vāto girimāvaheyya, cando ca sūriyo ca chamā pateyyuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbā ca najjo paṭisotaṃ vajeyyuṃ, na tvevahaṃ rāja musā bhaṇeyyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
406\.
::

::gatha1
{note:ayaṃ gāthā sī. pī. potthakesu na dissati} ‘‘Nabhaṃ {pb:M:2.0136} phaleyya udadhīpi susse, saṃvaṭṭaye bhūtadharā vasundharā;
::

::gathalast
Siluccayo meru samūlamuppate, na tvevahaṃ rāja musā bhaṇeyyaṃ’’ {note:ayaṃ gāthā sī. pī. potthakesu na dissati}.

::gatha1

::gathalast

408\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
409\.

::gatha1
‘‘Yo me kato saṅkaro brāhmaṇena, raṭṭhe {pb:T:2.0136} sake issariye ṭhitena;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ saṅkaraṃ brāhmaṇasappadāya, saccānurakkhī punarāvajissaṃ’’.

::hangnum
410\.

::gatha1
‘‘Mutto ca so porisādassa hatthā, gantvāna taṃ brāhmaṇaṃ etadavoca;
::

::gathalast
Suṇoma {note:suṇomi (sī. syā.)} gāthāyo satārahāyo, yā me sutā assu hitāya brahme’’.

::hangnum
411\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakideva sutasoma, sabbhi hoti {note:hotu (pī.)} samāgamo;
::

::gathalast
Sā naṃ saṅgati pāleti, nāsabbhi bahusaṅgamo.
::

::hangnum
412\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbhireva samāsetha, sabbhi kubbetha santhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sataṃ saddhammamaññāya, seyyo hoti na pāpiyo.
::

::hangnum
413\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jīranti ve rājarathā sucittā, atho sarīrampi jaraṃ upeti;
::

::gathalast
Satañca dhammo na jaraṃ upeti, santo have sabbhi pavedayanti.
::

::hangnum
414\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nabhañcaṃ {pb:M:2.0137} dūre pathavī ca dūre, pāraṃ {pb:T:2.0137} samuddassa tadāhu dūre;
::

::gathalast
Tato have dūrataraṃ vadanti, satañca dhammo {note:dhammaṃ (sī. pī.)} asatañca rāja’’.
::

::hangnum
415\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassiyā {note:sahassiyo (sī. pī.)} imā gāthā, nahimā {note:na imā, (sī. pī.) nayimā (syā.)} gāthā satārahā;
::

::gathalast
Cattāri tvaṃ sahassāni, khippaṃ gaṇhāhi brāhmaṇa’’.
::

::hangnum
416\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āsītiyā nāvutiyā {note:asītiyā navutiyā (pī.)} ca gāthā, satārahā cāpi bhaveyya {note:bhaveyyu (sī. syā. pī.)} gāthā;
::

::gathalast
Paccattameva sutasoma jānahi, sahassiyā nāma kā atthi {note:sahassiyo nāma idhatthi (sī.)} gāthā’’.
::

::hangnum
417\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Icchāmi vohaṃ sutavuddhimattano, santoti maṃ {note:santo mamaṃ (syā.), santo ca maṃ (sī. pī. ka.)} sappurisā bhajeyyuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ savantīhi mahodadhīva, na hi tāta tappāmi subhāsitena.
::

::hangnum
418\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aggi {pb:V:2.0096} yathā tiṇakaṭṭhaṃ dahanto, na tappatī sāgarova {note:sāgaro vā (sī. pī.)} nadīhi;
::

::gathalast
Evampi te paṇḍitā rājaseṭṭha, sutvā na tappanti subhāsitena.
::

::hangnum
419\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakassa dāsassa yadā suṇomi, gāthaṃ ahaṃ atthavatiṃ {note:gāthā ahaṃ atthavatī (sī. pī.)} janinda;
::

::gathalast
Tameva sakkacca nisāmayāmi, na {pb:T:2.0138} hi tāta dhammesu mamatthi titti’’.
::

::hangnum
420\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:M:2.0138} te raṭṭhaṃ sadhanaṃ sayoggaṃ, sakāyuraṃ sabbakāmūpapannaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ kāmahetu paribhāsasimaṃ {note:bhāsase maṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, gacchāmahaṃ porisādassa ñatte’’ {note:porisādassa kante (sī. pī.), porisādassupante (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
421\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Attānurakkhāya bhavanti hete, hatthārohā rathikā pattikā ca;
::

::gathalast
Assāruhā {note:assārohā (syā. pī.)} ye ca dhanuggahāse, senaṃ payuñjāma hanāma sattuṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
422\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sudukkaraṃ porisādo akāsi, jīvaṃ gahetvāna avassajī maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ tādisaṃ pubbakiccaṃ saranto, dubbhe ahaṃ tassa kathaṃ janinda’’.
::

::hangnum
423\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vanditvā so pitaraṃ mātarañca, anusāsetvā negamañca balañca;
::

::gathalast
Saccavādī saccānurakkhamāno, agamāsi so yattha porisādo’’.
::

::hangnum
424\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kato mayā saṅkaro brāhmaṇena, raṭṭhe sake issariye ṭhitena;
::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast
Yajassu yaññaṃ khāda maṃ porisāda’’.
::

::hangnum
425\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hāyate khāditaṃ {note:khādituṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} mayhaṃ pacchā, citakā ayaṃ tāva sadhūmikāva {note:sadhūmakā ca (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Niddhūmake pacitaṃ sādhupakkaṃ, suṇoma {note:suṇomi (sī.), suṇāma (pī.)} gāthāyo satārahāyo’’.

::hangnum
426\.

::gathalast

::

::gathalast
Na sā bhariyā yā patino na vibheti, na te puttā {note:puttā na te (ka.)} ye na bharanti jiṇṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
492\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na sā sabhā yattha na santi santo, na te santo {note:santo na te (ka.)} ye na bhaṇanti dhammaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rāgañca dosañca pahāya mohaṃ, dhammaṃ bhaṇantāva bhavanti santo.
::

::hangnum
493\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nābhāsamānaṃ jānanti, missaṃ bālehi paṇḍitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhāsamānañca jānanti, desentaṃ amataṃ padaṃ.
::

::hangnum
494\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhāsaye {pb:T:2.0152} jotaye dhammaṃ, paggaṇhe isinaṃ dhajaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Subhāsitaddhajā isayo, dhammo hi isinaṃ dhajo’’ti.
::

::centre
Mahāsutasomajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

::centre
Asītinipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sumukho pana haṃsavaro ca mahā, sudhabhojaniko ca paro pavaro;
::

::gathalast
Sakuṇāladijādhipativhayano, sutasomavaruttamasavhayanoti.
::

### 22. Mahānipāto

#### 538. Mūgapakkhajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā {pb:T:2.0153}{pb:V:2.0102}{pb:M:2.0149} paṇḍiccayaṃ {note:paṇḍitiyaṃ (sī.), paṇḍicciyaṃ (pī.)} vibhāvaya, bālamato bhava sabbapāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbo taṃ jano ocināyatu, evaṃ tava attho bhavissati’’.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Karomi te taṃ vacanaṃ, yaṃ maṃ bhaṇasi devate;
::

::gathalast
Atthakāmāsi me amma, hitakāmāsi devate’’.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ nu santaramānova, kāsuṃ khaṇasi sārathi;
::

::gathalast
Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi, kiṃ kāsuyā karissasi’’.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rañño mūgo ca pakkho ca, putto jāto acetaso;
::

::gathalast
Somhi raññā samajjhiṭṭho, puttaṃ me nikhaṇaṃ vane’’.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na badhiro na mūgosmi, na pakkho na ca vīkalo {note:napi paṅgulo (sī. pī.), na ca piṅgalo (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Adhammaṃ sārathi kayirā, maṃ ce tvaṃ nikhaṇaṃ vane’’.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ūrū bāhuṃ {note:bāhū (sī. ka.)} ca me passa, bhāsitañca suṇohi me;
::

::gathalast
Adhammaṃ sārathi kayirā, maṃ ce tvaṃ nikhaṇaṃ vane’’.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devatā nusi gandhabbo, adu {note:ādu (sī.), ādū (syā.)} sakko purindado;
::

::gathalast
Ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Namhi devo na gandhabbo, nāpi sakko purindado;
::

::gathalast
Kāsirañño ahaṃ putto, yaṃ kāsuyā nikhaññasi {note:nighaññasi (sī. pī.), nikhañchasi (?)}.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa {pb:T:2.0154} rañño ahaṃ putto, yaṃ tvaṃ sammūpajīvasi {note:samupajīvasi (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Adhammaṃ sārathi kayirā, maṃ ce tvaṃ nikhaṇaṃ vane.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya, nisīdeyya sayeyya vā;
::

::gathalast
Na tassa sākhaṃ bhañjeyya, mittadubbho {note:mittadūbho (sī. pī.)} hi pāpako.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā {pb:M:2.0150} rukkho tathā rājā, yathā sākhā tathā ahaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Yathā chāyūpago poso, evaṃ tvamasi sārathi;
::

::gathalast
Adhammaṃ sārathi kayirā, maṃ ce tvaṃ nikhaṇaṃ vane.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pahūtabhakkho {pb:V:2.0103} {note:bahuttabhakkho (ka.)} bhavati, vippavuṭṭho {note:vippavuttho (sī. pī.), vippamutto (ka.)} sakaṃ {note:sakā (sī. pī.)} gharā;
::

::gathalast
Bahū naṃ upajīvanti, yo mittānaṃ na dubbhati.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ janapadaṃ yāti, nigame rājadhāniyo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha pūjito hoti, yo mittānaṃ na dubbhati.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāssa corā pasāhanti {note:pasahanti (sī. syā. pī.)}, nātimaññanti khattiyā {note:nātimaññeti khattiyo (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sabbe amitte tarati, yo mittānaṃ na dubbhati.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkuddho sagharaṃ eti, sabhāyaṃ {note:sabhāya (sī. syā. pī.)} paṭinandito;
::

::gathalast
Ñātīnaṃ uttamo hoti, yo mittānaṃ na dubbhati.
::

::hangnum
16\.

::gatha1

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
18\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
20\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
21\.

::gatha1

::gatha1

::hangnum

::gathalast

::gatha1

::gathalast
Upāyanāni me dajjuṃ, rājaputta tayī gate’’.

::gathalast
Ekaṃ sūlasmiṃ uppetha {note:appetha (sī.), ubbetha (syā.), accetha (pī.)}, iccassa manusāsati.

::gathalast

51\.

::gatha1

::gatha1

56\.

::gatha1

::gatha1

Yaṃ {pb:T:2.0159} te sutaṃ vā diṭṭhaṃ vā, rājaputtassa santike’’.

58\.

::gatha1
‘‘Na so mūgo na so pakkho, visaṭṭhavacano ca so;

59\.

61\.

::gatha1

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
63\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Ehi taṃ pāpayissāmi, yattha sammati temiyo’’.

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yojayantu rathe asse, kacchaṃ nāgāna {note:nāgāni (syā. ka.)} bandhatha;
::

::gathalast
Udīrayantu saṅkhapaṇavā, vādantu {note:vadantu (sī.), nadantu (syā. ka.), vadataṃ (pī.)} ekapokkharā.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vādantu {note:nadantu (sī. syā. pī.)} bherī sannaddhā, vaggū vādantu dundubhī;
::

::gathalast
Negamā ca maṃ anventu, gacchaṃ puttanivedako {note:nivādako (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Orodhā ca kumārā ca, vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Khippaṃ yānāni yojentu, gacchaṃ puttanivedako {note:nivādako (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthārohā anīkaṭṭhā, rathikā pattikārakā;
::

::gathalast
Khippaṃ {pb:T:2.0160} yānāni yojentu, gacchaṃ puttanivedako {note:nivādako (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samāgatā jānapadā, negamā ca samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Khippaṃ yānāni yojentu, gacchaṃ puttanivedako’’ {note:nivādako (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asse ca sārathī yutte, sindhave sīghavāhane;
::

::gathalast
Rājadvāraṃ upāgacchuṃ, yuttā deva ime hayā’’.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Thūlā javena hāyanti, kisā hāyanti thāmunā;
::

::gathalast
Kise thūle vivajjetvā, saṃsaṭṭhā yojitā hayā’’.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:V:2.0107}{pb:M:2.0155} rājā taramāno, yuttamāruyha sandanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Itthāgāraṃ ajjhabhāsi {note:abhāsatha (ka.)}, sabbāva anuyātha maṃ.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vālabījanimuṇhīsaṃ, khaggaṃ chattañca paṇḍaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upādhi rathamāruyha {note:upādirathamāruyha (sī.), upādhī rathamāruyha (syā.)}, suvaṇṇehi alaṅkatā.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato sa {note:ca (sī. syā. pī.)} rājā pāyāsi, purakkhatvāna sārathiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khippameva upāgacchi, yattha sammati temiyo.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañca disvāna āyantaṃ, jalantamiva tejasā;
::

::gathalast
Khattasaṅghaparibyūḷhaṃ {note:paribbūḷhaṃ (sī.)}, temiyo etadabravi’’.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci nu tāta kusalaṃ, kacci tāta anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbā ca {note:kaccinnu (sī. pī.)} rājakaññāyo, arogā mayha mātaro’’.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusalañceva me putta, atho putta anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbā ca rājakaññāyo, arogā tuyha mātaro’’.

#### 539. Mahājanakajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum

‘‘Kadāhaṃ {pb:V:2.0119}{pb:M:2.0169} sabbattha gantvā {note:sabbahaṃ ṭhānaṃ (sī.), sabbaṇhaṃ gantvā (syā.), sabbāhaṃ ṭhānaṃ (pī.), sabbaṭṭhānaṃ (ka.)}, rukkhā rukkhaṃ vanā vanaṃ;

::gathalast

#### 540. Suvaṇṇasāmajātakaṃ (3)

::hangnum
296\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko nu maṃ usunā vijjhi, pamattaṃ udahārakaṃ {note:hārikaṃ (syā.), hāriyaṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Khattiyo brāhmaṇo vesso, ko maṃ viddhā nilīyasi.
::

::hangnum
297\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na me maṃsāni khajjāni, cammenattho na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, viddheyyaṃ maṃ amaññatha.
::

::hangnum
298\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi, kiṃ maṃ viddhā nilīyasi’’.
::

::hangnum
299\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājāhamasmi kāsīnaṃ, pīḷiyakkhoti maṃ vidū;
::

::gathalast
Lobhā raṭṭhaṃ pahitvāna, migamesaṃ carāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
300\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Issatthe casmi kusalo, daḷhadhammoti vissuto;
::

::gathalast
Nāgopi me na mucceyya, āgato usupātanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
301\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko {pb:V:2.0124}{pb:M:2.0175} vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto {note:tvaṃ ca kassa vā puttosi (sī. pī.)}, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pituno attano cāpi, nāmagottaṃ pavedaya’’.
::

::hangnum
302\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nesādaputto bhaddante, sāmo iti maṃ ñātayo;
::

::gathalast
Āmantayiṃsu jīvantaṃ, svajjevāhaṃ gato {note:svājjevaṅgato (syā.), svajjevaṅgate (ka.)} saye.
::

::hangnum
303\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Viddhosmi puthusallena, savisena yathā migo;
::

::gathalast
Sakamhi lohite rāja, passa semi paripluto.
::

::hangnum
304\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭivāmagataṃ {pb:T:2.0186} {note:paṭidhamma gataṃ (sī. pī.)} sallaṃ, passa dhimhāmi {note:vihāmhi (sī. pī.)} lohitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āturo tyānupucchāmi, kiṃ maṃ viddhā nilīyasi.
::

::hangnum
305\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajinamhi haññate dīpi, nāgo dantehi haññate;
::

::gathalast
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, viddheyyaṃ maṃ amaññatha’’.
::

::hangnum
306\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Migo upaṭṭhito āsi, āgato usupātanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ disvā ubbijī sāma, tena kodho mamāvisi’’.
::

::hangnum
307\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yato sarāmi attānaṃ, yato pattosmi viññutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na maṃ migā uttasanti, araññe sāpadānipi.
::

::hangnum
308\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yato nidhiṃ parihariṃ, yato pattosmi yobbanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na maṃ migā uttasanti, araññe sāpadānipi.
::

::hangnum
309\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhīrū kimpurisā rāja, pabbate gandhamādane;
::

::gathalast
Sammodamānā gacchāma, pabbatāni vanāni ca.
::

::hangnum
310\.
::

::gatha1
(‘‘Na maṃ migā uttasanti, araññe sāpadānipi;) {note:( ) natthi sī. syā. pī. potthakesu}
::

::gathalast
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, utrāsanti migā mamaṃ’’ {note:utrāse so migo mamaṃ (sī. pī.)}.

::hangnum
311\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na taṃ tasa {note:na taddasā (sī. pī.)} migo sāma, kiṃ tāhaṃ alikaṃ bhaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Kodhalobhābhibhūtāhaṃ, usuṃ te taṃ avassajiṃ {note:avissajiṃ (syā.)}.

::hangnum

::

::gatha1
‘‘Sā devatā antarahitā, pabbate gandhamādane;

::gathalast

#### 541. Nimijātakaṃ (4)

::hangnum
421\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accheraṃ {pb:T:2.0198} vata lokasmiṃ, uppajjanti vicakkhaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Yadā ahu nimirājā, paṇḍito kusalatthiko.
::

::hangnum
422\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājā sabbavidehānaṃ, adā dānaṃ arindamo;
::

::gatha2
Tassa taṃ dadato dānaṃ, saṅkappo udapajjatha;
::

::gathalast
Dānaṃ vā brahmacariyaṃ vā, katamaṃ su mahapphalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
423\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa saṅkappamaññāya, maghavā devakuñjaro;
::

::gathalast
Sahassanetto pāturahu, vaṇṇena vihanaṃ {note:nihanaṃ (sī. pī.), vihataṃ (syā. ka.)} tamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
424\.
::

::gatha1
Salomahaṭṭho {pb:M:2.0185} manujindo, vāsavaṃ avacā nimi;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Devatā nusi gandhabbo, adu sakko purindado.
::

::hangnum
425\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na ca me tādiso vaṇṇo, diṭṭho vā yadi vā suto;
::

::gathalast
{note:natthi sī. pī. potthakesu} Ācikkha me tvaṃ bhaddante, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ’’ {note:natthi sī. pī. potthakesu}.
::

::hangnum
426\.
::

::gatha1
Salomahaṭṭhaṃ ñatvāna, vāsavo avacā nimiṃ;
::

::gatha2
‘‘Sakkohamasmi devindo, āgatosmi tavantike;
::

::gathalast
Alomahaṭṭho manujinda, puccha pañhaṃ yamicchasi’’.
::

::hangnum
427\.
::

::gatha1
So ca tena katokāso, vāsavaṃ avacā nimi;
::

::gatha2
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ mahārāja {note:mahābāhu (sī. pī.), devarāja (ka.)}, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gathalast
Dānaṃ vā brahmacariyaṃ vā, katamaṃ su mahapphalaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
428\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
431\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Usindaro {note:usīnaro (sī. pī.)} kassapo ca {note:aṭṭhako ca (sī. pī.), atthako ca (syā.)}, asako ca puthujjano.

::hangnum

::gatha1

‘‘Cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ, yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī;
::

::gathalast
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, aṭṭhaṅgasusamāhitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
544\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uposathaṃ upavasī, sadā sīlesu saṃvuto;
::

::gathalast
Saṃyamā saṃvibhāgā ca, so vimānasmi modati’’.
::

::hangnum
545\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pabhāsati {pb:T:2.0218}{pb:V:2.0142} midaṃ byamhaṃ, veḷuriyāsu nimmitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upetaṃ bhūmibhāgehi, vibhattaṃ bhāgaso mitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
546\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
547\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ evaṃgataṃ jātu {note:jātaṃ (ka.)}, evaṃsuruciyaṃ pure;
::

::gathalast
Saddaṃ samabhijānāmi, diṭṭhaṃ vā yadi vā sutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
548\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vittī {pb:M:2.0200} hi maṃ vindati sūta disvā, pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi;
::

::gathalast
Ayaṃ nu macco kimakāsi sādhuṃ, yo modati saggapatto vimāne’’.
::

::hangnum
549\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::gathalast

::

::gathalast
Uyyāhi dāni rājīsi, devarājassa santike’’.

::hangnum
566\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Disvānāmantayī sūtaṃ, ‘‘ime ke nāma pabbatā’’.

::hangnum
567\.

::gatha1
{note:ayaṃ gāthā sī. syā. pī. potthakesu aṭṭhakathāyañca na dissati} Tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi, mātali devasārathi;

::gathalast

::

::gathalast
Pavisetena rājīsi, devānaṃ anumodanaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
582\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ devā paṭinandiṃsu, disvā rājānamāgataṃ;
::

::gatha2
‘‘Svāgataṃ te mahārāja, atho te adurāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nisīda dāni rājīsi, devarājassa santike’’.
::

::hangnum
583\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Nimantayittha {note:nimantayī ca (sī. pī.)} kāmehi, āsanena ca vāsavo.
::

::hangnum
584\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sādhu khosi anuppatto, āvāsaṃ vasavattinaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Vasa devesu rājīsi, sabbakāmasamiddhisu;
::

::gathalast
Tāvatiṃsesu devesu, bhuñja kāme amānuse’’.
::

::hangnum
585\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā {pb:V:2.0145} yācitakaṃ yānaṃ, yathā yācitakaṃ dhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃsampadamevetaṃ, yaṃ parato dānapaccayā.
::

::hangnum
586\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na cāhametamicchāmi, yaṃ parato dānapaccayā;
::

::gathalast
Sayaṃkatāni {pb:T:2.0223} puññāni, taṃ me āveṇikaṃ {note:āveṇiyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.), āvenikaṃ (ka.)} dhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
587\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sohaṃ gantvā manussesu, kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahuṃ;
::

::gatha2
Dānena samacariyāya, saṃyamena damena ca;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ katvā sukhito hoti, na ca pacchānutappati’’.
::

::hangnum
588\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahūpakāro no bhavaṃ, mātali devasārathi;
::

::gathalast
Yo me kalyāṇakammānaṃ, pāpānaṃ paṭidassayi’’ {note:paṭidaṃsayi (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
589\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvā nimirājā, vedeho mithilaggaho;
::

::gathalast
Puthuyaññaṃ yajitvāna, saṃyamaṃ ajjhupāgamī’’ti.
::

::centre
Nimijātakaṃ {note:nemirājajātakaṃ (syā.)} catutthaṃ.

#### 542. Umaṅgajātakaṃ (5)

::hangnum
590\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcālo {pb:M:2.0204} sabbasenāya, brahmadattoyamāgato;
::

::gathalast
Sāyaṃ pañcāliyā senā, appameyyā mahosadha.
::

::hangnum
591\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīthimatī {note:piṭṭhimatī (sī. pī.), viddhimatī (syā.)} pattimatī, sabbasaṅgāmakovidā;
::

::gathalast
Ohārinī saddavatī, bherisaṅkhappabodhanā.
::

::hangnum
592\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lohavijjā alaṅkārā, dhajinī vāmarohinī;
::

::gathalast
Sippiyehi susampannā, sūrehi suppatiṭṭhitā.
::

::hangnum
593\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dasettha paṇḍitā āhu, bhūripaññā rahogamā {note:rahogatā (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Mātā ekādasī rañño, pañcāliyaṃ pasāsati.
::

::hangnum
594\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athetthekasataṃ {pb:T:2.0224} khatyā, anuyantā yasassino;
::

::gathalast
Acchinnaraṭṭhā byathitā, pañcāliyaṃ {note:pañcālīnaṃ (bahūsu)} vasaṃ gatā.
::

::hangnum
595\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃvadā-takkarā rañño, akāmā piyabhāṇino;
::

::gathalast
Pañcālamanuyāyanti, akāmā vasino gatā.
::

::hangnum
596\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāya senāya mithilā, tisandhiparivāritā;
::

::gathalast
Rājadhānī videhānaṃ, samantā parikhaññati.
::

::hangnum
597\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uddhaṃ {pb:V:2.0146} tārakajātāva, samantā parivāritā;
::

::gathalast
Mahosadha vijānāhi, kathaṃ mokkho bhavissati’’.
::

::hangnum
598\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāde deva pasārehi, bhuñja kāme ramassu ca;
::

::gathalast
Hitvā pañcāliyaṃ senaṃ, brahmadatto palāyiti’’ {note:palāyati (sī. syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
599\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājā santhavakāmo te, ratanāni pavecchati;
::

::gathalast
Āgacchantu ito {note:tato (sī. syā.)} dūtā, mañjukā piyabhāṇino.
::

::hangnum
600\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhāsantu mudukā vācā, yā vācā paṭinanditā;
::

::gathalast
Pañcālo ca videho ca {note:pañcālā ca videhā ca (sī. pī.)}, ubho ekā bhavantu te’’.
::

::hangnum
601\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ nu kevaṭṭa mahosadhena, samāgamo āsi tadiṅgha brūhi;
::

::gathalast
Kacci te paṭinijjhatto, kacci tuṭṭho mahosadho’’.
::

::hangnum
602\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anariyarūpo {pb:M:2.0205} puriso janinda, asammodako thaddho asabbhirūpo;
::

::gathalast
Yathā mūgo ca badhiro ca, na kiñcitthaṃ abhāsatha’’ {note:abhāsittha (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
603\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā {pb:T:2.0225} idaṃ mantapadaṃ sududdasaṃ, attho suddho naravīriyena diṭṭho;
::

::gathalast
Tathā hi kāyo mama sampavedhati, hitvā sayaṃ ko parahatthamessati’’.
::

::hangnum
604\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Channañhi ekāva matī sameti, ye paṇḍitā uttamabhūripattā;
::

::gathalast
Yānaṃ ayānaṃ atha vāpi ṭhānaṃ, mahosadha tvampi matiṃ karohi’’.
::

::hangnum
605\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jānāsi kho rāja mahānubhāvo, mahabbalo cūḷanibrahmadatto;
::

::gathalast
Rājā ca taṃ icchati māraṇatthaṃ {note:kāraṇatthaṃ (sī. pī.)}, migaṃ yathā okacarena luddo.
::

::hangnum
606\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāpi maccho baḷisaṃ, vaṅkaṃ maṃsena chāditaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āmagiddho na jānāti, maccho maraṇamattano.
::

::hangnum
607\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evameva tuvaṃ rāja, cūḷaneyyassa dhītaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāmagiddho na jānāsi, macchova maraṇamattano.
::

::hangnum
608\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace gacchasi pañcālaṃ, khippamattaṃ jahissati;
::

::gathalast
Migaṃ panthānubandhaṃva {note:pathānupannaṃva (sī. syā. pī.)}, mahantaṃ bhayamessati’’.
::

::hangnum
609\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mayameva bālamhase eḷamūgā, ye uttamatthāni tayī lapimhā;
::

::gathalast
Kimeva {pb:T:2.0226} tvaṃ naṅgalakoṭivaḍḍho, atthāni jānāsi yathāpi aññe’’.
::

::hangnum
610\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imaṃ gale gahetvāna, nāsetha vijitā mama;
::

::gathalast
Yo me ratanalābhassa, antarāyāya bhāsati’’.
::

::hangnum
611\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:M:2.0206} ca so apakkamma, vedehassa upantikā;
::

::gathalast
Atha āmantayī dūtaṃ, mādharaṃ {note:maḍharaṃ (sī.), mādhuraṃ (syā.), māṭharaṃ (pī.)} suvapaṇḍitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
612\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ehi {pb:V:2.0147} samma haritapakkha {note:harīpakkha (sī. pī.)}, veyyāvaccaṃ karohi me;
::

::gathalast
Atthi pañcālarājassa, sāḷikā sayanapālikā.
::

::hangnum
613\.
::

::gatha1
‘Taṃ bandhanena {note:taṃ pattharena (sī. pī.), taṃ santhavena (syā.)} pucchassu, sā hi sabbassa kovidā;
::

::gathalast
Sā tesaṃ sabbaṃ jānāti, rañño ca kosiyassa ca.
::

::hangnum
614\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘‘Āmo’ti so paṭissutvā, mādharo suvapaṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Agamāsi haritapakkho {note:harīpakkho (sī. pī.)}, sāḷikāya upantikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
615\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato ca kho so gantvāna, mādharo suvapaṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Athāmantayi sugharaṃ, sāḷikaṃ mañjubhāṇikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
616\.
::

::gatha1
‘Kacci te sughare khamanīyaṃ, kacci vesse anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kacci te madhunā lājā, labbhate sughare tuvaṃ’ {note:tava (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
617\.
::

::gatha1
‘Kusalañceva me samma, atho samma anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atho me madhunā lājā, labbhate suvapaṇḍita.
::

::hangnum
618\.
::

::gatha1
‘Kuto nu samma āgamma, kassa vā pahito tuvaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na {pb:T:2.0227} ca mesi ito pubbe, diṭṭho vā yadi vā suto’’.
::

::hangnum
619\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahosiṃ sivirājassa, pāsāde sayanapālako;
::

::gathalast
Tato so dhammiko rājā, baddhe mocesi bandhanā’’.
::

::hangnum
620\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa mekā dutiyāsi, sāḷikā mañjubhāṇikā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ tattha avadhī seno, pekkhato sughare mama’’.
::

::hangnum
621\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassā kāmā hi sammatto, āgatosmi tavantike;
::

::gathalast
Sace kareyya {note:kareyyāsi (sī.), kareyu (syā.), kareyyāsi me (pī.)} okāsaṃ, ubhayova vasāmase’’.
::
