::gatha1
‘‘Āhaññantu {pb:V:2.0159} sabbavīṇā, bheriyo dindimāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Dhamentu māgadhā saṅkhā, vaggū nadantu dundubhī’’.
::

::hangnum
780\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Orodhā ca kumārā ca, vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Bahuṃ annañca pānañca, paṇḍitassābhihārayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
781\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthārohā anīkaṭṭhā, rathikā pattikārakā;
::

::gathalast
Bahuṃ annañca pānañca, paṇḍitassābhihārayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
782\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samāgatā jānapadā, negamā ca samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Bahuṃ {pb:T:2.0245} annañca pānañca, paṇḍitassābhihārayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
783\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahujano {pb:M:2.0221} pasannosi, disvā paṇḍitamāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paṇḍitamhi anuppatte, celukkhepo avattathā’’ti.
::

::centre
Umaṅgajātakaṃ {note:mahāummaggajātakaṃ (sī. pī.), mahosadhajātakaṃ (syā.§ka.)} pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 543. Bhūridattajātakaṃ (6)

::hangnum
784\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci ratanaṃ atthi, dhataraṭṭhanivesane;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāni te upayantu, dhītaraṃ dehi rājino’’.
::

::hangnum
785\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na no vivāho nāgehi, katapubbo kudācanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ vivāhaṃ asaṃyuttaṃ, kathaṃ amhe karomase’’.
::

::hangnum
786\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jīvitaṃ nūna te cattaṃ, raṭṭhaṃ vā manujādhipa;
::

::gathalast
Na hi nāge kupitamhi, ciraṃ jīvanti tādisā.
::

::hangnum
787\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo tvaṃ deva manussosi, iddhimantaṃ aniddhimā;
::

::gathalast
Varuṇassa niyaṃ puttaṃ, yāmunaṃ atimaññasi’’.
::

::hangnum
788\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nātimaññāmi rājānaṃ, dhataraṭṭhaṃ yasassinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhataraṭṭho hi nāgānaṃ, bahūnamapi issaro.
::

::hangnum
789\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahi mahānubhāvopi, na me dhītaramāraho;
::

::gathalast
Khattiyo ca videhānaṃ, abhijātā samuddajā’’.
::

::hangnum
790\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kambalassatarā uṭṭhentu, sabbe nāge nivedaya;
::

::gathalast
Bārāṇasiṃ pavajjantu, mā ca kañci {note:kiñci (sī. pī. ka.)} viheṭhayuṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
791\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nivesanesu {pb:T:2.0246}{pb:V:2.0160} sobbhesu, rathiyā caccaresu ca;
::

::gathalast
Rukkhaggesu ca lambantu, vitatā toraṇesu ca.
::

::hangnum
792\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahampi sabbasetena, mahatā sumahaṃ puraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parikkhipissaṃ bhogehi, kāsīnaṃ janayaṃ bhayaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
793\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, uragānekavaṇṇino;
::

::gathalast
Bārāṇasiṃ pavajjiṃsu, na ca kañci viheṭhayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
794\.
::

::gatha1
Nivesanesu sobbhesu, rathiyā caccaresu ca;
::

::gathalast
Rukkhaggesu ca lambiṃsu, vitatā toraṇesu ca.
::

::hangnum
795\.
::

::gatha1
Tesu {pb:M:2.0222} disvāna lambante, puthū kandiṃsu nāriyo;
::

::gathalast
Nāge soṇḍikate disvā, passasante muhuṃ muhuṃ.
::

::hangnum
796\.
::

::gatha1
Bārāṇasī pabyadhitā, āturā samapajjatha;
::

::gathalast
Bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ, ‘‘dhītaraṃ dehi rājino’’.
::

::hangnum
797\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pupphābhihārassa vanassa majjhe, ko lohitakkho vitatantaraṃso;
::

::gathalast
Kā kambukāyūradharā suvatthā, tiṭṭhanti nāriyo dasa vandamānā.
::

::hangnum
798\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko tvaṃ brahābāhu vanassa majjhe, virocasi ghatasittova aggi;
::

::gathalast
Mahesakkho aññatarosi yakkho, udāhu nāgosi mahānubhāvo’’.
::

::hangnum
799\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāgohamasmi {pb:T:2.0247} iddhimā, tejassī {note:tejasī (sī. syā. pī. ka.)} duratikkamo;
::

::gathalast
Ḍaṃseyyaṃ tejasā kuddho, phītaṃ janapadaṃ api.
::

::hangnum
800\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samuddajā hi me mātā, dhataraṭṭho ca me pitā;
::

::gathalast
Sudassanakaniṭṭhosmi, bhūridattoti maṃ vidū’’.
::

::hangnum
801\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ gambhīraṃ sadāvaṭṭaṃ, rahadaṃ bhismaṃ pekkhasi;
::

::gathalast
Esa dibyo mamāvāso, anekasataporiso.
::

::hangnum
802\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mayūrakoñcābhirudaṃ, nīlodaṃ vanamajjhato;
::

::gathalast
Yamunaṃ pavisa mā bhīto, khemaṃ vattavataṃ {note:vattavatiṃ (syā. ka.)} sivaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
803\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha patto sānucaro, saha puttena brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Pūjito mayhaṃ kāmehi, sukhaṃ brāhmaṇa vacchasi’’.
::

::hangnum
804\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samā samantaparito, pahūtatagarā {note:bahukā taggarā (sī. syā. pī.)} mahī;
::

::gathalast
Indagopakasañchannā, sobhati harituttamā.
::

::hangnum
805\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rammāni vanacetyāni, rammā haṃsūpakūjitā;
::

::gathalast
Opupphāpadmā tiṭṭhanti, pokkharañño {note:pokkharaññā (syā. pī.)} sunimmitā.
::

::hangnum
806\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭhaṃsā {pb:V:2.0161}{pb:M:2.0223} sukatā thambhā, sabbe veḷuriyāmayā;
::

::gathalast
Sahassathambhā pāsādā, pūrā kaññāhi jotare.
::

::hangnum
807\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vimānaṃ upapannosi, dibyaṃ puññehi attano;
::

::gathalast
Asambādhaṃ sivaṃ rammaṃ, accantasukhasaṃhitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
808\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maññe sahassanettassa, vimānaṃ nābhikaṅkhasi;
::

::gathalast
Iddhī hi tyāyaṃ vipulā, sakkasseva jutīmato’’.
::

::hangnum
809\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Manasāpi {pb:T:2.0248} na pattabbo, ānubhāvo jutīmato;
::

::gathalast
Paricārayamānānaṃ, saindānaṃ {note:indānaṃ (syā. ka.)} vasavattinaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
810\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ vimānaṃ abhijjhāya, amarānaṃ sukhesinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uposathaṃ upavasanto, semi vammikamuddhani’’.
::

::hangnum
811\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahañca migamesāno, saputto pāvisiṃ vanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ maṃ mataṃ vā jīvaṃ vā, nābhivedenti ñātakā.
::

::hangnum
812\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āmantaye bhūridattaṃ, kāsiputtaṃ yasassinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tayā no samanuññātā, api passemu ñātake’’.
::

::hangnum
813\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Eso hi vata me chando, yaṃ vasesi mamantike;
::

::gathalast
Na hi etādisā kāmā, sulabhā honti mānuse.
::

::hangnum
814\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace tvaṃ nicchase vatthuṃ, mama kāmehi pūjito;
::

::gathalast
Mayā tvaṃ samanuññāto, sotthiṃ passāhi ñātake’’.
::

::hangnum
815\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhārayimaṃ maṇiṃ dibyaṃ, pasuṃ putte ca vindati;
::

::gathalast
Arogo sukhito hoti {note:hohi (syā.)}, gacchevādāya brāhmaṇa’’.
::

::hangnum
816\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusalaṃ paṭinandāmi, bhūridatta vaco tava;
::

::gathalast
Pabbajissāmi jiṇṇosmi, na kāme abhipatthaye’’.
::

::hangnum
817\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Brahmacariyassa ce bhaṅgo, hoti bhogehi kāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Avikampamāno eyyāsi, bahuṃ dassāmi te dhanaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
818\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusalaṃ paṭinandāmi, bhūridatta vaco tava;
::

::gathalast
Punapi āgamissāmi, sace attho bhavissati’’.
::

::hangnum
819\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:T:2.0249}{pb:M:2.0224} vatvā bhūridatto, pesesi caturo jane;
::

::gathalast
Etha gacchatha uṭṭhetha, khippaṃ pāpetha brāhmaṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
820\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, uṭṭhāya caturo janā;
::

::gathalast
Pesitā bhūridattena, khippaṃ pāpesu brāhmaṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
821\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maṇiṃ {pb:V:2.0162} paggayha maṅgalyaṃ, sādhuvittaṃ {note:sādhucittaṃ (pī.)} manoramaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Selaṃ byañjanasampannaṃ, ko imaṃ maṇimajjhagā’’.
::

::hangnum
822\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lohitakkhasahassāhi, samantā parivāritaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ajja kālaṃ pathaṃ {note:padaṃ (sī. pī.)} gacchaṃ, ajjhagāhaṃ maṇiṃ imaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
823\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Supaciṇṇo ayaṃ selo, accito mahito {note:mānito (ka.)} sadā;
::

::gathalast
Sudhārito sunikkhitto, sabbatthamabhisādhaye.
::

::hangnum
824\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upacāravipannassa, nikkhepe dhāraṇāya vā;
::

::gathalast
Ayaṃ selo vināsāya, pariciṇṇo ayoniso.
::

::hangnum
825\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na imaṃ akusalo {note:kusalaṃ (ka.)} dibyaṃ, maṇiṃ dhāretumāraho;
::

::gathalast
Paṭipajja sataṃ nikkhaṃ, dehimaṃ ratanaṃ mama’’.
::

::hangnum
826\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na ca myāyaṃ maṇī keyyo, gohi {note:kehi (ka.)} vā ratanehi vā;
::

::gathalast
Selo byañjanasampanno, neva keyyo maṇī mama’’.
::

::hangnum
827\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘No ce tayā maṇī keyyo, gohi {note:kehi (ka.)} vā ratanehi vā;
::

::gathalast
Atha kena maṇī keyyo, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito’’.
::

::hangnum
828\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo me saṃse mahānāgaṃ, tejassiṃ duratikkamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa {pb:T:2.0250} dajjaṃ imaṃ selaṃ, jalantamiva tejasā’’.
::

::hangnum
829\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko nu brāhmaṇavaṇṇena, supaṇṇo patataṃ varo;
::

::gathalast
Nāgaṃ jigīsamanvesi, anvesaṃ bhakkhamattano.
::

::hangnum
830\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ dijādhipo homi, na diṭṭho garuḷo mayā;
::

::gathalast
Āsīvisena vittoti {note:vittosmi (syā. ka.)}, vajjo brāhmaṇa maṃ vidū’’.
::

::hangnum
831\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ nu tuyhaṃ balaṃ atthi, kiṃ sippaṃ vijjate tava;
::

::gathalast
Kismiṃ vā tvaṃ paratthaddho, uragaṃ nāpacāyasi’’.
::

::hangnum
832\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āraññikassa {pb:M:2.0225} isino, cirarattaṃ tapassino;
::

::gathalast
Supaṇṇo kosiyassakkhā, visavijjaṃ anuttaraṃ.

::hangnum
833\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ bhāvitattaññataraṃ, sammantaṃ pabbatantare;
::

::gathalast
Sakkaccaṃ taṃ upaṭṭhāsiṃ, rattindivamatandito.
::

::hangnum
834\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So tadā pariciṇṇo me, vattavā brahmacariyavā;
::

::gathalast
Dibbaṃ pātukarī mantaṃ, kāmasā bhagavā mama.
::

::hangnum
835\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tyāhaṃ mante paratthaddho, nāhaṃ bhāyāmi bhoginaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ācariyo visaghātānaṃ, alampānoti {note:ālambānoti (sī. pī.), ālambāyanoti (syā.)} maṃ vidū’’.

::hangnum
836\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gaṇhāmase {pb:V:2.0163} maṇiṃ tāta, somadatta vijānahi;
::

::gathalast
Mā daṇḍena siriṃ pattaṃ, kāmasā pajahimhase’’.
::

::hangnum
837\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakaṃ nivesanaṃ pattaṃ, yo taṃ brāhmaṇa pūjayi;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ kalyāṇakārissa, kiṃ mohā dubbhimicchasi’’.
::

::hangnum
838\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace {pb:T:2.0251} tvaṃ {note:sace hi (sī. pī. ka.)} dhanakāmosi, bhūridatto padassati {note:bhūridattaṃ padissasi (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Tameva gantvā yācassu, bahuṃ dassati te dhanaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
839\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthagataṃ pattagataṃ, nikiṇṇaṃ khādituṃ varaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mā no sandiṭṭhiko attho, somadatta upaccagā’’.
::

::hangnum
840\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paccati niraye ghore, mahissamapi vivarati {note:mahissamava dīyati (sī. pī.), mahimassa vindrīyati (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Mittadubbhī hitaccāgī, jīvarevāpi sussati {note:jīvare cāpi sussare (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
841\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace tvaṃ {note:sace hi (sī. pī. ka.)} dhanakāmosi, bhūridatto padassati;
::

::gathalast
Maññe attakataṃ veraṃ, naciraṃ vedayissasi’’.

::hangnum
842\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāyaññaṃ yajitvāna, evaṃ sujjhanti brāhmaṇā;

::gathalast

::hangnum
843\.

::gatha1

Padampekaṃ {note:padamekaṃ (syā. ka.)} na gaccheyyaṃ, evaṃ kibbisakārinā’’.

::hangnum
844\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
845\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
846\.

::gatha1

::gathalast
Vammikaggagato seti, taṃ tvaṃ gaṇhāhi brāhmaṇa’’.

::hangnum
847\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athosadhehi dibbehi, jappaṃ mantapadāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ taṃ asakkhi satthuṃ {note:saṭṭhuṃ (sī. pī.), yuṭṭhuṃ (syā.), suttuṃ (ka.)}, katvā parittamattano’’.
::

::hangnum
848\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mamaṃ {pb:T:2.0252} disvāna āyantaṃ, sabbakāmasamiddhinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Indriyāni ahaṭṭhāni, sāvaṃ {note:sāmaṃ (sī. pī.)} jātaṃ mukhaṃ tava.
::

::hangnum
849\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padmaṃ yathā hatthagataṃ, pāṇinā parimadditaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāvaṃ jātaṃ {note:yantaṃ (ka.)} mukhaṃ tuyhaṃ, mamaṃ disvāna edisaṃ.
::

::hangnum
850\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci nu te nābhisasi {note:te nābhisayi (sī.), te nābhissasi (syā.)}, kacci te atthi vedanā;
::

::gathalast
Yena sāvaṃ mukhaṃ tuyhaṃ, mamaṃ disvāna āgataṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
851\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Supinaṃ {pb:V:2.0164} tāta addakkhiṃ, ito māsaṃ adhogataṃ;
::

::gatha2
Dakkhiṇaṃ viya me bāhuṃ, chetvā ruhiramakkhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Puriso ādāya pakkāmi, mama rodantiyā sati.
::

::hangnum
852\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yatohaṃ {note:yato taṃ (sī.)} supinamaddakkhiṃ, sudassana vijānahi;
::

::gathalast
Tato divā vā rattiṃ vā, sukhaṃ me nopalabbhati’’.
::

::hangnum
853\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ pubbe parivāriṃsu {note:paricāriṃsu (sī. pī.)}, kaññā ruciraviggahā;
::

::gathalast
Hemajālapaṭicchannā, bhūridatto na dissati.
::

::hangnum
854\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ pubbe parivāriṃsu {note:paricāriṃsu (sī. pī.)}, nettiṃsavaradhārino;

::gathalast

::hangnum
855\.
::

::gatha1

::hangnum
856\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
857\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puttaṃ teyye na jānāma, ito māsaṃ adhogataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mataṃ {pb:T:2.0253} vā yadi vā jīvaṃ, bhūridattaṃ yasassinaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
858\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakuṇī hataputtāva, suññaṃ disvā kulāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ciraṃ dukkhena jhāyissaṃ, bhūridattaṃ apassatī {note:imissā gāthāyānantare sī. pī. potthakesu – ‘‘sakuṇī hataputtāva, suññaṃ disvā kulāvakaṃ; tena tena padhāvissa, piyaputtaṃ apassatī’’ti iti ayampi gāthā āgatā}.
::

::hangnum
859\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kurarī hatachāpāva, suññaṃ disvā kulāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ciraṃ dukkhena jhāyissaṃ, bhūridattaṃ apassatī.
::

::hangnum
860\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sā nūna cakkavākīva, pallalasmiṃ anodake;
::

::gathalast
Ciraṃ dukkhena jhāyissaṃ, bhūridattaṃ apassatī.
::

::hangnum
861\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kammārānaṃ yathā ukkā, anto jhāyati no bahi;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ jhāyāmi sokena, bhūridattaṃ apassatī’’.

::hangnum
862\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sālāva sampamathitā {note:sampamadditā (syā. ka.)}, mālutena pamadditā;
::

::gathalast
Senti puttā ca dārā ca, bhūridattanivesane’’.

‘‘Yasmā ca etaṃ vacanaṃ abhūtaṃ, musāvime odariyā bhaṇanti;
::

::gathalast
Tadappapaññā abhisaddahanti, passanti taṃ paṇḍitā attanāva.
::

::hangnum
935\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khatyā {pb:V:2.0170}{pb:M:2.0236} hi vessānaṃ {note:khattā na vessā na (sī. pī.)} baliṃ haranti, ādāya satthāni caranti brāhmaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ tādisaṃ saṅkhubhitaṃ pabhinnaṃ, kasmā brahmā nujju karoti lokaṃ.
::

::hangnum
936\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace hi so issaro sabbaloke, brahmā bahūbhūtapatī {note:brahmapahū bhūtapatī (syā.)} pajānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ sabbalokaṃ vidahī alakkhiṃ, kiṃ sabbalokaṃ na sukhiṃ akāsi.
::

::hangnum
937\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace hi so issaro sabbaloke, brahmā bahūbhūtapatī pajānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Māyā musāvajjamadena {note:musāvañcanapadena (ka.)} cāpi, lokaṃ adhammena kimatthamakāri {note:kimattha’kāsi (sī. pī.), kimatthakārī (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
938\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace hi so issaro sabbaloke, brahmā bahūbhūtapatī pajānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Adhammiko {pb:T:2.0265} bhūtapatī ariṭṭha, dhamme sati yo vidahī adhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
939\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kīṭā paṭaṅgā uragā ca bhekā {note:bhiṅgā (syā.)}, hantvā kimī sujjhati makkhikā ca;
::

::gathalast
Etepi dhammā anariyarūpā, kambojakānaṃ vitathā bahūnaṃ.
::

::hangnum
940\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace hi so sujjhati yo hanāti, hatopi so saggamupeti ṭhānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhovādi bhovādina mārayeyyuṃ {note:mārabheyyuṃ (ka.)}, ye cāpi tesaṃ abhisaddaheyyuṃ.
::

::hangnum
941\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Neva {pb:M:2.0237} migā na pasū nopi gāvo, āyācanti attavadhāya keci;
::

::gathalast
Vipphandamāne idha jīvikatthā, yaññesu pāṇe pasumārabhanti {note:māharanti (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
942\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yūpussane {note:yūpassa te (sī.), yūpassa ne (pī.)} pasubandhe ca bālā, cittehi vaṇṇehi mukhaṃ nayanti;
::

::gathalast
Ayaṃ te yūpo kāmaduho parattha, bhavissati sassato samparāye.
::

::hangnum
943\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace ca yūpe maṇisaṅkhamuttaṃ, dhaññaṃ {pb:T:2.0266} dhanaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sukkhesu kaṭṭhesu navesu cāpi, sace duhe tidive sabbakāme;
::

::gathalast
Tevijjasaṅghāva puthū yajeyyuṃ, abrāhmaṇaṃ {note:na brāhmaṇā (sī. syā.)} kañci na yājayeyyuṃ.
::

::hangnum
944\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuto ca yūpe maṇisaṅkhamuttaṃ, dhaññaṃ dhanaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sukkhesu kaṭṭhesu navesu cāpi, kuto duhe tidive sabbakāme.
::

::hangnum
945\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṭhā ca luddā ca paluddhabālā {note:upaladdhabālā (sī. pī.)}, cittehi vaṇṇehi mukhaṃ nayanti;
::

::gathalast
Ādāya aggiṃ mama dehi vittaṃ, tato sukhī hohisi sabbakāme.
::

::hangnum
946\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamaggihuttaṃ saraṇaṃ pavissa, cittehi vaṇṇehi mukhaṃ nayanti;
::

::gathalast
Oropayitvā kesamassuṃ nakhañca, vedehi vittaṃ atigāḷhayanti {note:atigāḷayanti (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
947\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kākā {pb:M:2.0238} ulūkaṃva raho labhitvā, ekaṃ samānaṃ bahukā samecca;
::

::gathalast
Annāni bhutvā kuhakā kuhitvā, muṇḍaṃ {pb:T:2.0267} karitvā yaññapathossajanti.
::

::hangnum
948\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evañhi so vañcito brāhmaṇehi, eko samāno bahukā {note:bahuhī (sī.)} samecca;
::

::gathalast
Te yogayogena vilumpamānā, diṭṭhaṃ adiṭṭhena dhanaṃ haranti.
::

::hangnum
949\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akāsiyā {pb:V:2.0171} rājūhivānusiṭṭhā, tadassa ādāya dhanaṃ haranti;
::

::gathalast
Te tādisā corasamā asantā, vajjhā na haññanti ariṭṭha loke.
::

::hangnum
950\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Indassa bāhārasi dakkhiṇāti, yaññesu chindanti palāsayaṭṭhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ cepi saccaṃ maghavā chinnabāhu, kenassa indo asure jināti.
::

::hangnum
951\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañceva tucchaṃ maghavā samaṅgī, hantā avajjho paramo sa devo {note:sudevo (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Mantā ime brāhmaṇā tuccharūpā, sandiṭṭhikā vañcanā esa loke.
::

::hangnum
952\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mālāgiri himavā yo ca gijjho, sudassano nisabho kuveru;
::

::gathalast
Ete ca aññe ca nagā mahantā, cityā {pb:T:2.0268} katā yaññakarehi māhu.
::

::hangnum
953\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāpakārāni hi iṭṭhakāni, cityā katā yaññakarehi māhu;
::

::gathalast
Na pabbatā honti tathāpakārā, aññā disā acalā tiṭṭhaselā.
::

::hangnum
954\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:2.0239} iṭṭhakā honti silā cirena {note:cirenapi (sī. pī.)}, na tattha sañjāyati ayo na lohaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaññañca etaṃ parivaṇṇayantā, cityā katā yaññakarehi māhu.
::

::hangnum
955\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjhāyakaṃ mantaguṇūpapannaṃ, tapassinaṃ yācayogotidhāhu;
::

::gathalast
Tīre samuddassudakaṃ sajantaṃ, taṃ sāgarojjhohari tenapeyyo.
::

::hangnum
956\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Parosahassampi samantavede, mantūpapanne nadiyo vahanti;
::

::gathalast
Na tena byāpannarasūdakā na, kasmā samuddo atulo apeyyo.
::

::hangnum
957\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye keci kūpā idha jīvaloke, loṇūdakā kūpakhaṇehi khātā;
::

::gathalast
Na brāhmaṇajjhoharaṇena {note:brāhmaṇajjhohari tena (ka.)} tesu, āpo {pb:T:2.0269} apeyyo dvirasaññu māhu.
::

::hangnum
958\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pure puratthā kā kassa bhariyā, mano manussaṃ ajanesi pubbe;
::

::gathalast
Tenāpi dhammena na koci hīno, evampi vossaggavibhaṅgamāhu {note:vossaggavibhāgamāhu (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
959\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Caṇḍālaputtopi adhicca vede, bhāseyya mante kusalo matīmā {note:mutīmā (sī. pī.)};

::gathalast
Na tassa muddhāpi phaleyya sattadhā, mantā ime attavadhāya katā {note:katta (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
960\.

::gatha1

::gathalast
Bālāna cittaṃ visame niviṭṭhaṃ, tadappapaññā abhisaddahanti.

::hangnum
961\.

::gathalast

::hangnum
962\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
963\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
964\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Lābho alābho ayaso yaso ca, sabbeva tesaṃ catunnañca {note:sabbe te sabbesaṃ catunna (sī. pī.)} dhammā.
::

::hangnum
965\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Tevijjasaṅghā ca tatheva ajja, kammāni karonti {note:kārenti (sī. syā. pī.)} puthū pathabyā.
::

::hangnum
966\.

::

::gathalast
Kammāni karonti {note:kārenti (sī. syā. pī.)} puthū pathabyā, tadappapaññā dvirasaññurā te’’.

::hangnum
967\.

::gatha1

Kañcanamaṇidaṇḍāni {note:tapaññamaṇidaṇḍāni (sī. pī.), suvaṇṇamaṇidaṇḍāni (syā. ka.)}, caranti dubhato mukhaṃ.

973\.

::hangnum
974\.

975\.

::hangnum
976\.

977\.

::gathalast
Ko {pb:T:2.0272} so odātapāvāro, jayaṃ indova sobhati.

979\.

::gatha1

Ko so parisamogayha, īsaṃ khaggaṃ pamuñcati {note:īso khaggaṃva muñcati (sī. pī.), bhante khaggaṃ pamuñcati (syā.)}.

::hangnum

Ko so omuñcate pādā, namo katvā mahesino’’.

::hangnum
981\.

::gatha1

::centre
Bhūridattajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 544. Candakumārajātakaṃ (7)

::hangnum
982\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājāsi luddakammo, ekarājā pupphavatīyā;
::

::gathalast
So pucchi brahmabandhuṃ, khaṇḍahālaṃ purohitaṃ mūḷhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
983\.
::

::gatha1
‘Saggāna maggamācikkha {note:saggamaggamācikkha (sī. pī.)}, tvaṃsi brāhmaṇa dhammavinayakusalo;
::

::gathalast
Yathā ito vajanti sugatiṃ, narā puññāni katvāna’.
::

::hangnum
984\.
::

::gatha1
‘Atidānaṃ daditvāna, avajjhe {pb:T:2.0273} deva ghātetvā;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ vajanti sugatiṃ, narā puññāni katvāna’.
::

::hangnum
985\.
::

::gatha1
‘Kiṃ pana taṃ atidānaṃ, ke ca avajjhā imasmi lokasmiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etañca kho no akkhāhi, yajissāmi dadāmi {note:yajissāma dadāma (sī. pī.)} dānāni’.
::

::hangnum
986\.
::

::gatha1
‘Puttehi deva yajitabbaṃ, mahesīhi negamehi ca;
::

::gathalast
Usabhehi ājāniyehi catūhi, sabbacatukkena deva yajitabbaṃ’’’.
::

::hangnum
987\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ sutvā antepure, kumārā mahesiyo ca haññantu;
::

::gathalast
Eko ahosi nigghoso, bhismā accuggato saddo’’.
::

::hangnum
988\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gacchatha vadetha kumāre, candaṃ sūriyañca bhaddasenañca;
::

::gathalast
Sūrañca vāmagottañca, pacurā {note:pasurā (sī. pī. ka.)} kira hotha yaññatthāya.
::

::hangnum
989\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kumāriyopi vadetha, upasenaṃ {pb:T:2.0274} {note:upaseniṃ (sī.), upaseṇiṃ (pī.)} kokilañca muditañca;
::

::gathalast
Nandañcāpi kumāriṃ, pacurā {note:pasurā (sī. pī. ka.)} kira hotha yaññatthāya.
::

::hangnum
990\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vijayampi mayhaṃ mahesiṃ, erāvatiṃ {note:ekapatiṃ (pī.), erāpatiṃ (ka.)} kesiniṃ sunandañca;
::

::gathalast
Lakkhaṇavarūpapannā, pacurā kira hotha yaññatthāya.
::

::hangnum
991\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gahapatayo {pb:V:2.0174}{pb:M:2.0243} ca vadetha, puṇṇamukhaṃ bhaddiyaṃ siṅgālañca;
::

::gathalast
Vaḍḍhañcāpi gahapatiṃ, pacurā kira hotha yaññatthāya’’.
::

::hangnum
992\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te tattha gahapatayo, avocisuṃ samāgatā puttadāraparikiṇṇā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbeva sikhino deva karohi, atha vā no dāse sāvehi’’.
::

::hangnum
993\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhayaṃkarampi me hatthiṃ, nāḷāgiriṃ accuggataṃ varuṇadantaṃ {note:nāḷāgiriṃ accutaṃ varuṇadantaṃ (sī.), rājagiriṃ accutavaruṇadantaṃ (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Ānetha kho ne khippaṃ, yaññatthāya bhavissanti.
::

::hangnum
994\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assaratanampi {note:assatarampi (sī. pī.), assaratanampi me (syā.)} kesiṃ, surāmukhaṃ puṇṇakaṃ vinatakañca;
::

::gathalast
Ānetha kho ne khippaṃ, yaññatthāya bhavissanti.
::

::hangnum
995\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Usabhampi {pb:T:2.0275} {note:usabhampi me (syā.)} yūthapatiṃ anojaṃ, nisabhaṃ gavampatiṃ tepi mayhaṃ ānetha;
::

::gathalast
Samūha {note:samupā (sī. pī.), sammukhā (syā.)} karontu sabbaṃ, yajissāmi dadāmi dānāni.
::

::hangnum
996\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbaṃ {note:sabbampi (syā.)} paṭiyādetha, yaññaṃ pana uggatamhi sūriyamhi;
::

::gathalast
Āṇāpetha ca kumāre {note:āṇāpetha candakumāre (syā. ka.)}, abhiramantu imaṃ rattiṃ.
::

::hangnum
997\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbaṃ {note:sabbampi (syā.)} upaṭṭhapetha, yaññaṃ pana uggatamhi sūriyamhi;
::

::gathalast
Vadetha dāni kumāre, ajja kho {note:vo (pī.)} pacchimā ratti’’.
::

::hangnum
998\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃtaṃ mātā avaca, rodantī āgantvā vimānato;
::

::gathalast
Yañño kira te putta, bhavissati catūhi puttehi’’.
::

::hangnum
999\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbepi mayhaṃ puttā cattā, candasmiṃ haññamānasmiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Puttehi yaññaṃ yajitvāna, sugatiṃ saggaṃ gamissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
1000\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā taṃ {note:mā (sī. pī.)} putta saddahesi, sugati kira hoti puttayaññena;
::

::gathalast
Nirayāneso maggo, neso maggo hi saggānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1001\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dānāni {pb:M:2.0244} dehi koṇḍañña, ahiṃsā sabbabhūtabhabyānaṃ’’;
::

::gathalast
Esa maggo sugatiyā, na ca maggo puttayaññena’’.
::

::hangnum
1002\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ācariyānaṃ {pb:T:2.0276} vacanā, ghātessaṃ candañca sūriyañca;
::

::gathalast
Puttehi yaññaṃ {note:puttehi (sī. syā. pī.)} yajitvāna duccajehi, sugatiṃ saggaṃ gamissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
1003\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃtaṃ pitāpi avaca, vasavattī orasaṃ sakaṃ puttaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yañño kira te putta, bhavissati catūhi puttehi’’.
::

::hangnum
1004\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbepi mayhaṃ puttā cattā, candasmiṃ haññamānasmiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Puttehi yaññaṃ yajitvāna, sugatiṃ saggaṃ gamissāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
1005\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā taṃ putta saddahesi, sugati kira hoti puttayaññena;
::

::gathalast
Nirayāneso maggo, neso maggo hi saggānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1006\.
::

::gatha1

‘‘Ummattikā bhavissāmi, bhūnahatā paṃsunā ca {note:paṃsunāva (syā. ka.)} parikiṇṇā;
::

::gathalast
Sace candavaraṃ {note:candakumāraṃ (syā.)} hanti, pāṇā me deva rujjhanti {note:nirujjhanti (sī.), bhijjanti (syā.)}.

::gathalast

::

::gathalast
Candasūriyesu naccantiyo, samā tāsaṃ na vijjati’’.

#### 545. Mahānāradakassapajātakaṃ (8)

::hangnum
1153\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahu {pb:V:2.0186}{pb:M:2.0257} rājā videhānaṃ, aṅgati {note:aṅgāti (sī.) evamuparipi} nāma khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Pahūtayoggo dhanimā, anantabalaporiso.
::

::hangnum
1154\.
::

::gatha1
So ca pannarasiṃ {note:pannarase (syā. ka.)} rattiṃ, purimayāme anāgate;
::

::gathalast
Cātumāsā {note:cātumassa (sī. pī.)} komudiyā, amacce sannipātayi.
::

::hangnum
1155\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṇḍite sutasampanne, mitapubbe {note:mihitapubbe (sī. pī.)} vicakkhaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Vijayañca sunāmañca, senāpatiṃ alātakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1156\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamanupucchi vedeho, ‘‘paccekaṃ brūtha saṃ ruciṃ;
::

::gatha2
Cātumāsā komudajja, juṇhaṃ byapahataṃ {note:byapagataṃ (sī. pī.)} tamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāyajja ratiyā rattiṃ, viharemu imaṃ utuṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1157\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato senāpati rañño, alāto etadabravi;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Haṭṭhaṃ yoggaṃ balaṃ sabbaṃ, senaṃ sannāhayāmase.
::

::hangnum
1158\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Niyyāma deva yuddhāya, anantabalaporisā;
::

::gatha2
Ye te vasaṃ na āyanti, vasaṃ upanayāmase {note:upaniyyāmase (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Esā mayhaṃ sakā diṭṭhi, ajitaṃ ojināmase.
::

::hangnum
1159\.
::

::gatha1
Alātassa {pb:T:2.0293} vaco sutvā, sunāmo etadabravi;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Sabbe tuyhaṃ mahārāja, amittā vasamāgatā.
::

::hangnum
1160\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nikkhittasatthā paccatthā, nivātamanuvattare;
::

::gathalast
Uttamo ussavo ajja, na yuddhaṃ mama ruccati.
::

::hangnum
1161\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Annapānañca khajjañca, khippaṃ abhiharantu te;
::

::gathalast
Ramassu deva kāmehi, naccagīte suvādite’’.
::

::hangnum
1162\.
::

::gatha1
Sunāmassa vaco sutvā, vijayo etadabravi;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Sabbe kāmā mahārāja, niccaṃ tava mupaṭṭhitā.
::

::hangnum
1163\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hete dullabhā deva, tava kāmehi modituṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sadāpi kāmā sulabhā, netaṃ cittamataṃ {note:cittaṃ matī (ka.)} mama.
::

::hangnum
1164\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samaṇaṃ {pb:M:2.0258} brāhmaṇaṃ vāpi, upāsemu bahussutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yo najja vinaye kaṅkhaṃ, atthadhammavidū ise’’.
::

::hangnum
1165\.
::

::gatha1
Vijayassa vaco sutvā, rājā aṅgati mabravi;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Yathā vijayo bhaṇati, mayhampetaṃva ruccati.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::gathalast
Yo {note:ko (sī. pī.)} najja vinaye kaṅkhaṃ, atthadhammavidū ise’’.

1169\.

::gathalast
Taṃ deva {note:tadeva (ka.)} payirupāsemu {note:payirupāsaya (sī. pī.)}, so no kaṅkhaṃ vinessati’’.

::hangnum
1170\.

::gatha1

::hangnum

Upamāya {pb:T:2.0302} midhekacce, atthaṃ jānanti paṇḍitā.

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Sañchinnagattaṃ ruhiraṃ savantaṃ, ko codaye paraloke sahassaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1322\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:M:2.0273} nikkhantamattaṃ taṃ, asipattācitā dumā {note:asipattanirayā dukhā (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sampatitaṃ vetaraṇiṃ, ko taṃ yāceyya taṃ dhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1323\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kharā kharodakā {note:khārodikā (sī.), kharodikā (pī.)} tattā, duggā vetaraṇī nadī;
::

::gathalast
Ayopokkharasañchannā, tikkhā pattehi sandati.
::

::hangnum
1324\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha {pb:T:2.0313} sañchinnagattaṃ taṃ, vuyhantaṃ ruhiramakkhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vetaraññe anālambe, ko taṃ yāceyya taṃ dhanaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1325\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vedhāmi {pb:V:2.0198} rukkho viya chijjamāno, disaṃ na jānāmi pamūḷhasañño;
::

::gathalast
Bhayānutappāmi mahā ca me bhayā, sutvāna kathā {note:gāthā (sī. syā. pī.)} tava bhāsitā ise.
::

::hangnum
1326\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āditte vārimajjhaṃva, dīpaṃvoghe mahaṇṇave;
::

::gathalast
Andhakāreva pajjoto, tvaṃ nosi saraṇaṃ ise.
::

::hangnum
1327\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthañca dhammaṃ anusāsa maṃ ise, atītamaddhā aparādhitaṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Ācikkha me nārada suddhimaggaṃ, yathā ahaṃ no nirayaṃ pateyyaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1328\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā ahu dhataraṭṭho ( ) {note:ettha kiñci ūnaṃ viya dissati}, vessāmitto aṭṭhako yāmataggi;
::

::gathalast
Usindaro cāpi sivī ca rājā, paricārakā samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1329\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ete caññe ca rājāno, ye saggavisayaṃ {note:sakkavisayaṃ (sī. pī.)} gatā;
::

::gathalast
Adhammaṃ parivajjetvā, dhammaṃ cara mahīpati.
::

::hangnum
1330\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Annahatthā ca te byamhe, ghosayantu pure tava;
::

::gatha2
Ko chāto ko ca tasito, ko mālaṃ ko vilepanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānārattānaṃ vatthānaṃ, ko naggo paridahissati.
::

::hangnum
1331\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko {pb:T:2.0314}{pb:M:2.0274} panthe chattamāneti {note:chatta’mādeti (sī. syā. pī.)}, pādukā ca mudū subhā;
::

::gathalast
Iti sāyañca pāto ca, ghosayantu pure tava.
::

::hangnum
1332\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jiṇṇaṃ posaṃ gavassañca, māssu yuñja yathā pure;
::

::gathalast
Parihārañca dajjāsi, adhikārakato balī.
::

::hangnum
1333\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāyo te rathasaññāto, manosārathiko lahu;
::

::gathalast
Avihiṃsāsāritakkho, saṃvibhāgapaṭicchado.
::

::hangnum
1334\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pādasaññamanemiyo, hatthasaññamapakkharo;
::

::gathalast
Kucchisaññamanabbhanto, vācāsaññamakūjano.
::

::hangnum
1335\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saccavākyasamattaṅgo, apesuññasusaññato;
::

::gathalast
Girāsakhilanelaṅgo, mitabhāṇisilesito.
::

::hangnum
1336\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhālobhasusaṅkhāro, nivātañjalikubbaro;
::

::gathalast
Athaddhatānatīsāko {note:atthaddhatānatīsāko (sī. pī.)}, sīlasaṃvaranandhano.
::

::hangnum
1337\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkodhanamanugghātī, dhammapaṇḍarachattako;
::

::gathalast
Bāhusaccamapālambo, ṭhitacittamupādhiyo {note:dhiticittamupādhiyo (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
1338\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kālaññutācittasāro, vesārajjatidaṇḍako;
::

::gathalast
Nivātavuttiyottako {note:nivātavuttiyottaṅgo (ka.)}, anatimānayugo lahu.
::

::hangnum
1339\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Alīnacittasanthāro{pb:V:2.0199}, vuddhisevī rajohato;
::

::gathalast
Sati patodo dhīrassa, dhiti yogo ca rasmiyo.
::

::hangnum
1340\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mano dantaṃ pathaṃ neti {note:patha’nveti (sī. pī.)}, samadantehi vāhibhi;
::

::gathalast
Icchā {pb:T:2.0315} lobho ca kummaggo, ujumaggo ca saṃyamo.
::

::hangnum
1341\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rūpe sadde rase gandhe, vāhanassa padhāvato;
::

::gathalast
Paññā ākoṭanī rāja, tattha attāva sārathi.
::

::hangnum
1342\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace etena yānena, samacariyā daḷhā dhiti;
::

::gathalast
Sabbakāmaduho rāja, na jātu nirayaṃ vaje’’.
::

::hangnum
1343\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Alāto {pb:M:2.0275} devadattosi, sunāmo āsi bhaddaji;
::

::gathalast
Vijayo sāriputtosi, moggallānosi bījako.
::

::hangnum
1344\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sunakkhatto licchaviputto, guṇo āsi acelako;
::

::gathalast
Ānando sā rucā āsi, yā rājānaṃ pasādayi.
::

::hangnum
1345\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ūruveḷakassapo rājā, pāpadiṭṭhi tadā ahu;
::

::gathalast
Mahābrahmā bodhisatto, evaṃ dhāretha jātaka’’nti.
::

::centre
Mahānāradakassapajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 546. Vidhurajātakaṃ (9)

#### Dohaḷakaṇḍaṃ

::hangnum
1346\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṇḍu kisiyāsi dubbalā, vaṇṇarūpaṃ {note:vaṇṇarūpe (ka.)} natavedisaṃ pure;
::

::gathalast
Vimale akkhāhi pucchitā, kīdisī tuyhaṃ sarīravedanā’’.
::

::hangnum
1347\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammo manujesu mātīnaṃ {note:mātinaṃ (sī. pī.)}, dohaḷo nāma janinda vuccati;
::

::gathalast
Dhammāhataṃ {pb:T:2.0316} nāgakuñjara, vidhurassa hadayābhipatthaye’’.
::

::hangnum
1348\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Candaṃ kho tvaṃ dohaḷāyasi, sūriyaṃ vā atha vāpi mālutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dullabhañhi {note:dullabhe (sī. pī.)} vidhurassa dassanaṃ {note:dassane (sī. pī.)}, ko vidhuramidha mānayissati’’.
::

::hangnum
1349\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kinnu tāta tuvaṃ pajjhāyasi, padumaṃ hatthagataṃva te mukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kinnu dummanarūposi issara, mā tvaṃ soci amittatāpana’’.
::

::hangnum
1350\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mātā {pb:V:2.0200}{pb:M:2.0276} hi tava irandhati {note:irandati (sī. syā. pī.)}, vidhurassa hadayaṃ dhaniyati;
::

::gathalast
Dullabhañhi vidhurassa dassanaṃ, ko vidhuramidha mānayissati’’.
::

::hangnum
1351\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa bhattupariyesanaṃ {note:bhattupariyesanaṃ (sī. pī.)} cara, yo vidhuramidha mānayissati’’;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Pituno ca sā sutvāna vākyaṃ, rattiṃ nikkhamma avassutiṃ cari’’.
::

::hangnum
1352\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ke gandhabbe rakkhase ca nāge, ke kimpurise cāpi mānuse;
::

::gathalast
Ke {pb:T:2.0317} paṇḍite sabbakāmadade {note:sabbakāmade (sī. pī.)}, dīgharattaṃ bhattā me bhavissati’’.
::

::hangnum
1353\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assāsa hessāmi te pati, bhattā te hessāmi anindalocane;
::

::gathalast
Paññā hi mamaṃ tathāvidhā, assāsa hessasi bhariyā mama.
::

::hangnum
1354\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avacāsi puṇṇakaṃ irandhatī {note:irandatī (sī. pī.)}, pubbapathānugatena cetasā;
::

::gathalast
Ehi gacchāma pitu mamantike {note:pitu mama santikaṃ (ka.)}, esova te etamatthaṃ pavakkhati.
::

::hangnum
1355\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Alaṅkatā suvasanā, mālinī candanussadā;
::

::gathalast
Yakkhaṃ hatthe gahetvāna, pitusantikupāgami’’.
::

::hangnum
1356\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāgavara vaco suṇohi me, patirūpaṃ paṭipajja suṅkiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Patthemi ahaṃ irandhatiṃ, tāya samaṅgiṃ karohi maṃ tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1357\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sataṃ hatthī sataṃ assā, sataṃ assatarīrathā;
::

::gatha2
Sataṃ valabhiyo puṇṇā, nānāratnassa kevalā;
::

::gathalast
Te nāga paṭipajjassu, dhītaraṃ dehirandhatiṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1358\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāva {pb:T:2.0318}{pb:M:2.0277} āmantaye ñātī, mitte ca suhadajjane {note:suhadaṃjanaṃ (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Anāmanta kataṃ kammaṃ, taṃ pacchā anutappati’’.
::

::hangnum
1359\.
::

::gatha1
Tato so varuṇo nāgo, pavisitvā nivesanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhariyaṃ āmantayitvāna, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
1360\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayaṃ so puṇṇako yakkho, yācatī maṃ irandhatiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bahunā vittalābhena, tassa dema piyaṃ mamaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1361\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na dhanena na vittena, labbhā amhaṃ irandhatī;
::

::gatha2
Sace ca kho hadayaṃ paṇḍitassa, dhammena laddhā idha māhareyya;
::

::gathalast
Etena vittena kumāri labbhā, nāññaṃ dhanaṃ uttari patthayāma’’.
::

::hangnum
1362\.
::

::gatha1
Tato so varuṇo nāgo, nikkhamitvā nivesanā;
::

::gathalast
Puṇṇakāmantayitvāna, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
1363\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:2.0201} dhanena na vittena, labbhā amhaṃ irandhatī;
::

::gatha2
Sace tuvaṃ hadayaṃ paṇḍitassa, dhammena laddhā idha māharesi;
::

::gathalast
Etena vittena kumāri labbhā, nāññaṃ dhanaṃ uttari patthayāma’’.
::

::hangnum
1364\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ paṇḍitotyeke vadanti loke, tameva bāloti punāhu aññe;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi {pb:T:2.0319} me vippavadanti ettha, kaṃ paṇḍitaṃ nāga tuvaṃ vadesi’’.
::

::hangnum
1365\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Korabyarājassa dhanañcayassa {note:dhanañjayassa (sī. syā. pī.)}, yadi te suto vidhuro nāma kattā;
::

::gathalast
Ānehi taṃ paṇḍitaṃ dhammaladdhā, irandhatī padacarā {note:paddhacarā (sī. pī.), paṭṭhacarā (syā. ka.)} te hotu.
::

::hangnum
1366\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idañca sutvā varuṇassa vākyaṃ, uṭṭhāya yakkho paramappatīto;
::

::gathalast
Tattheva santo purisaṃ asaṃsi, ānehi ājaññamidheva yuttaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1367\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātarūpamayā {pb:M:2.0278} kaṇṇā, kācamhicamayā {note:kācamhamayā (sī.), kācambhamayā (pī.)} khurā;
::

::gathalast
Jambonadassa pākassa, suvaṇṇassa uracchado’’.
::

::hangnum
1368\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devavāhavahaṃ yānaṃ, assamāruyha puṇṇako;
::

::gathalast
Alaṅkato kappitakesamassu, pakkāmi vehāyasamantalikkhe {note:antalikkhaṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
1369\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So puṇṇako kāmarāgena {note:kāmavegena (sī. pī.)} giddho, irandhatiṃ nāgakaññaṃ jigīsaṃ {note:jigiṃsaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Gantvāna taṃ bhūtapatiṃ yasassiṃ, iccabravī vessavaṇaṃ kuveraṃ.
::

::hangnum
1370\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhogavatī nāma mandire, vāsā {pb:T:2.0320} hiraññavatīti vuccati;
::

::gathalast
Nagare nimmite kañcanamaye, maṇḍalassa uragassa niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1371\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṭṭālakā oṭṭhagīviyo, lohitaṅkassa masāragallino;
::

::gathalast
Pāsādettha silāmayā, sovaṇṇaratanehi chāditā.
::

::hangnum
1372\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ambā tilakā ca jambuyo, sattapaṇṇā mucalindaketakā;
::

::gathalast
Piyaṅgu {note:piyakā (sī. pī.), piyaṅgukā (syā.)} uddālakā sahā, uparibhaddakā sinduvārakā {note:bhinduvāritā (syā. pī.), bhindhavāritā (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
1373\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Campeyyakā nāgamallikā, bhaginīmālā atha mettha koliyā;
::

::gathalast
Ete dumā pariṇāmitā, sobhayanti uragassa mandiraṃ {note:mandire (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
1374\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khajjurettha {pb:M:2.0279} silāmayā, sovaṇṇadhuvapupphitā bahū;
::

::gathalast
Yattha vasato papātiko, nāgarājā varuṇo mahiddhiko.
::

::hangnum
1375\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa komārikā bhariyā, vimalā kañcanavelliviggahā;
::

::gathalast
Kālā {pb:T:2.0321} taruṇāva uggatā, pucimandatthanī cārudassanā.
::

::hangnum
1376\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lākhārasarattasucchavī{pb:V:2.0202}, kaṇikārāva nivātapupphitā {note:kaṇikārova nivātapupphito (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tidivokacarāva accharā, vijjuvabbhaghanā vinissaṭā.
::

::hangnum
1377\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sā dohaḷinī suvimhitā, vidhurassa hadayaṃ dhaniyati;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ tesaṃ demi issara, tena te denti irandhatiṃ mamaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1378\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So puṇṇako bhūtapatiṃ yasassiṃ, āmantaya vessavaṇaṃ kuveraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tattheva santo {note:santaṃ (pī.)} purisaṃ asaṃsi, ānehi ājaññamidheva yuttaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1379\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātarūpamayā kaṇṇā, kācamhicamayā khurā;
::

::gathalast
Jambonadassa pākassa, suvaṇṇassa uracchado.
::

::hangnum
1380\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devavāhavahaṃ yānaṃ, assamāruyha puṇṇako;
::

::gathalast
Alaṅkato kappitakesamassu, pakkāmi vehāyasamantalikkhe’’.
::

::hangnum
1381\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So {pb:M:2.0280} aggamā rājagahaṃ surammaṃ, aṅgassa {pb:T:2.0322} rañño nagaraṃ durāyutaṃ {note:durāsadaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Pahūtabhakkhaṃ bahuannapānaṃ, masakkasāraṃ viya vāsavassa.
::

::hangnum
1382\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mayūrakoñcāgaṇasampaghuṭṭhaṃ, dijābhighuṭṭhaṃ dijasaṅghasevitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānāsakuntābhirudaṃ suvaṅgaṇaṃ {note:subhaṅgaṇaṃ (sī. pī.)}, pupphābhikiṇṇaṃ himavaṃva pabbataṃ.
::

::hangnum
1383\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So puṇṇako vepulamābhirūhi {note:vepullamābhirucchi (sī. pī.)}, siluccayaṃ kimpurisānuciṇṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anvesamāno maṇiratanaṃ uḷāraṃ, tamaddasā pabbatakūṭamajjhe.
::

::hangnum
1384\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvā maṇiṃ pabhassaraṃ jātimantaṃ {note:jātivantaṃ (sī. syā.)}, manoharaṃ {note:dhanāharaṃ (sī. pī. ka.)} maṇiratanaṃ uḷāraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Daddallamānaṃ yasasā yasassinaṃ, obhāsatī vijjurivantalikkhe.
::

::hangnum
1385\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamaggahī veḷuriyaṃ mahagghaṃ, manoharaṃ nāma mahānubhāvaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ājaññamāruyha manomavaṇṇo, pakkāmi vehāyasamantalikkhe.
::

::hangnum
1386\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So {pb:T:2.0323} aggamā {note:agamā (syā. pī. ka.)} nagaramindapatthaṃ, oruyhupāgacchi sabhaṃ kurūnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samāgate ekasataṃ samagge, avhettha yakkho avikampamāno.
::

::hangnum
1387\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko nīdha raññaṃ varamābhijeti, kamābhijeyyāma varaddhanena {note:varaṃdhanena (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Kamanuttaraṃ ratanavaraṃ jināma, ko vāpi no jeti varaddhanena’’.
::

::hangnum
1388\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuhiṃ {pb:M:2.0281} nu raṭṭhe tava jātibhūmi, na korabyasseva vaco tavedaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abhītosi {note:abhibhosi (sī. pī.)} no vaṇṇanibhāya sabbe, akkhāhi me nāmañca bandhave ca’’.
::

::hangnum
1389\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaccāyano māṇavakosmi rāja, anūnanāmo iti mavhayanti;
::

::gathalast
Aṅgesu me ñātayo bandhavā ca, akkhena devasmi idhānupatto’’.
::

::hangnum
1390\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ māṇavassa ratanāni atthi, ye taṃ jinanto hare akkhadhutto;
::

::gathalast
Bahūni rañño ratanāni atthi, te tvaṃ daliddo kathamavhayesi’’.
::

::hangnum
1391\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Manoharo {pb:T:2.0324}{pb:V:2.0203} nāma maṇī mamāyaṃ, manoharaṃ maṇiratanaṃ uḷāraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Imañca ājaññamamittatāpanaṃ, etaṃ me jinitvā hare akkhadhutto’’.
::

::hangnum
1392\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Eko maṇī māṇava kiṃ karissati, ājāniyeko pana kiṃ karissati;
::

::gathalast
Bahūni rañño maṇiratanāni atthi, ājāniyā vātajavā anappakā’’.
::

::centre
Dohaḷakaṇḍaṃ nāma.
::

#### Maṇikaṇḍaṃ

::hangnum
1393\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idañca me maṇiratanaṃ, passa tvaṃ dvipaduttama;
::

::gathalast
Itthīnaṃ viggahā cettha, purisānañca viggahā.
::

::hangnum
1394\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Migānaṃ viggahā cettha, sakuṇānañca viggahā;
::

::gathalast

#### Akkhakaṇḍaṃ

::hangnum
1434\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upāgataṃ rāja mupehi lakkhaṃ, netādisaṃ maṇiratanaṃ tavatthi;
::

::gathalast
Dhammena jissāma {note:jiyyāma (sī. syā. pī.)} asāhasena, jito ca no khippamavākarohi.
::

::hangnum
1435\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcāla {pb:T:2.0329} -paccuggata-sūrasena, macchā {note:majjhā (ka.)} ca maddā saha kekakebhi;
::

::gathalast
Passantu note asaṭhena yuddhaṃ, na no sabhāyaṃ na karonti kiñci’’.
::

::hangnum
1436\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te pāvisuṃ akkhamadena mattā, rājā kurūnaṃ puṇṇako cāpi yakkho;
::

::gathalast
Rājā kaliṃ viccinamaggahesi, kaṭaṃ aggahī puṇṇako nāma yakkho.
::

::hangnum
1437\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te tattha jūte ubhaye samāgate, raññaṃ sakāse sakhīnañca majjhe;
::

::gathalast
Ajesi yakkho naravīraseṭṭhaṃ, tatthappanādo tumulo babhūva’’.
::

::hangnum
1438\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jayo mahārāja parājayo ca, āyūhataṃ aññatarassa hoti;
::

::gathalast
Janinda jīnosi {note:jinnosi (syā.), jitosi (pī.) jinomhi (ka.)} varaddhanena, jito ca me khippamavākarohi’’.
::

::hangnum
1439\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthī {pb:M:2.0286} gavassā maṇikuṇḍalā ca, yañcāpi mayhaṃ {note:aññaṃ (ka.)} ratanaṃ pathabyā;
::

::gathalast
Gaṇhāhi kaccāna varaṃ dhanānaṃ, ādāya {pb:T:2.0330} yenicchasi tena gaccha’’.
::

::hangnum
1440\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthī gavassā maṇikuṇḍalā ca, yañcāpi tuyhaṃ ratanaṃ pathabyā;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ varo vidhuro nāma kattā, so me jito taṃ me avākarohi’’.
::

::hangnum
1441\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Attā ca me so saraṇaṃ gatī ca, dīpo ca leṇo ca parāyaṇo ca;
::

::gathalast
Asantuleyyo mama so dhanena, pāṇena me sādiso esa kattā’’.
::

::hangnum
1442\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ciraṃ vivādo mama tuyhañcassa, kāmañca pucchāma tameva gantvā;
::

::gathalast
Esova no vivaratu etamatthaṃ, yaṃ vakkhatī hotu kathā {note:tathā (syā. ka.)} ubhinnaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1443\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, na ca māṇava sāhasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tameva gantvā pucchāma, tena tussāmubho janā’’.
::

::hangnum
1444\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saccaṃ nu devā vidahū kurūnaṃ, dhamme ṭhitaṃ vidhuraṃ nāmamaccaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dāsosi rañño uda vāsi ñāti, vidhuroti saṅkhā katamāsi loke’’.
::

::hangnum
1445\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āmāyadāsāpi {pb:V:2.0207} bhavanti heke, dhanena {pb:T:2.0331} kītāpi bhavanti dāsā;
::

::gathalast
Sayampi heke upayanti dāsā, bhayā paṇunnāpi bhavanti dāsā.
::

::hangnum
1446\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ete {pb:M:2.0287} narānaṃ caturova dāsā, addhā hi yonito ahampi jāto;
::

::gatha2
Bhavo ca rañño abhavo ca rañño, dāsāhaṃ devassa parampi gantvā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammena maṃ māṇava tuyha dajjā’’.
::

::hangnum
1447\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayaṃ {note:ayampi (syā. ka.)} dutīyo vijayo mamajja, puṭṭho hi kattā vivarettha {note:vivarittha (sī. syā. ka.)} pañhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Adhammarūpo vata rājaseṭṭho, subhāsitaṃ nānujānāsi mayhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1448\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ ce no so vivarettha pañhaṃ, dāsohamasmi na ca khosmi ñāti;
::

::gatha2
Gaṇhāhi kaccāna varaṃ dhanānaṃ, ādāya yenicchasi tena gaccha’’.
::

::centre
Akkhakaṇḍaṃ nāma.

#### Gharāvāsapañhā

::hangnum
1449\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vidhura vasamānāssa, gahaṭṭhassa sakaṃ gharaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khemā vutti kathaṃ assa, kathannu assa saṅgaho.
::

::hangnum
1450\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abyābajjhaṃ {note:abyāpajjhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} kathaṃ assa, saccavādī ca māṇavo;
::

::gathalast
Asmā {pb:T:2.0332} lokā paraṃ lokaṃ, kathaṃ pecca na socati’’.
::

::hangnum
1451\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ tattha gatimā dhitimā, matimā atthadassimā;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkhātā {note:saṅkhāto (ka.)} sabbadhammānaṃ, vidhuro etadabravi.
::

::hangnum
1452\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na sādhāraṇadārassa, na bhuñje sādumekako;
::

::gathalast
Na seve lokāyatikaṃ, netaṃ paññāya vaḍḍhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1453\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīlavā vattasampanno, appamatto vicakkhaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Nivātavutti atthaddho, surato sakhilo mudu.
::

::hangnum
1454\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅgahetā {pb:M:2.0288} ca mittānaṃ, saṃvibhāgī vidhānavā;
::

::gathalast
Tappeyya annapānena, sadā samaṇabrāhmaṇe.
::

::hangnum
1455\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammakāmo sutādhāro, bhaveyya paripucchako;
::

::gathalast
Sakkaccaṃ payirupāseyya, sīlavante bahussute.
::

::hangnum
1456\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gharamāvasamānassa, gahaṭṭhassa sakaṃ gharaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khemā vutti siyā evaṃ, evaṃ nu assa saṅgaho.
::

::hangnum
1457\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abyābajjhaṃ {pb:V:2.0208} siyā evaṃ, saccavādī ca māṇavo;
::

::gathalast
Asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ, evaṃ pecca na socati’’.
::

::centre
Gharāvāsapañhā nāma.
::

::centre
Lakkhaṇakaṇḍaṃ
::

::hangnum
1458\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ehi dāni gamissāma, dinno no issarena me;
::

::gathalast
Mamevatthaṃ {note:tamevatthaṃ (pī.)} paṭipajja, esa dhammo sanantano’’.
::

::hangnum
1459\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jānāmi māṇava tayāhamasmi, dinnohamasmi tava issarena;
::

::gathalast
Tīhañca {pb:T:2.0333} taṃ vāsayemu agāre, yenaddhunā anusāsemu putte’’.
::

::hangnum
1460\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ me tathā hotu vasemu tīhaṃ, kurutaṃ bhavajja gharesu kiccaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anusāsataṃ puttadāre bhavajja, yathā tayī pecca {note:pacchā (sī. pī.)} sukhī bhaveyya’’.
::

::hangnum
1461\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sādhūti vatvāna pahūtakāmo, pakkāmi yakkho vidhurena saddhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ kuñjarājaññahayānuciṇṇaṃ, pāvekkhi antepuramariyaseṭṭho’’.
::

::hangnum
1462\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Koñcaṃ mayūrañca piyañca ketaṃ, upāgami tattha surammarūpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pahūtabhakkhaṃ bahuannapānaṃ, masakkasāraṃ viya vāsavassa’’.
::

::hangnum
1463\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha {pb:M:2.0289} naccanti gāyanti, avhāyanti varāvaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Accharā viya devesu, nāriyo samalaṅkatā.
::

::hangnum
1464\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samaṅgikatvā pamadāhi yakkhaṃ, annena pānena ca dhammapālo;
::

::gathalast
Atthattha {note:aggattha (syā. aṭṭha.)} mevānuvicintayanto, pāvekkhi bhariyāya tadā sakāse.
::

::hangnum
1465\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:T:2.0334} candanagandharasānulittaṃ, suvaṇṇajambonadanikkhasādisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhariyaṃvacā ehi suṇohi bhoti, puttāni āmantaya tambanette.
::

::hangnum
1466\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sutvāna vākyaṃ patino anujjā {note:anojā (syā. ka.)}, suṇisaṃvaca tambanakhiṃ sunettaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āmantaya vammadharāni cete, puttāni indīvarapupphasāme’’.
::

::hangnum
1467\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te āgate muddhani dhammapālo, cumbitvā putte avikampamāno;
::

::gathalast
Āmantayitvāna avoca vākyaṃ, dinnāhaṃ raññā idha māṇavassa.
::

::hangnum
1468\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassajjahaṃ attasukhī vidheyyo, ādāya yenicchati tena gacchati;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca vo sāsitumāgatosmi {note:anusāsituṃ āgatosmi (syā. ka.)}, kathaṃ ahaṃ aparittāya gacche.
::

::hangnum
1469\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace {pb:V:2.0209}{pb:M:2.0290} vo rājā kururaṭṭhavāsī {note:kurukhettavāsī (sī. pī.)}, janasandho puccheyya pahūtakāmo;
::

::gathalast
Kimābhijānātha pure purāṇaṃ, kiṃ vo pitā anusāse puratthā.
::

::hangnum
1470\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samāsanā {pb:T:2.0335} hotha mayāva sabbe, konīdha rañño abbhatiko manusso;
::

::gatha2
Tamañjaliṃ kariya vadetha evaṃ, mā hevaṃ deva na hi esa dhammo;
::

::gathalast
Viyaggharājassa nihīnajacco, samāsano deva kathaṃ bhaveyya’’.
::

::centre
Lakkhaṇakaṇḍaṃ {note:pekkhaṇakaṇḍaṃ (sī. ka.)} nāma.
::

#### Rājavasati

::hangnum
1471\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So ca putte {note:mitte (sī. pī.)} amacce ca, ñātayo suhadajjane;

#### Antarapeyyālaṃ

::hangnum
1518\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ samanusāsitvā, ñātisaṅghaṃ vicakkhaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Parikiṇṇo suhadehi, rājānamupasaṅkami.
::

::hangnum
1519\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vanditvā sirasā pāde, katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vidhuro avaca rājānaṃ, paggahetvāna añjaliṃ.
::

::hangnum
1520\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayaṃ maṃ māṇavo neti, kattukāmo {note:gantukāmo (ka.)} yathāmati;
::

::gathalast
Ñātīnatthaṃ pavakkhāmi, taṃ suṇohi arindama.
::

::hangnum
1521\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Putte {pb:V:2.0213} ca me udikkhesi, yañca maññaṃ ghare dhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yathā pecca {note:pacchā (syā. ka.)} na hāyetha, ñātisaṅgho mayī gate.
::

::hangnum
1522\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yatheva khalatī bhūmyā, bhūmyāyeva patiṭṭhati;
::

::gathalast
Evetaṃ khalitaṃ mayhaṃ, etaṃ passāmi accayaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1523\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakkā {pb:T:2.0341} na gantuṃ iti mayha hoti, chetvā {note:jhatvā (sī. pī.)} vadhitvā idha kātiyānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idheva hohī iti mayha ruccati, mā tvaṃ agā uttamabhūripañña’’.
::

::hangnum
1524\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā {pb:M:2.0295} hevadhammesu manaṃ paṇīdahi, atthe ca dhamme ca yutto bhavassu;
::

::gathalast
Dhiratthu kammaṃ akusalaṃ anariyaṃ, yaṃ katvā pacchā nirayaṃ vajeyya.
::

::hangnum
1525\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nevesa dhammo na puneta {note:puneti (syā. ka.)} kiccaṃ, ayiro hi dāsassa janinda issaro;
::

::gathalast
Ghātetuṃ jhāpetuṃ athopi hantuṃ, na ca mayha kodhatthi vajāmi cāhaṃ’’.

::hangnum
1526\.

::gatha1
‘‘Jeṭṭhaputtaṃ upaguyha, vineyya hadaye daraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Assupuṇṇehi nettehi, pāvisī so mahāgharaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1527\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sālāva sammapatitā {note:sampamathitā (sī. pī.)}, mālutena pamadditā;
::

::gathalast

1528\.

::gathalast

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

#### Sādhunaradhammakaṇḍaṃ

::hangnum
1549\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So {pb:V:2.0215} tattha gantvāna vicintayanto, uccāvacā cetanakā {note:cetanatā (ka.)} bhavanti;
::

::gathalast
Nayimassa jīvena mamatthi kiñci, hantvānimaṃ {pb:T:2.0345} hadayamānayissaṃ’’ {note:ādiyissaṃ (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
1550\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So tattha gantvā pabbatantarasmiṃ {note:pabbatapādasmiṃ (ka.)}, anto pavisitvāna paduṭṭhacitto;
::

::gathalast
Asaṃvutasmiṃ jagatippadese, adhosiraṃ dhārayi kātiyāno.
::

::hangnum
1551\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So lambamāno narake papāte, mahabbhaye lomahaṃse vidugge;
::

::gathalast
Asantasanto kurūnaṃ kattuseṭṭho, iccabravi puṇṇakaṃ nāma yakkhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1552\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ariyāvakāsosi {pb:M:2.0298} anariyarūpo, asaññato saññatasannikāso;
::

Accāhitaṃ kammaṃ karosi ludraṃ, bhāve ca te kusalaṃ natthi kiñci.

::hangnum
1553\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ maṃ papātasmiṃ papātumicchasi, ko nu tavattho maraṇena mayhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Amānusasseva tavajja vaṇṇo, ācikkha me tvaṃ katamāsi devatā’’.
::

::hangnum
1554\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadi te suto puṇṇako nāma yakkho, rañño kuverassa hi so sajibbo {note:sajīvo (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Bhūmindharo {pb:T:2.0346} varuṇo nāma nāgo, brahā sucī vaṇṇabalūpapanno.
::

::hangnum
1555\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassānujaṃ dhītaraṃ kāmayāmi, irandhatī nāma sā nāgakaññā;
::

::gathalast
Tassā sumajjhāya piyāya hetu, patārayiṃ tuyha vadhāya dhīra’’.
::

::hangnum
1556\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā heva tvaṃ {note:te (syā. ka.)} yakkha ahosi mūḷho, naṭṭhā bahū duggahītena loke {note:lokā (sī. syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ te sumajjhāya piyāya kiccaṃ, maraṇena me iṅgha suṇomi {note:suṇoma (sī. pī.)} sabbaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1557\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahānubhāvassa mahoragassa, dhītukāmo ñātibhato {note:ñātigato (pī.)} hamasmi;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ yācamānaṃ sasuro avoca, yathā mamaññiṃsu sukāmanītaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1558\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dajjemu {pb:M:2.0299} kho te sutanuṃ sunettaṃ, sucimhitaṃ candanalittagattaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sace tuvaṃ hadayaṃ paṇḍitassa, dhammena laddhā idha māharesi;
::

::gathalast
Etena vittena kumāri labbhā, naññaṃ dhanaṃ uttari patthayāma.
::

::hangnum
1559\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ {pb:T:2.0347} na mūḷhosmi suṇohi katte, na cāpi me duggahitatthi kiñci;
::

::gathalast
Hadayena te dhammaladdhena nāgā, irandhatiṃ nāgakaññaṃ dadanti.
::

::hangnum
1560\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā ahaṃ tuyhaṃ vadhāya yutto, evaṃ mamattho maraṇena tuyhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idheva taṃ narake pātayitvā, hantvāna taṃ hadayamānayissaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1561\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khippaṃ mamaṃ uddhara kātiyāna, hadayena me yadi te atthi kiccaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ye kecime sādhunarassa dhammā, sabbeva te pātukaromi ajja’’.
::

::hangnum
1562\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So {pb:V:2.0216} puṇṇako kurūnaṃ kattuseṭṭhaṃ, nagamuddhani khippaṃ patiṭṭhapetvā;
::

::gathalast
Assatthamāsīnaṃ samekkhiyāna, paripucchi kattāramanomapaññaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1563\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samuddhato mesi tuvaṃ papātā, hadayena te ajja mamatthi kiccaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ye kecime sādhunarassa dhammā, sabbeva me pātukarohi ajja’’.
::

::hangnum
1564\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samuddhato {pb:T:2.0348} tyasmi ahaṃ papātā, hadayena me yadi te atthi kiccaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ye kecime sādhunarassa dhammā, sabbeva te pātukaromi ajja’’.
::

::hangnum
1565\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yātānuyāyī {pb:M:2.0300} ca bhavāhi māṇava, allañca {note:addañca (sī. pī.)} pāṇiṃ parivajjayassu;
::

::gathalast
Mā cassu mittesu kadāci dubbhī, mā ca vasaṃ asatīnaṃ nigacche’’.
::

::hangnum
1566\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ nu yātaṃ anuyāyī hoti, allañca pāṇiṃ dahate kathaṃ so;
::

::gathalast
Asatī ca kā ko pana mittadubbho, akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1567\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asanthutaṃ {note:asandhavaṃ (syā. ka.)} nopi ca diṭṭhapubbaṃ, yo āsanenāpi nimantayeyya;
::

::gathalast
Tasseva atthaṃ puriso kareyya, yātānuyāyīti tamāhu paṇḍitā.
::

::hangnum
1568\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassekarattampi ghare vaseyya, yatthannapānaṃ puriso labheyya;
::

::gathalast
Na tassa pāpaṃ manasāpi cintaye, adubbhī {pb:T:2.0349} pāṇiṃ dahate mittadubbho.
::

::hangnum
1569\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya, nisīdeyya sayeyya vā;
::

::gathalast
Na tassa sākhaṃ bhañjeyya, mittadubbho hi pāpako.
::

::hangnum
1570\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puṇṇampi cemaṃ pathaviṃ dhanena, dajjitthiyā puriso sammatāya;
::

::gathalast
Laddhā khaṇaṃ atimaññeyya tampi, tāsaṃ vasaṃ asatīnaṃ na gacche.
::

::hangnum
1571\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ kho yātaṃ anuyāyī hoti, allañca pāṇiṃ dahate punevaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asatī ca sā so pana mittadubbho, so dhammiko hoti jahassu adhammaṃ’’.
::

::centre
Sādhunaradhammakaṇḍaṃ nāma.
::

#### Kālāgirikaṇḍaṃ

::hangnum
1572\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avasiṃ {pb:M:2.0301} ahaṃ tuyhaṃ tīhaṃ agāre, annena pānena upaṭṭhitosmi;
::

::gathalast
Mitto mamāsī visajjāmahaṃ taṃ, kāmaṃ gharaṃ uttamapañña gaccha.
::

::hangnum
1573\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Api hāyatu nāgakulā {note:nāgakulassa (sī. syā. pī.)} attho, alampi me nāgakaññāya hotu;
::

::gathalast
So tvaṃ sakeneva subhāsitena, muttosi me ajja vadhāya pañña’’.
::

::hangnum
1574\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Handa {pb:T:2.0350}{pb:V:2.0217} tuvaṃ yakkha mamampi nehi, sasuraṃ te {note:sassuraṃ nu te (sī. syā. pī. ka.)} atthaṃ mayi carassu;
::

::gathalast
Mayañca nāgādhipatiṃ vimānaṃ, dakkhemu nāgassa adiṭṭhapubbaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1575\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ ve narassa ahitāya assa, na taṃ pañño arahati dassanāya;
::

::gathalast
Atha kena vaṇṇena amittagāmaṃ, tuvamicchasi uttamapañña gantuṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1576\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā pajānāmi ahampi etaṃ, na taṃ pañño arahati dassanāya;
::

::gathalast
Pāpañca me natthi kataṃ kuhiñci, tasmā na saṅke maraṇāgamāya’’.
::

::hangnum
1577\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Handa ca ṭhānaṃ atulānubhāvaṃ, mayā saha dakkhasi ehi katte;
::

::gathalast
Yatthacchati naccagītehi nāgo, rājā yathā vessavaṇo naḷiññaṃ {note:niḷiññaṃ (syā.), niḷaññaṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
1578\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:M:2.0302} nāgakaññā caritaṃ gaṇena, nikīḷitaṃ niccamaho ca rattiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pahūtamālyaṃ {note:bahuttamallaṃ (ka.)} bahupupphachannaṃ {note:bahupupphasañchannaṃ (ka.)}, obhāsatī {pb:T:2.0351} vijjurivantalikkhe.
::

::hangnum
1579\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Annena pānena upetarūpaṃ, naccehi gītehi ca vāditehi;
::

::gathalast
Paripūraṃ kaññāhi alaṅkatāhi, upasobhati vatthapilandhanena {note:vatthapilandhanehi (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
1580\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So puṇṇako kurūnaṃ kattuseṭṭhaṃ, nisīdayī pacchato āsanasmiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ādāya kattāramanomapaññaṃ, upānayī bhavanaṃ nāgarañño.
::

::hangnum
1581\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Patvāna ṭhānaṃ atulānubhāvaṃ, aṭṭhāsi kattā pacchato puṇṇakassa;
::

::gathalast
Sāmaggi pekkhamāno {note:sāmaggipekkhī pana (sī. syā. pī.)} nāgarājā, pubbeva jāmātaramajjhabhāsatha’’.
::

::hangnum
1582\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yannu tuvaṃ agamā maccalokaṃ, anvesamāno hadayaṃ paṇḍitassa;
::

::gathalast
Kacci samiddhena idhānupatto, ādāya kattāramanomapaññaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1583\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayañhi so āgato yaṃ tvamicchasi, dhammena laddho mama dhammapālo;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ passatha sammukhā {note:taṃ passa dhammaṃ samukhā (ka.)} bhāsamānaṃ, sukho {pb:T:2.0352} have {note:bhave (pī.)} sappurisehi saṅgamo’’.
::

::centre
Kālāgirikaṇḍaṃ nāma.
::

::hangnum
1584\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Byamhito nābhivādesi, nayidaṃ paññavatāmiva’’.

::hangnum
1585\.

::gatha1
‘‘Na camhi byamhito nāga, na ca maccubhayaṭṭito;
::

::gathalast
Na vajjho abhivādeyya, vajjhaṃ vā nābhivādaye.
::

::hangnum
1586\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Yaṃ naro hantumiccheyya, taṃ kammaṃ nupapajjati’’.
::

::hangnum
1587\.

::

::gathalast
Na vajjho abhivādeyya, vajjhaṃ vā nābhivādaye.

::hangnum
1588\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Yaṃ naro hantumiccheyya, taṃ kammaṃ nupapajjati’’.

::hangnum
1589\.

::gatha1
‘‘Asassataṃ sassataṃ nu tavayidaṃ, iddhījutībalavīriyūpapatti {note:iddhiṃ jutiṃ balaṃ vīriyūpapatti (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ nāgarājetamatthaṃ, kathaṃ nu te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1590\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adhiccaladdhaṃ pariṇāmajaṃ te, sayaṃkataṃ udāhu devehi dinnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi me nāgarājetamatthaṃ, yatheva te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1591\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nādhiccaladdhaṃ {pb:T:2.0353} na pariṇāmajaṃ me, na sayaṃkataṃ nāpi devehi dinnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakehi kammehi apāpakehi, puññehi me laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1592\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ te vataṃ kiṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ, kissa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko;
::

::gathalast
Iddhījutībalavīriyūpapatti, idañca te nāga mahāvimānaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1593\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahañca {pb:M:2.0304} bhariyā ca manussaloke, saddhā ubho dānapatī ahumhā;
::

::gathalast
Opānabhūtaṃ me gharaṃ tadāsi, santappitā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca.
::

::hangnum
1594\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mālañca gandhañca vilepanañca, padīpiyaṃ seyyamupassayañca;
::

::gathalast
Acchādanaṃ sāyanamannapānaṃ, sakkacca dānāni adamha tattha.
::

::hangnum
1595\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ me vataṃ taṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ, tassa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko;
::

::gathalast
Iddhījutībalavīriyūpapatti, idañca me dhīra mahāvimānaṃ’.
::

::hangnum
1596\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ {pb:T:2.0354} ce te laddhamidaṃ vimānaṃ, jānāsi puññānaṃ phalūpapattiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā hi dhammaṃ cara appamatto, yathā vimānaṃ puna māvasesi’.

1597\.

::gathalast

::hangnum

::

::gathalast
Ṭhatvā idha yāvatāyukaṃ vimāne, uddhaṃ ito gacchasi devalokaṃ’’.

::hangnum
1600\.

::gatha1

1601\.

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ tuvaṃ nāgi asampadosaṃ, anupālaya vacasā kammunā ca;
::

::gathalast
Ṭhatvā idha yāvatāyukaṃ vimāne, uddhaṃ ito gacchasi devalokaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1624\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā hi so socati rājaseṭṭho, tayā vinā yassa tuvaṃ sajibbo;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhūpanītopi {pb:T:2.0359} tayā samecca, vindeyya poso sukhamāturopi’’.
::

::hangnum
1625\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā {pb:M:2.0308} sataṃ bhāsasi nāgi dhammaṃ, anuttaraṃ atthapadaṃ suciṇṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etādisiyāsu hi āpadāsu, paññāyate mādisānaṃ viseso’’.
::

::hangnum
1626\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkhāhi no tāyaṃ mudhā nu laddho, akkhehi no tāyaṃ ajesi jūte;
::

::gathalast
Dhammena laddho iti tāyamāha, kathaṃ nu tvaṃ hatthamimassa māgato’’.
::

::hangnum
1627\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo missaro tattha ahosi rājā, tamāyamakkhehi ajesi jūte;
::

::gathalast
So maṃ jito rājā imassadāsi, dhammena laddhosmi asāhasena.
::

::hangnum
1628\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yatheva varuṇo nāgo, pañhaṃ pucchittha paṇḍitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tatheva nāgakaññāpi, pañhaṃ pucchittha paṇḍitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1629\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yatheva varuṇaṃ nāgaṃ, dhīro tosesi pucchito;
::

::gathalast
Tatheva nāgakaññampi, dhīro tosesi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
1630\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubhopi te attamane viditvā, mahoragaṃ nāgakaññañca dhīro {note:vidhūro (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Achambhī {pb:T:2.0360} abhīto alomahaṭṭho, iccabravi varuṇaṃ nāgarājānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1631\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā rodhayi {note:mā heṭhayi (pī.)} nāga āyāhamasmi, yena tavattho idaṃ sarīraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hadayena maṃsena karohi kiccaṃ, sayaṃ karissāmi yathāmati te’’.
::

::hangnum
1632\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paññā {pb:V:2.0221} have hadayaṃ paṇḍitānaṃ, te tyamha paññāya mayaṃ sutuṭṭhā;
::

::gathalast
Anūnanāmo labhatajja dāraṃ, ajjeva taṃ kuruyo pāpayātu’’.
::

::hangnum
1633\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa {pb:M:2.0309} puṇṇako attamano udaggo, irandhatiṃ nāgakaññaṃ labhitvā;
::

::gathalast
Haṭṭhena bhāvena patītarūpo, iccabravi kurūnaṃ kattuseṭṭhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1634\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhariyāya maṃ tvaṃ akari samaṅgiṃ, ahañca te vidhura karomi kiccaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idañca te maṇiratanaṃ dadāmi, ajjeva taṃ kuruyo pāpayāmi’’.
::

::hangnum
1635\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajeyyamesā tava hotu metti, bhariyāya {pb:T:2.0361} kaccāna piyāya saddhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ānandi vitto {note:ānandacitto (syā. pī.)} sumano patīto, datvā maṇiṃ mañca nayindapatthaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1636\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa puṇṇako kurūnaṃ kattuseṭṭhaṃ, nisīdayī purato āsanasmiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ādāya kattāramanomapaññaṃ, upānayī nagaraṃ indapatthaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1637\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mano manussassa yathāpi gacche, tatopissa khippataraṃ {note:tatopi saṃkhippataraṃ (sī. pī.)} ahosi;
::

::gathalast
Sa puṇṇako kurūnaṃ kattuseṭṭhaṃ, upānayī nagaraṃ indapatthaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1638\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etindapatthaṃ nagaraṃ padissati, rammāni ca ambavanāni bhāgaso;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca bhariyāya samaṅgibhūto, tuvañca pattosi sakaṃ niketaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1639\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa puṇṇako kurūnaṃ kattuseṭṭhaṃ, oropiya dhammasabhāya majjhe;
::

::gathalast
Ājaññamāruyha anomavaṇṇo, pakkāmi {pb:T:2.0362} vehāyasamantalikkhe.
::

::hangnum
1640\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ {pb:M:2.0310} disvā rājā paramappatīto, uṭṭhāya bāhāhi palissajitvā;
::

::gathalast
Avikampayaṃ dhammasabhāya majjhe, nisīdayī pamukhamāsanasmiṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1641\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tvaṃ no vinetāsi rathaṃva naddhaṃ, nandanti taṃ kuruyo dassanena;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ, kathaṃ pamokkho ahu māṇavassa’’.
::

::hangnum
1642\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ māṇavotyābhivadī janinda, na so manusso naravīraseṭṭha;
::

::gathalast
Yadi te suto puṇṇako nāma yakkho, rañño kuverassa hi so sajibbo.
::

::hangnum
1643\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhūmindharo varuṇo nāma nāgo, brahā sucī vaṇṇabalūpapanno;
::

::gathalast
Tassānujaṃ dhītaraṃ kāmayāno, irandhatī nāma sā nāgakaññā.
::

::hangnum
1644\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassā sumajjhāya piyāya hetu, patārayittha maraṇāya mayhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So ceva bhariyāya samaṅgibhūto, ahañca {pb:T:2.0363} anuññāto maṇi ca laddho’’.
::

::hangnum
1645\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rukkho hi mayhaṃ paddhāre {note:gharadvāre (syā.)} sujāto, paññākkhandho sīlamayassa sākhā;
::

::gathalast
Atthe ca dhamme ca ṭhito nipāko, gavapphalo hatthigavassachanno.
::

::hangnum
1646\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Naccagītatūriyābhinādite, ucchijja senaṃ {note:menaṃ (sī. pī.)} puriso ahāsi;
::

::gathalast
So no ayaṃ āgato sanniketaṃ, rukkhassimassāpacitiṃ karotha.
::

::hangnum
1647\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:V:2.0222}{pb:M:2.0311} keci vittā mama paccayena, sabbeva te pātukarontu ajja;
::

::gathalast
Tibbāni katvāna upāyanāni, rukkhassimassāpacitiṃ karotha.
::

::hangnum
1648\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye keci baddhā mama atthi raṭṭhe, sabbeva te bandhanā mocayantu;
::

::gathalast
Yatheva yaṃ bandhanasmā pamutto, evamete muñcare bandhanasmā.
::

::hangnum
1649\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Unnaṅgalā māsamimaṃ karontu, maṃsodanaṃ brāhmaṇā bhakkhayantu;
::

::gathalast
Amajjapā majjarahā pivantu, puṇṇāhi {pb:T:2.0364} thālāhi palissutāhi.
::

::hangnum
1650\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāpathaṃ nicca samavhayantu, tibbañca rakkhaṃ vidahantu raṭṭhe;
::

::gathalast
Yathāññamaññaṃ na viheṭhayeyyuṃ, rukkhassimassāpacitiṃ karotha’’.
::

::hangnum
1651\.
::

::gatha1
Orodhā ca kumārā ca, vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Bahuṃ annañca pānañca, paṇḍitassābhihārayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
1652\.
::

::gatha1
Hatthārohā anīkaṭṭhā, rathikā pattikārakā;
::

::gathalast
Bahuṃ annañca pānañca, paṇḍitassābhihārayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
1653\.
::

::gatha1
Samāgatā jānapadā, negamā ca samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Bahuṃ annañca pānañca, paṇḍitassābhihārayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
1654\.
::

::gatha1
Bahujano pasannosi, disvā paṇḍitamāgate;
::

::gathalast
Paṇḍitamhi anuppatte, celukkhepo pavattathāti.
::

::centre
Vidhurajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 547. Vessantarajātakaṃ (10)

#### Dasavarakathā

::hangnum
1655\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Phussatī {pb:T:2.0365}{pb:V:2.0223}{pb:M:2.0312} {note:phusati (sī. pī.)} varavaṇṇābhe, varassu dasadhā vare;
::

::gathalast
Pathabyā cārupubbaṅgi, yaṃ tuyhaṃ manaso piyaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1656\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Devarāja namo tyatthu, kiṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Rammā cāvesi maṃ ṭhānā, vātova dharaṇīruhaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1657\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na ceva te kataṃ pāpaṃ, na ca me tvamasi appiyā;
::

::gathalast
Puññañca te parikkhīṇaṃ, yena tevaṃ vadāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1658\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Santike maraṇaṃ tuyhaṃ, vinābhāvo bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Paṭigaṇhāhi me ete, vare dasa pavecchato’’.
::

::hangnum
1659\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Varaṃ ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gathalast
Sivirājassa bhaddante, tattha assaṃ nivesane.
::

::hangnum
1660\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nīlanettā nīlabhamu, nilakkhī ca yathā migī;
::

::gathalast
Phussatī nāma nāmena, tatthapassaṃ purindada.
::

::hangnum
1661\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puttaṃ labhetha varadaṃ, yācayogaṃ {note:yācayogiṃ (ka.)} amacchariṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pūjitaṃ paṭirājūhi, kittimantaṃ yasassinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1662\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gabbhaṃ me dhārayantiyā, majjhimaṅgaṃ anunnataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kucchi anunnato assa, cāpaṃva likhitaṃ samaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1663\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Thanā me nappapateyyuṃ, palitā na santu vāsava;
::

::gathalast
Kāye rajo na limpetha, vajjhañcāpi pamocaye.
::

::hangnum
1664\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mayūrakoñcābhirude, nārivaragaṇāyute;
::

::gathalast
Khujjacelāpakākiṇṇe{pb:T:2.0366}, sūdamāgadhavaṇṇite.
::

::hangnum
1665\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Citraggaḷerughusite, surāmaṃsapabodhane;
::

::gathalast
Sivirājassa bhaddante, tatthassaṃ mahesī piyā’’.
::

::hangnum
1666\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye te dasa varā dinnā, mayā sabbaṅgasobhane;
::

::gathalast
Sivirājassa vijite, sabbe te lacchasī vare.
::

::hangnum
1667\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:M:2.0313} vatvāna maghavā, devarājā sujampati;
::

::gathalast
Phussatiyā varaṃ datvā, anumodittha vāsavo.
::

::centre
Dasavarakathā nāma.
::

#### Hemavantaṃ

::hangnum
1668\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Parūḷhakacchanakhalomā{pb:T:2.0367}{pb:V:2.0224}, paṅkadantā rajassirā;
::

::gathalast
Paggayha dakkhiṇaṃ bāhuṃ, kiṃ maṃ yācanti brāhmaṇā’’.
::

::hangnum
1669\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ratanaṃ deva yācāma, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dadāhi pavaraṃ nāgaṃ, īsādantaṃ urūḷhavaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1670\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dadāmi na vikampāmi, yaṃ maṃ yācanti brāhmaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Pabhinnaṃ kuñjaraṃ dantiṃ, opavayhaṃ gajuttamaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1671\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthikkhandhato oruyha, rājā cāgādhimānaso;
::

::gathalast
Brāhmaṇānaṃ adā dānaṃ, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano’’.
::

::hangnum
1672\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāsi yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ, tadāsi lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hatthināge padinnamhi, medanī sampakampatha.
::

::hangnum
1673\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāsi yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ, tadāsi lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hatthināge padinnamhi, khubbhittha nagaraṃ tadā.
::

::hangnum
1674\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samākulaṃ puraṃ āsi, ghoso ca vipulo mahā;
::

::gathalast
Hatthināge {pb:T:2.0368} padinnamhi, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane’’.
::

::hangnum
1675\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uggā ca rājaputtā ca, vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Hatthārohā anīkaṭṭhā, rathikā pattikārakā.
::

::hangnum
1676\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kevalo cāpi nigamo, sivayo ca samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Disvā nāgaṃ nīyamānaṃ, te rañño paṭivedayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
1677\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vidhamaṃ deva te raṭṭhaṃ, putto vessantaro tava;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ no hatthinaṃ dajjā, nāgaṃ raṭṭhassa pūjitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1678\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ no kuñjaraṃ dajjā, īsādantaṃ urūḷhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khettaññuṃ sabbayuddhānaṃ, sabbasetaṃ gajuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1679\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṇḍukambalasañchannaṃ, {pb:M:2.0314} pabhinnaṃ sattumaddanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dantiṃ savāḷabījaniṃ, setaṃ kelāsasādisaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1680\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sasetacchattaṃ {pb:V:2.0225} saupādheyyaṃ, sāthabbanaṃ sahatthipaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aggayānaṃ rājavāhiṃ, brāhmaṇānaṃ adā gajaṃ {note:dhanaṃ (sī. pī.), dānaṃ (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
1681\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Annaṃ pānañca yo {note:so (sī. syā. ka.)} dajjā, vatthasenāsanāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ kho dānaṃ patirūpaṃ, etaṃ kho brāhmaṇārahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1682\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayaṃ te vaṃsarājā no, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano {note:raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ (sī.), raṭṭhavaḍḍhana (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ vessantaro putto, gajaṃ bhājeti sañjaya.
::

::hangnum
1683\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace tvaṃ na karissasi, sivīnaṃ vacanaṃ idaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maññe taṃ saha puttena, sivī hatthe karissare’’.
::

::hangnum
1684\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāmaṃ {pb:T:2.0369} janapado māsi, raṭṭhañcāpi vinassatu;
::

::gatha2
Nāhaṃ sivīnaṃ vacanā, rājaputtaṃ adūsakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pabbājeyyaṃ sakā raṭṭhā, putto hi mama oraso.
::

::hangnum
1685\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāmaṃ janapado māsi, raṭṭhañcāpi vinassatu;
::

::gatha2
Nāhaṃ sivīnaṃ vacanā, rājaputtaṃ adūsakaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
1686\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na cāhaṃ tasmiṃ dubbheyyaṃ, ariyasīlavato hi so;
::

::gatha2
Asilokopi me assa, pāpañca pasave bahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ vessantaraṃ puttaṃ, satthena ghātayāmase’’.
::

::hangnum
1687\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā naṃ daṇḍena satthena, na hi so bandhanāraho;
::

::gathalast
Pabbājehi ca naṃ raṭṭhā, vaṅke vasatu pabbate’’.
::

::hangnum
1688\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Eso ce sivīnaṃ chando, chandaṃ na panudāmase;
::

::gathalast
Imaṃ so vasatu rattiṃ, kāme ca paribhuñjatu.
::

::hangnum
1689\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato ratyā vivasāne, sūriyassuggamanaṃ pati {note:sūriyuggamane sati (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Samaggā sivayo hutvā, raṭṭhā pabbājayantu naṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1690\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uṭṭhehi {pb:M:2.0315} katte taramāno, gantvā vessantaraṃ vada;
::

::gathalast
Sivayo deva te kuddhā, negamā ca samāgatā.
::

::hangnum
1691\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uggā ca rājaputtā ca, vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā;

Kevalo {pb:T:2.0370} cāpi nigamo, sivayo ca samāgatā.

::hangnum
1692\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asmā ratyā vivasāne, sūriyassuggamanaṃ pati;
::

::gathalast
Samaggā sivayo hutvā, raṭṭhā pabbājayanti taṃ.
::

::hangnum
1693\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sa {pb:V:2.0226} kattā taramānova, sivirājena pesito;
::

::gathalast
Āmuttahatthābharaṇā, suvattho candanabhūsito.
::

::hangnum
1694\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīsaṃ nhāto udake so, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalo;
::

::gathalast
Upāgami puraṃ rammaṃ, vessantaranivesanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1695\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthaddasa kumāraṃ so, ramamānaṃ sake pure;
::

::gathalast
Parikiṇṇaṃ amaccehi, tidasānaṃva vāsavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1696\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So tattha gantvā taramāno, kattā vessantaraṃbravi;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhaṃ te vedayissāmi, mā me kujjhi rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
1697\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vanditvā rodamāno so, kattā rājānamabravi;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
1698\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
1699\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
1700\.

::gatha1
‘‘Asmā ratyā vivasāne, sūriyassuggamanaṃ pati;
::

::gathalast
Samaggā sivayo hutvā, raṭṭhā pabbājayanti taṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1701\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kismiṃ {pb:T:2.0371} me sivayo kuddhā, nāhaṃ passāmi dukkaṭaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ me katte viyācikkha, kasmā pabbājayanti maṃ’’.

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gatha1
‘‘Tvaṃ maddi kaṇhaṃ gaṇhāhi, lahu esā kaniṭṭhikā;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ jāliṃ gahessāmi, garuko bhātiko hi so’’.
::

::hangnum
1868\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājā kumāramādāya, rājaputtī ca dārikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sammodamānā pakkāmuṃ, aññamaññaṃ piyaṃvadā’’.
::

::centre
Dānakaṇḍaṃ nāma.
::

#### Vanapavesanaṃ

::hangnum
1869\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadi {pb:M:2.0330} keci manujā enti, anumagge paṭipathe;
::

::gathalast
Maggaṃ te paṭipucchāma, kuhiṃ vaṅkatapabbato.
::

::hangnum
1870\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te tattha amhe passitvā, kalunaṃ paridevayuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhaṃ {pb:T:2.0390} te paṭivedenti, dūre vaṅkatapabbato’’.
::

::hangnum
1871\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadi passanti pavane, dārakā phaline {note:phalite (sī. syā. pī.)} dume;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ phalānaṃ hetumhi, uparodanti dārakā.
::

::hangnum
1872\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rodante dārake disvā, ubbiddhā {note:ubbiggā (sī. syā. pī.)} vipulā dumā;
::

::gathalast
Sayamevonamitvāna, upagacchanti dārake.
::

::hangnum
1873\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ accherakaṃ disvā, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sādhukāraṃ pavattesi, maddī sabbaṅgasobhanā.
::

::hangnum
1874\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accheraṃ vata lokasmiṃ, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vessantarassa tejena, sayamevonatā dumā’’.
::

::hangnum
1875\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅkhipiṃsu pathaṃ yakkhā, anukampāya dārake;
::

::gathalast
Nikkhantadivaseneva, cetaraṭṭhaṃ upāgamuṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1876\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te gantvā dīghamaddhānaṃ, cetaraṭṭhaṃ upāgamuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Iddhaṃ phītaṃ janapadaṃ, bahumaṃsasurodanaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1877\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cetiyo parivāriṃsu, disvā lakkhaṇamāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sukhumālī vata ayyā, pattikā paridhāvati.
::

::hangnum
1878\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vayhāhi {pb:V:2.0240} pariyāyitvā, sivikāya rathena ca;
::

::gathalast
Sājja maddī araññasmiṃ, pattikā paridhāvati’’.
::

::hangnum
1879\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ disvā cetapāmokkhā, rodamānā upāgamuṃ;
::

::gatha2
Kacci nu deva kusalaṃ, kacci deva anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kacci {pb:T:2.0391} pitā arogo te, sivīnañca anāmayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1880\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko te balaṃ mahārāja, ko nu te rathamaṇḍalaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Anassako arathako, dīghamaddhānamāgato;
::

::gathalast
Kaccāmittehi pakato, anuppattosimaṃ disaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
1881\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusalañceva {pb:M:2.0331} me samma, atho samma anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atho pitā arogo me, sivīnañca anāmayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1882\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahañhi kuñjaraṃ dajjaṃ, īsādantaṃ urūḷhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khettaññuṃ sabbayuddhānaṃ, sabbasetaṃ gajuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1883\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṇḍukambalasañchannaṃ, pabhinnaṃ sattumaddanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dantiṃ savāḷabījaniṃ, setaṃ kelāsasādisaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1884\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sasetacchattaṃ saupādheyyaṃ, sāthappanaṃ sahatthipaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
1885\.

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmiṃ me sivayo kuddhā, pitā cupahatomano;

::gatha2

::

::gathalast
Okāsaṃ sammā jānātha, vane yattha vasāmase’’.

::hangnum
1886\.

::

::gathalast

1887\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
1890\.

::gatha1
‘‘Accuggatā hi sivayo, balaggā negamā ca ye;
::

::gathalast
Te vidhaṃsetumicchanti, rājānaṃ mama kāraṇā’’.
::

::hangnum
1893\.

::gatha1

::gathalast
Idheva rajjaṃ kārehi, cetehi parivārito.

::gathalast

::hangnum
1895\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum

#### Jūjakapabbaṃ

::hangnum
1914\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahu vāsī kaliṅgesu, jūjako nāma brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Tassāsi daharā bhariyā, nāmenāmittatāpanā.
::

::hangnum
1915\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tā naṃ tattha gatāvocuṃ, nadiṃ udakahāriyā;
::

::gathalast
Thiyo {pb:T:2.0395} naṃ paribhāsiṃsu, samāgantvā kutūhalā.
::

::hangnum
1916\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amittā {pb:V:2.0243} nūna te mātā, amitto nūna te pitā;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1917\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahitaṃ {pb:M:2.0334} vata te ñātī, mantayiṃsu rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1918\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amittā vata te ñātī, mantayiṃsu rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1919\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dukkaṭaṃ vata te ñātī, mantayiṃsu rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1920\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāpakaṃ vata te ñātī, mantayiṃsu rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1921\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amanāpaṃ vata te ñātī, mantayiṃsu rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1922\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amanāpavāsaṃ vasi, jiṇṇena patinā saha {note:evaṃ dahariyā satī (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yā tvaṃ vasasi jiṇṇassa, mataṃ te jīvitā varaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1923\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi nūna tuyhaṃ kalyāṇi, pitā mātā ca sobhane;
::

::gatha2
Aññaṃ bhattāraṃ vindiṃsu, ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1924\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duyiṭṭhaṃ te navamiyaṃ, akataṃ aggihuttakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1925\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samaṇe brāhmaṇe nūna, brāhmaṇacariyaparāyaṇe;
::

::gatha2
Sā {pb:T:2.0396} tvaṃ loke abhisapi, sīlavante bahussute;
::

::gathalast
Yā tvaṃ vasasi jiṇṇassa, evaṃ dahariyā satī.
::

::hangnum
1926\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na dukkhaṃ ahinā daṭṭhaṃ, na dukkhaṃ sattiyā hataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tañca dukkhañca tibbañca, yaṃ passe jiṇṇakaṃ patiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1927\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Natthi khiḍḍā natthi rati, jiṇṇena patinā saha;
::

::gathalast
Natthi allāpasallāpo, jagghitumpi {note:jagghitampi (sī. pī.)} na sobhati.
::

::hangnum
1928\.

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā ca daharo daharā, mantayanti {note:mantayiṃsu (syā. ka.)} rahogatā;

::gathalast
Sabbesaṃ sokā nassanti, ye keci hadayassitā.

::hangnum
1929\.

::gatha1
‘‘Daharā {pb:M:2.0335} tvaṃ rūpavatī, purisānaṃbhipatthitā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
1930\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:2.0244} te brāhmaṇa gacchāmi, nadiṃ udakahāriyā;
::

::gathalast
Thiyo maṃ paribhāsanti, tayā jiṇṇena brāhmaṇa’’.
::

::hangnum
1931\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā me tvaṃ akarā kammaṃ, mā me udakamāhari;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ udakamāhissaṃ, mā bhoti kupitā ahu’’.
::

::hangnum
1932\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ tamhi kule jātā, yaṃ tvaṃ udakamāhare;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ brāhmaṇa jānāhi, na te vacchāmahaṃ ghare.

::hangnum
1933\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace me dāsaṃ dāsiṃ vā, nānayissasi brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
1934\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ bhotiṃ upaṭṭhissaṃ, mā bhoti kupitā ahu’’.
::

::hangnum
1935\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
1936\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ tvaṃ gantvāna yācassu, dāsaṃ dāsiñca brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
So te dassati yācito, dāsaṃ dāsiñca khattiyo’’.
::

::hangnum
1937\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jiṇṇohamasmi dubbalo {note:abalo (sī. pī. ka.)}, dīgho caddhā suduggamo;
::

::gatha2
Mā bhoti paṭidevesi, mā ca tvaṃ {note:mā bhoti (syā. ka.)} vimanā ahu;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ bhotiṃ upaṭṭhissaṃ, mā bhoti kupitā ahu’’.
::

::hangnum
1938\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā agantvā saṅgāmaṃ, ayuddhova parājito;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
1939\.
::

::gatha1

::gatha2

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
1940\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
1941\.

::gatha1
‘‘Adassanena {pb:M:2.0336} mayhaṃ te, jiṇṇassa paridevato;
::

::gathalast
Bhiyyo vaṅkā ca palitā, bahū hessanti brāhmaṇa’’.

::hangnum
1942\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Aṭṭito kāmarāgena, brāhmaṇiṃ etadabravi’’.

::hangnum
1943\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pātheyyaṃ {pb:T:2.0398}{pb:V:2.0245} me karohi tvaṃ, saṃkulyā saguḷāni ca {note:saṅkulā saṅguḷāni ca (syā.), aṅguḷā sakalāni ca (ka.)};

1944\.

1945\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
1946\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
1947\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So tattha gantvā avaca {note:avacāsi (syā. ka.)}, ye tatthāsuṃ samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Kuhiṃ vessantaro rājā, kattha passemu khattiyaṃ’’.

#### Dārakapabbaṃ

::hangnum
2087\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uṭṭhehi {pb:V:2.0256} jāli patiṭṭha, porāṇaṃ viya dissati;
::

::gathalast
Brāhmaṇaṃ viya passāmi, nandiyo mābhikīrare’’.
::

::hangnum
2088\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahampi tāta passāmi, yo so brahmāva dissati;
::

::gathalast
Addhiko viya {note:atthiko viya (sī. pī.)} āyāti, atithī no bhavissati’’.
::

::hangnum
2089\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci nu bhoto kusalaṃ, kacci bhoto anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kacci uñchena yāpetha, kacci mūlaphalā bahū.
::

::hangnum
2090\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci ḍaṃsā makasā ca, appameva sarīsapā;
::

::gathalast
Vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe, kacci hiṃsā na vijjati’’.
::

::hangnum
2091\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusalañceva no brahme, atho brahme anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atho uñchena yāpema, atho mūlaphalā bahū.
::

::hangnum
2092\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atho {pb:M:2.0349} ḍaṃsā makasā ca, appameva sarīsapā;
::

::gathalast
Vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe, hiṃsā amhaṃ {note:mayhaṃ (syā. ka.)} na vijjati’’.
::

::hangnum
2093\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satta no māse vasataṃ, araññe jīvasokinaṃ {note:jīvisokinaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gatha2
Idampi paṭhamaṃ passāma, brāhmaṇaṃ devavaṇṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ādāya veḷuvaṃ daṇḍaṃ, aggihuttaṃ kamaṇḍaluṃ.
::

::hangnum
2094\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ te mahābrahme, atho te adurāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anto pavisa bhaddante, pāde pakkhālayassu te.

2095\.

2096\.

2097\.

::hangnum
2109\.

::gatha1
‘‘Acchedanassa bhāyāmi, rājaputta suṇohi me;

::gatha2
